# QSP Disease Model Library

> **мһҗлҸҷ м—…лҚ°мқҙнҠё мӨ‘ вҖ” Automatically maintained by [Claude Code Routine (CCR)](https://code.claude.com)**  
> л§Ө м„ём…ҳл§ҲлӢӨ мғҲ м§Ҳнҷҳ лӘЁлҚёмқҙ мһҗлҸҷмңјлЎң м¶”к°Җлҗ©лӢҲлӢӨ В· A new disease model is added automatically each session.

---

## к°ңмҡ” (Overview)

### н•ңкөӯм–ҙ

мқҙ м ҖмһҘмҶҢлҠ” **м •лҹүм Ғ мӢңмҠӨн…ң м•ҪлҰ¬н•ҷ(Quantitative Systems Pharmacology, QSP)** лӘЁлҚёмқ„ м§Ҳнҷҳлі„лЎң мІҙкі„м ҒмңјлЎң кө¬м¶•В·м¶•м Ғн•ҳлҠ” мӮҙм•„мһҲлҠ” лқјмқҙлёҢлҹ¬лҰ¬мһ…лӢҲлӢӨ.

лӘЁл“  мҪҳн…җмё лҠ” **Anthropicмқҳ Claude Code Routine (CCR)** мқ„ нҶөн•ҙ мҷ„м „ мһҗлҸҷмңјлЎң мғқм„ұлҗ©лӢҲлӢӨ. CCRмқҖ мӣҗкІ© нҒҙлқјмҡ°л“ң м»Ён…Ңмқҙл„Ҳм—җм„ң Claudeк°Җ м§Ғм ‘ мҪ”л“ңлҘј мһ‘м„ұн•ҳкі , нҢҢмқјмқ„ л ҢлҚ”л§Ғн•ҳкі , м»Өл°ӢВ·н‘ёмӢңк№Ңм§Җ мҷ„лЈҢн•ҳлҠ” мһҗмңЁ мӢӨн–ү нҷҳкІҪмһ…лӢҲлӢӨ. л§Ө м„ём…ҳмқҙ мў…лЈҢлҗ  л•Ң л°ҳл“ңмӢң ліҖкІҪ мӮ¬н•ӯмқҙ м»Өл°ӢВ·н‘ёмӢңлҗҳм–ҙ мһҲм–ҙм•ј н•ҳлҠ” **Stop Hook**(`stop-hook-git-check.sh`)мқҙ м„Өм •лҗҳм–ҙ мһҲм–ҙ, **мӮ¬лһҢмқҳ к°ңмһ… м—ҶмқҙлҸ„ м ҖмһҘмҶҢк°Җ м§ҖмҶҚм ҒмңјлЎң к°ұмӢ **лҗ©лӢҲлӢӨ.

#### к°Ғ лӘЁлҚём—җ нҸ¬н•ЁлҗҳлҠ” лӮҙмҡ©

| мӮ°м¶ңл¬ј | лӮҙмҡ© |
|--------|------|
| **кё°кі„лЎ м Ғ м§ҖлҸ„** (`.dot` / `.svg` / `.png`) | 100к°ң мқҙмғҒ л…ёл“ң, Graphviz DOT нҳ•мӢқ; м§Ҳнҷҳ нҠ№мқҙ мғқл¬јн•ҷм Ғ кІҪлЎң, м•Ҫл¬ј PK/PD, л°”мқҙмҳӨл§Ҳм»Ө, мһ„мғҒ м—”л“ңнҸ¬мқёнҠёлҘј н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ мӢңк°Ғнҷ”лЎң нҶөн•© |
| **mrgsolve ODE лӘЁлҚё** (`.R`) | лҜёл¶„л°©м •мӢқ кё°л°ҳ PK/PD лӘЁлҚё; мЈјмҡ” мһ„мғҒмӢңн—ҳ нҢҢлқјлҜён„°лЎң ліҙм •; ліөмҲҳмқҳ м№ҳлЈҢ мӢңлӮҳлҰ¬мҳӨ мӢңл®¬л Ҳмқҙм…ҳ; мҡ©лҹү-л°ҳмқ‘ л¶„м„қ нҸ¬н•Ё |
| **Shiny лҢҖмӢңліҙл“ң** (`.R`) | мқён„°лһҷнӢ°лёҢ мӣ№ м•ұ; нҷҳмһҗ нҢҢлқјлҜён„° м„Өм •, м•Ҫл¬ј м„ нғқ, PK/PD мӢӨмӢңк°„ мӢңк°Ғнҷ”, мӢңлӮҳлҰ¬мҳӨ л№„көҗн‘ң, мһ„мғҒ мң„н—ҳ м§Җн‘ң |
| **м°ёкі л¬ён—Ң** (`.md`) | PubMed л§ҒнҒ¬ нҸ¬н•Ё 30к°ң мқҙмғҒмқҳ м„ лі„ л…јл¬ё; лі‘нғңмғқлҰ¬, мһ„мғҒмӢңн—ҳ, л°”мқҙмҳӨл§Ҳм»Ө м„№м…ҳлі„ л¶„лҘҳ |

#### м§Ҳнҷҳ м„ нғқ кё°мӨҖ

м„ нғқ лӘ©лЎқмқҖ мһҗк°Җл©ҙм—ӯм§Ҳнҷҳ 49мў… + л§Ңм„ұм§Ҳнҷҳ 44мў…(мҙқ 93мў…)мңјлЎң кө¬м„ұлҗ©лӢҲлӢӨ. м„ём…ҳл§ҲлӢӨ **мқҙлҜё мҷ„м„ұлҗң м§Ҳнҷҳкіј мӨ‘ліөлҗҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ** лӮ м§ң кё°л°ҳмңјлЎң лӢӨлҘё м§Ҳнҷҳмқ„ м„ нғқн•©лӢҲлӢӨ. м„ нғқ мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„:
- мөңк·ј FDA/EMA мҠ№мқё лҳҗлҠ” мһ„мғҒ 3мғҒмқҙ мһҲлҠ” м§Ҳнҷҳ
- PK/PD нҢҢлқјлҜён„°к°Җ л¬ён—Ңм—җ м¶©л¶„нһҲ кіөк°ңлҗң м§Ҳнҷҳ
- мқҙм „ лӘЁлҚёл“Өкіј лі‘нғңмғқлҰ¬ м№ҙн…Ңкі лҰ¬к°Җ лӢӨлҘё м§Ҳнҷҳ

#### кё°мҲ  мҠӨнғқ

```
Graphviz (dot)        вҶ’  кё°кі„лЎ м Ғ м§ҖлҸ„ л ҢлҚ”л§Ғ (.dot вҶ’ .svg + .png)
mrgsolve (R)          вҶ’  ODE кё°л°ҳ PK/PD мӢңл®¬л Ҳмқҙм…ҳ
Shiny (R)             вҶ’  мқён„°лһҷнӢ°лёҢ лҢҖмӢңліҙл“ң
Claude Code Routine   вҶ’  лӘЁл“  нҢҢмқј мһҗлҸҷ мғқм„ұ л°Ҹ м»Өл°Ӣ
CCR Stop Hook         вҶ’  м„ём…ҳ мў…лЈҢ мӢң м»Өл°Ӣ/н‘ёмӢң к°•м ң мӢӨн–ү
```

---

### English

This repository is a **living QSP (Quantitative Systems Pharmacology) model library** that grows automatically with each session. Every model follows the same four-deliverable structure: mechanistic map В· mrgsolve ODE model В· Shiny app В· curated references.

#### How the Automation Works

All content is generated by **Anthropic's Claude Code Routine (CCR)** вҖ” an autonomous cloud execution environment where Claude writes code, renders files, and pushes commits without human intervention. A mandatory **Stop Hook** (`stop-hook-git-check.sh`) is configured: the session cannot close unless every change is committed and pushed to the remote branch. This guarantees that the repository always reflects the full output of each session.

The workflow per session:

```
1. Pull latest main
2. Select a new disease from the curated list (93 diseases total)
   вҶ’ Avoid duplicates, rotate categories, prioritize recent clinical data
3. Build the mechanistic map (.dot вҶ’ .svg + .png via Graphviz)
4. Write mrgsolve R model (ODE compartments, PK/PD parameters, scenarios)
5. Scaffold the Shiny app (вүҘ6 interactive tabs)
6. Compile references (вүҘ30 PubMed-linked papers)
7. Update README.md (table row + detailed section) and create CLAUDE.md
8. git add -A вҶ’ commit вҶ’ push to main (enforced by Stop Hook)
```

#### Per-Model Content Standards

| Deliverable | Standards |
|-------------|-----------|
| **Mechanistic map** | вүҘ100 nodes; вүҘ8 subgraph clusters; drug mechanisms, clinical endpoints, and biomarkers all visualized |
| **mrgsolve model** | вүҘ15 ODE states; вүҘ5 treatment scenarios; calibrated to published clinical trial PK/PD; doseвҖ“response analysis |
| **Shiny dashboard** | вүҘ6 tabs; interactive patient profile, drug PK, PD biomarkers, scenario comparison table, risk classification |
| **References** | вүҘ30 curated papers with PubMed links; categorized by mechanism / biomarker / clinical trial sections |

#### Disease Coverage

Models span two major categories drawn from a curated list of **93 diseases**:

- **мһҗк°Җл©ҙм—ӯм§Ҳнҷҳ (Autoimmune, 49 diseases)** вҖ” RA, SLE, SjГ¶gren's, MCTD, vasculitides (GPA/EGPA/MPA/PAN/Takayasu/GCA), IBD, PSC/PBC, AIH, MS, MG, NMO, GBS, CIDP, autoimmune encephalitis, ITP, AIHA, pemphigus, IgAN, and more
- **л§Ңм„ұм§Ҳнҷҳ (Chronic/Metabolic, 44 diseases)** вҖ” T2DM, PCOS, HFrEF/HFpEF, COPD, IPF, PAH, OSA, CKD/ADPKD/FSGS/MCD, NAFLD, cirrhosis, chronic hepatitis B, BPH, and more

See [`CLAUDE.md`](CLAUDE.md) for the complete disease list and model-building guidelines used by each CCR session.

## QSP Disease Models

к°Ғ лӘЁлҚёмқҖ мҶҢл¬ёмһҗ н•ҳмқҙн”Ҳ л””л үнҶ лҰ¬м—җ м ҖмһҘлҗ©лӢҲлӢӨ В· Each model lives in its own lowercase-dash subdirectory containing:
- `*.dot` вҖ” Mechanistic map source (Graphviz DOT, вүҘ100 nodes)
- `*.svg` / `*.png` вҖ” Rendered mechanistic map (vector + raster)
- `*_references.md` вҖ” Curated PubMed literature (вүҘ30 papers)
- `*_mrgsolve_model.R` / `*_model.R` вҖ” mrgsolve ODE model + simulation scenarios
- `*_shiny_app.R` / `shiny_app/app.R` вҖ” Interactive Shiny PK/PD dashboard

ліҙм •: Gipson 2011(Kidney Int, Pred 25% мҷ„м „кҙҖн•ҙ)В·Cattran 1999(CsA 70% л¶Җл¶„кҙҖн•ҙ)В·Kronbichler 2014(RTX 57% л°ҳмқ‘)В·Rheault 2023(DUPLEX NEJM, Sparsentan мҷ„м „кҙҖн•ҙ 18% vs 9%)В·PLANET-I(Sparsentan UPCR -46%) | [![FSGS](fsgs/fsgs_qsp_model.png)](fsgs/fsgs_qsp_model.svg) | [R](fsgs/fsgs_mrgsolve_model.R) | [refs](fsgs/fsgs_references.md) | [Shiny](fsgs/fsgs_shiny_app.R) |

### Rheumatoid Arthritis

> Directory: [`rheumatoid-arthritis/`](rheumatoid-arthritis/)

**Mechanistic Map** (130+ nodes, 13 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Immune Cell Activation | DC, Macrophage M0/M1, Th1/Th17/Treg, Tfh, B cells, Plasma cells, NK, Neutrophils, Mast cells, NETosis |
| Autoantibody Formation | PAD4, citrullination, ACPA/RF, immune complexes, complement (C1q/C3/C5a), FcОіRIII |
| Cytokine Network | TNF-Оұ, IL-1ОІ, IL-6, IL-8, IL-10, IL-12, IL-17A/F, IL-21, IL-23, IFN-Оі, GM-CSF, TGF-ОІ, VEGF, OSM, CXCL13, CCL2/5 |
| Intracellular Signaling | JAK1/2/3/TYK2, STAT1/3/4/5/6, NF-ОәB/IKK, p38 MAPK, ERK, JNK, PI3K/Akt/mTOR, AP-1, HIF-1Оұ, NFATc1, Wnt/ОІ-catenin |
| Synovial Pathology | FLS (quiescent/activated), synovial macrophage, pannus, COX-2/PGE2/LTB4, MMPs 1/2/3/9/13, ADAMTS-4/5, TIMPs |
| Synovial Vasculature | Endothelium, ICAM-1/VCAM-1, E-selectin, VEGF-driven neo-angiogenesis, HIF-1Оұ, eNOS |
| Bone & Cartilage | RANKL/RANK/OPG, osteoclast/osteoblast, bone erosion, cartilage ECM (type II collagen, aggrecan), Wnt/DKK-1/sclerostin, chondrocyte apoptosis |
| Pain Signaling | Nociceptor (C/AОҙ), NGF/TrkA, TRPV1, Nav1.7/1.8, Substance P/CGRP, bradykinin, peripheral & central sensitization |
| Drug PK | Oral/SC/IV compartments, FcRn recycling, TMDD, ADA, protein binding |
| Drug Mechanisms | MTX (DHFR/adenosine), LEF (DHODH), HCQ (lysosomal), SSZ (NF-ОәB); 5Г—TNFi; 4Г—IL-6Ri; Abatacept; Rituximab; Denosumab; 4Г—JAKi |
| Biomarkers | CRP, ESR, IL-6, TNF-Оұ, MMP-3, RF, Anti-CCP, fibrinogen, SAA, hepcidin, Hb, RANKL/OPG serum |
| Clinical Endpoints | DAS28-CRP/ESR, ACR20/50/70, CDAI, SDAI, HAQ-DI, Sharp/vdH score, RAMRIS, EULAR remission, MBDA |
| Systemic Complications | CV risk, atherosclerosis, BMD loss, RA-ILD, lymphoma, infections, VTE (JAKi), anemia, depression |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![RA QSP Map](rheumatoid-arthritis/ra_qsp.png)](rheumatoid-arthritis/ra_qsp.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| TCZ PK | DEPOT_TCZ, C1_TCZ, C2_TCZ | 2-compartment SC/IV with first-order absorption |
| TMDD | R_FREE, RC | Free sIL-6RОұ and TCZ-receptor complex |
| MTX PK | GI_MTX, C1_MTX | 1-compartment oral; active metabolite proxy |
| PD | TNFa, IL6, CRP, RANKL_pd | Cytokine and biomarker ODE dynamics |
| Scores | SJC28_ode, TJC28_ode | Inflammation-driven joint count adaptation |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dCRP/dt = ksyn_CRP Г— IL6_eff/(EC50+IL6_eff) вҲ’ kout_CRP Г— CRP` (IL-6R blockade suppresses IL6_eff via TMDD)
- `DAS28-CRP = 0.56вҲҡTJC + 0.28вҲҡSJC + 0.36В·ln(CRP+1) + 0.014В·PtGA + 0.96`

### Pulmonary Arterial Hypertension (PAH)

> Directory: [`pulmonary-arterial-hypertension/`](pulmonary-arterial-hypertension/)

> нҸҗлҸҷл§Ҙ лӮҙн”јм„ёнҸ¬ кё°лҠҘ л¶Җм „ л°Ҹ нҳҲкҙҖ нҸүнҷңк·ј л№„лҢҖлЎң нҸҗнҳҲкҙҖ м Җн•ӯмқҙ мғҒмҠ№н•ҳм—¬ мҡ°мӢ¬мӢӨ л¶Җм „мқ„ мң л°ңн•ҳлҠ” нқ¬к·Җ м§„н–үм„ұ м§Ҳнҷҳ.

**Mechanistic Map** (130+ nodes, 10 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| ET-1 Vasoconstriction | ET-1 вҶ’ ETA/ETB вҶ’ Gq/G12 вҶ’ PLC/RhoA вҶ’ IPвӮғ/CaВІвҒә/ROCK вҶ’ MLCK/MLCP вҶ’ vasoconstriction |
| NO-cGMP Vasodilation | eNOS/BH4/L-Arg вҶ’ NO вҶ’ sGC вҶ’ cGMP вҶ’ PKG вҶ’ Kv-channel opening вҶ’ vasodilation; PDE5 degradation |
| PGIвӮӮ-cAMP Vasodilation | AA вҶ’ COX вҶ’ PGIS вҶ’ PGIвӮӮ вҶ’ IP-receptor вҶ’ Gs вҶ’ AC вҶ’ cAMP вҶ’ PKA вҶ’ vasodilation |
| Growth Factor Signalling | BMPR2/ALK1/BMP9 вҶ’ SMAD1/5/8 вҶ’ ID1; TGF-ОІ вҶ’ SMAD2/3; PDGFR/VEGFR/FGFR вҶ’ RAS-ERK/PI3K-AKT-mTOR/STAT3 |
| Vascular Remodelling | PASMC proliferation, EC dysfunction, EndMT, collagen synthesis, MMP-2/9, ECM remodelling, plexiform lesion |
| Inflammation & Immune | Th1/Th2/Th17/Treg, M1/M2 macrophage, mast cells, B cells, NK/CD8+, IL-6/IL-1ОІ/TNF-Оұ вҶ’ NF-ОәB |
| Hypoxia & Metabolism | HIF-1Оұ/2Оұ, VHL/PHD axis, Warburg glycolysis, mitochondrial fission (DRP1/OPA1), Kv1.5вҶ“, ROS/NOX4/SOD2 |
| RV-PA Haemodynamics | PVR вҶ’ mPAP (Ohm's law); Ees/Ea coupling; Frank-Starling; RV hypertrophy вҶ’ failure; TR; IVS bowing; RAAS/SNS |
| Biomarkers | BNP/NT-proBNP, hs-TnI, TAPSE, RVEF, RAP, ET-1, DLCO |
| Drug PK/PD | ERA (bosentan/ambrisentan/macitentan, ICвӮ…вӮҖ Emax Hill); PDE5i (sildenafil/tadalafil); sGC stimulator (riociguat); PGIвӮӮ analogues (epoprostenol/treprostinil/selexipag) |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![PAH QSP Map](pulmonary-arterial-hypertension/pah_qsp_model.png)](pulmonary-arterial-hypertension/pah_qsp_model.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| ERA PK | ERA_gut, ERA_central, ERA_periph, ERA_effect | 2-compartment oral + effect-site equilibration |
| PDE5i PK | PDE5_gut, PDE5_central, PDE5_effect | 1-compartment oral + effect-site |
| PGIвӮӮ PK | PGI2_central, PGI2_effect | IV infusion (tВҪ ~3 min) |
| PD вҖ” Mediators | ET1, cGMP, cAMP | Turnover ODE for each second messenger |
| PD вҖ” Structure | VRI | Vascular Remodelling Index (logistic growth, drug reversal) |
| RV Function | Ees_RV | Adaptive hypertrophy вҶ’ maladaptive decompensation |
| Biomarker | BNP_conc | Wall-stressвҖ“driven BNP production |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dVRI/dt = k_growth Г— VRI Г— (1 вҲ’ VRI/VRI_max) вҲ’ (k_ERAГ—ERA_Inh + k_PDEГ—О”cGMP + k_PGIГ—PGIвӮӮ_Act) Г— VRI`
- `PVR = PVR_normal + (PVR_PAH0 вҲ’ PVR_normal) Г— [tone_frac Г— ET1/ET1_PAH Г— (1вҲ’ERA_Inh) Г— cGMPвӮҖ/cGMP Г— cAMPвӮҖ/cAMP + remod_frac Г— VRI/VRIвӮҖ]`
- `mPAP = CO Г— PVR/80 + PAWP`
- Simulates 6 scenarios (no treatment вҶ’ triple ERA+PDE5i+PGIвӮӮ) over 12 weeks

### Systemic Lupus Erythematosus (SLE)

> Directory: [`systemic-lupus-erythematosus/`](systemic-lupus-erythematosus/)

> NETs/cGAS-STING/TLR7/9 вҶ’ pDC вҶ’ IFN-Оұ кіјлӢӨ вҶ’ BAFFвҶ‘ вҶ’ Bм„ёнҸ¬ кіјнҷңм„ұнҷ” вҶ’ мһҗк°Җн•ӯмІҙ(anti-dsDNA) вҶ’ л©ҙм—ӯліөн•©мІҙ вҶ’ ліҙмІҙ мҶҢлӘЁ + лЈЁн‘ёмҠӨ мӢ м—јмқ„ мң л°ңн•ҳлҠ” ліөмһЎн•ң лӢӨмһҘкё° мһҗк°Җл©ҙм—ӯм§Ҳнҷҳ.

**Mechanistic Map** (161 nodes, 9 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Cell Death & Antigen Release | UV вҶ’ apoptosis, NETosis/PAD4 citrullination, secondary necrosis, HMGB1, mitochondrial DNA, defective phagocytosis, TREX1 deficiency |
| Innate Immunity & Type I IFN | pDC/mDC/monocytes, TLR7/TLR9/TLR4, cGAS-STING вҶ’ cGAMP, IRF3/IRF5/IRF7/MyD88/TRIF, NF-ОәB, IFN-Оұ/ОІ, IFNAR1/2 вҶ’ JAK1/TYK2 вҶ’ ISGF3(STAT1/STAT2/IRF9) вҶ’ ISGs (MX1/IFIT1/OAS/ISG15), DNase I, IL-1ОІ/NLRP3/TNF-Оұ/IL-12/IL-18 |
| B Cell Activation & Autoantibodies | NaГҜve B вҶ’ GC вҶ’ LLPC; BAFF/APRIL вҶ’ BAFF-R/TACI/BCMA; BCR/SYK/BTK/PI3KОҙ; CD40-CD40L; IL-21; anti-dsDNA/anti-Sm/anti-Ro/anti-La/anti-C1q/anti-nucleosome/ANA; IgG immune complexes |
| T Cell Dysregulation | Th1/Th2/Th17/Tfh/Treg/DN T cells/CD8+CTL; T-bet/RORОіt/FoxP3; IFN-Оі/IL-17A/IL-4/IL-6/IL-2/TGF-ОІ; calcineurin/NFAT; mTOR; JAK3/STAT3/STAT5; CTLA-4/PD-1/PDL-1/ICOS |
| Complement System | Classical (C1q/C1r-C1s/C4/C2/C3), Alternative (Factor B/H/Properdin/C3 tick-over), Lectin (MBL); C3a/C5a anaphylatoxins; MAC (C5b-9); FcОіRIIA/III; CR1; C4d deposition; C1q/C2/C4 gene deficiency |
| Lupus Nephritis | IC deposition вҶ’ mesangial/endothelial/podocyte injury вҶ’ GBM damage вҶ’ proteinuria; eGFR decline вҶ’ ESRD; TGF-ОІ fibrosis; ISN/RPS Class IвҖ“VI; VEGF; IL-6; neutrophil infiltration; hematuria; hypertension |
| Multi-Organ Involvement | Malar rash/discoid lupus/SCLE/photosensitivity; BBB disruption вҶ’ anti-NMDAR вҶ’ NPSLE; accelerated atherosclerosis; endothelial dysfunction; aPL antibodies вҶ’ APS/thrombosis; serositis; arthritis; alopecia; cytopenias |
| Drug PK/PD | HCQ (lysosomotropic TLR7/9 block; Vd ~5000 L, tВҪ ~50 days); Belimumab (anti-BAFF TMDD; tВҪ ~19 days; FcRn); Anifrolumab (anti-IFNAR1; 300 mg q4w); MMF/MPA (IMPDH inhibition); Voclosporin/Tacrolimus (calcineurin-NFAT); Cyclophosphamide (DNA alkylation); Azathioprine (6-MP/PRPP); Corticosteroids (GR transrepression); Obinutuzumab (anti-CD20) |
| Biomarkers & Clinical Endpoints | SLEDAI-2K; BILAG; SLICC damage index; anti-dsDNA titer; C3/C4 serum; ESR/CRP; lymphopenia; thrombocytopenia; UPCR; IFN score; BAFF level; SRI-4; BICLA; complete/partial renal response; LLDAS; DORIS remission; flare rate |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![SLE QSP Map](systemic-lupus-erythematosus/sle_qsp.png)](systemic-lupus-erythematosus/sle_qsp.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| HCQ PK | HCQ_gut, HCQ_cent | 1-compartment oral; Vd ~5200 L, tВҪ ~50 days |
| Belimumab PK+TMDD | BELI_cent, BELI_periph, BAFF_free, BELI_cmplx | 2-compartment IV + TMDD for free BAFF |
| Anifrolumab PK | ANIF_cent | 1-compartment IV (300 mg q4w); IFNAR occupancy |

| Autoantibodies | AntiDsDNA, IC_burden | LLPCвҶ’anti-dsDNAвҶ’IC turnover |
| Complement | C3_serum, C4_serum | IC-driven consumption; liver synthesis |
| Kidney | Proteinuria, eGFR_ode | ICвҶ’glomerular injuryвҶ’UPCR; voclosporin podocyte protection |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dIFNa/dt = k_pDC Г— TLR_act Г— (1 вҲ’ E_ANIF) вҲ’ k_IFNA Г— IFNa`
- `dBAFF/dt = Rin_BAFF вҲ’ kout_BAFF Г— BAFF вҲ’ kon Г— (BELI/V1) Г— BAFF + koff Г— complex + k_IFN_BAFF Г— IFNa`
- `dProteinuria/dt = k_IC_prot Г— IC_burden вҲ’ kout_prot Г— Prot Г— (1 + 1.5Г—E_VOC + 0.5Г—E_CS)`
- Simulates 7 scenarios (no Tx вҶ’ HCQ вҶ’ +MMF вҶ’ +Belimumab вҶ’ +Anifrolumab вҶ’ LN regimen вҶ’ triple LN) over 52 weeks

### IgA Nephropathy (IgAN)

> Directory: [`iga-nephropathy/`](iga-nephropathy/)

> л№„м •мғҒм ҒмңјлЎң лӢ№нҷ”лҗң IgA1(Gd-IgA1) л©ҙм—ӯліөн•©мІҙк°Җ мӮ¬кө¬мІҙ л©”мӮ°м§ҖмӣҖм—җ м№Ём°©лҗҳм–ҙ ліҙмІҙлҘј нҷңм„ұнҷ”мӢңмјң мЎұм„ёнҸ¬ мҶҗмғҒ л°Ҹ мӢ¬н•ң лӢЁл°ұлҮЁлҘј мң л°ңн•ҳлҠ” л©ҙм—ӯ л§Өк°ң мӮ¬кө¬мІҙмӢ м—ј. **мӮ¬мӨ‘ нғҖкІ© к°Җм„Ө(four-hit hypothesis)** кё°л°ҳ QSP лӘЁлҚё.

**Mechanistic Map** (155+ nodes, 12 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic/Environmental Risk | HLA-DQB1, TNFSF13/TNFSF13B (APRIL/BAFF genes), C1GALT1/Cosmc mutations, ST6GalNAc-II, DEFA1A3, gut dysbiosis, mucosal infection |
| Mucosal Immunity | Naive B вҶ’ Peyer's patch GC / tonsillar MALT, Tfh, IL-21/IL-4/IL-6/IL-10/TGF-ОІ class switching, AID, APRIL/BAFF, pIgR, sIgA |
| Hit 1 вҖ“ Gd-IgA1 | IgA1 hinge O-glycosylation; C1GalT1вҶ“/CosmcвҶ“ вҶ’ exposed GalNAc вҶ’ Gd-IgA1 serum elevation; ST6GalNAc-II competition; ASGPR hepatic clearance |
| Hit 2 вҖ“ Autoantibody | BCR (GalNAc epitope), GC reaction, SHM, class-switch вҶ’ anti-Gd-IgA1 IgG/IgA; CD4+ Tfh, IL-21, IL-17A |
| Hit 3+4 вҖ“ IC Deposition | Gd-IgA1 Г— IgG IC formation, IC polymerization/hexamerization, FcОұRI (CD89)/TfR1 mesangial receptors, mesangial deposition вҶ‘вҶ‘вҶ‘ |
| Complement System | Lectin (MBL/Ficolins/MASP-1/2), Classical (C1q), AP amplification (Factor B/D/P), C3 convertases CP+AP, C3 cleavage вҶ’ C3a/C3b, C5 convertase вҶ’ C5a/MAC (C5b-9), CD46/CD55 regulators |
| Mesangial Signaling | MC quiescentвҶ’activated; NF-ОәB, ERK, PI3K/AKT, PDGFR-ОІ/PDGF-BB; TGF-ОІ1/SMAD2-3/CTGF; IL-6/TNF-Оұ/MCP-1; MC proliferation, mesangial matrix expansion; ROS/NOX4; HIF-1Оұ |
| Glomerular Injury | Podocyte (healthyвҶ’injured); Nephrin/Podocin/Synaptopodin/TRPC6; foot process effacement; GBM thickening; вҶ‘glomerular permeability; proteinuria; hematuria; crescents; VEGF/Ang-2 |
| Tubular/Interstitial Fibrosis | PTC protein overload, TEC-EMT, interstitial macrophage/T cell, TGF-ОІ1 TIF, myofibroblast, Collagen I/III, MMP-2/9, TIMP-1/2, tubulointerstitial fibrosis, tubular atrophy |
| RAAS | Renin/AGT/AngI/ACE/AngII/AT1RвҖ“AT2R, aldosterone, NaвҒә retention, intraglomerular hypertension, SNS, ET-1, ACE2/Ang(1-7)/MasR |
| Drug PK/PD | ACEi/ARB, Sparsentan (dual AT1R+ETB), Budesonide TRF/Nefecon (mucosal APRIL suppression), Iptacopan (Factor B), Sibeprenlimab (anti-APRIL), Zigakibart (anti-C5), SGLT2i (dapagliflozin), Prednisolone, MMF, Atrasentan, Belimumab |
| Clinical Endpoints | eGFR, UPCR, 24-h proteinuria, serum Gd-IgA1/IgA, serum C3, creatinine, BP, Oxford MEST-C score (M/E/S/T/C), ESKD, CR50, complete remission, eGFR slope |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![IgAN QSP Map](iga-nephropathy/igan_qsp_model.png)](iga-nephropathy/igan_qsp_model.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| Budesonide TRF PK | BUD_gut, BUD_central | 1-compartment oral; F=15% (high hepatic extraction) |
| Sparsentan PK | SPA_gut, SPA_central | 1-compartment oral; F=85% |
| Iptacopan PK | IPT_gut, IPT_central | 1-compartment oral; BID dosing |
| Sibeprenlimab PK | SIB_depot, SIB_central, SIB_periph | SC 2-compartment; Q4W dosing |
| Four-hit PD | GdIgA1, AutoAb, IC_mes, CompAP | Hit 1вҖ“4 cascade with Emax drug effects |
| Glomerular | Podocyte, UPCR | Injury/repair ODE; proteinuria driven by podocyte loss |
| Fibrosis | TIF | Slow logistic fibrosis; protein-overload amplification |
| Renal function | eGFR | Continuous GFR loss from TIF + podocyte depletion |
| Hemodynamics | BP_sys | AngII-driven setpoint model |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dGdIgA1/dt = k_syn Г— (1 вҲ’ E_mucosal) вҲ’ k_deg Г— GdIgA1`  (budesonide + sibeprenlimab reduce synthesis)
- `dCompAP/dt = k_syn_CP Г— IC_mes Г— (1 вҲ’ E_iptacopan) вҲ’ k_deg Г— CompAP`  (AP pathway; Factor B blocked by iptacopan)
- `dUPCR/dt = k_syn_UPCR Г— (1вҲ’Podocyte) Г— (1+0.4Г—Mesangial) Г— (1вҲ’E_spa) Г— (1вҲ’E_RAAS) вҲ’ k_deg Г— UPCR`
- `deGFR/dt = вҲ’[k_loss_GFR Г— TIF + k_RAAS_GFR Г— (1вҲ’E_RAAS) Г— (1вҲ’Podocyte)] Г— eGFR`
- Simulates 7 scenarios (untreated вҶ’ triple Budesonide+Sparsentan+Iptacopan) over 2 years

**Calibration landmarks (trial data):**
- NefIgArd (Barratt 2023): Budesonide TRF вҶ’ UPCR вҲ’22% at 9 months вң“
- PROTECT (Heerspink 2023/2024): Sparsentan вҶ’ UPCR вҲ’49% at week 36 vs. irbesartan вң“
- APPLAUSE-IgAN (Rovin 2024): Iptacopan вҶ’ UPCR вҲ’38% vs. placebo вң“
- AFFINITY (Barratt 2023): Sibeprenlimab 700 mg вҶ’ UPCR вҲ’47% at 9 months вң“
- DAPA-CKD IgAN sub-analysis: dapagliflozin вҶ’ 71% RR reduction in composite ESKD вң“

### Multiple Sclerosis (MS)

> Directory: [`multiple-sclerosis/`](multiple-sclerosis/)  
> Disease category: **мһҗк°Җл©ҙм—ӯм§Ҳнҷҳ / мӢ кІҪкі„ (Autoimmune вҖ” CNS)**  
> Date added: **2026-06-16**

**Pathophysiology Summary:**  
Multiple sclerosis is a chronic autoimmune demyelinating disease of the CNS affecting ~2.8 million people worldwide. The immunopathology begins in peripheral lymphoid organs where myelin antigens (MOG, MBP, PLP) are presented by dendritic cells to naГҜve CD4вҒә T cells, driving Th1 (IFN-Оі+) and Th17 (IL-17A+) differentiation. These effector T cells up-regulate VLA-4 (Оұ4ОІ1 integrin) to engage VCAM-1 on blood-brain barrier (BBB) endothelium, triggering diapedesis into the CNS. Th17-derived IL-17A/MMP-9 additionally disrupts claudin-5 and ZO-1 tight junction proteins to widen the BBB leak. Once inside the CNS, infiltrating T cells together with activated microglia release TNF-Оұ, IL-1ОІ, NO, and ROS that are directly cytotoxic to oligodendrocytes, leading to demyelination. Loss of myelin trophic support results in NaV channel redistribution, CaВІвҒә overload, mitochondrial dysfunction, and axonal transection вҖ” the substrate of irreversible disability. B cells contribute via anti-MOG antibody production (intrathecal IgG; oligoclonal bands), complement activation, and antigen presentation. OPC-mediated remyelination can partially restore function but is inhibited by LINGO-1 and Nogo-A in the chronic lesion environment.

**Mechanistic Map:**

[![MS QSP Map](multiple-sclerosis/ms_qsp.png)](multiple-sclerosis/ms_qsp.svg)

*12 subgraph clusters В· 160+ nodes В· 7 drug PK/PD arms including TMDD (natalizumab)*

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| IFN-ОІ PK | A1_ifnb, C1_ifnb, C2_ifnb | 2-compartment SC/IM; F=40%; JAK-STAT PD |
| Natalizumab PK | C1_nat, C2_nat, RC_nat, R_nat | 2-comp IV + TMDD; kon/koff/kint |
| Ocrelizumab PK | C1_ocre, C2_ocre | 2-comp IV; Emax B cell depletion |
| Siponimod PK | C1_sip, C2_sip | 2-comp oral; S1PR1/5 antagonism |
| DMF/MMF PK | C1_dmf | 1-comp oral; Nrf2/NF-ОәB dual PD |
| Cladribine PK | C1_clad | 1-comp oral; dATP-mediated lymphodepletion |
| Peripheral immunity | Th1, Th17, Treg, Bcell | Normalized cell levels; drug inhibition terms |
| BBB | BBB | Integrity 0вҖ“1; IL-17A/MMP-9 disruption; natalizumab/IFNb protection |
| CNS infiltration | cTh1, cTh17 | BBB-gated infiltration; natalizumab blocks |
| Neuroinflammation | Micro | Microglia activation; Treg dampening |
| Myelination | Oligo, OPC, Myelin | OPC differentiation вҶ’ remyelination; LINGO-1 inhibition |
| Axonal integrity | Axon | Loss from demyelination + smouldering inflammation |
| Biomarkers | NfL, GFAP | Serum biomarkers; axon and astrocyte damage |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dMyelin/dt = k_remyelin Г— OPC Г— (1вҲ’Myelin) вҲ’ kdmyelin Г— Micro Г— Myelin Г— (1вҲ’E_Nrf2) + kin_myelin Г— (1вҲ’Myelin)`
- `dAxon/dt = k_repair Г— Myelin вҲ’ k_loss Г— (1вҲ’Myelin) вҲ’ k_lossГ—0.5 Г— Micro Г— Axon`
- `dRC_nat/dt = kon Г— Cnat Г— R вҲ’ (koff + kint) Г— RC_nat`  *(TMDD natalizumab)*
- `EDSS = 10 Г— (1вҲ’Axon) Г— 0.8 + 10 Г— (1вҲ’Myelin) Г— 0.2`
- Simulates 7 arms (untreated, IFN-ОІ, natalizumab, ocrelizumab, siponimod, DMF, cladribine) over 2 years

**Calibration landmarks (Phase III trial data):**
- AFFIRM (Polman 2006): Natalizumab вҶ’ ARR вҲ’68%, T2 вҲ’83% вң“
- OPERA I/II (Hauser 2017): Ocrelizumab вҶ’ ARR вҲ’46вҖ“47%, B cell depletion >95% вң“
- EXPAND (Kappos 2018): Siponimod вҶ’ 3m-CDP вҲ’21% in SPMS вң“
- DEFINE (Gold 2012): DMF 240 mg BID вҶ’ ARR вҲ’49% вң“
- CLARITY (Giovannoni 2010): Cladribine 3.5 mg/kg вҶ’ ARR вҲ’58% вң“
- MSCRG (Jacobs 1996): IFN-ОІ-1a IM вҶ’ ARR вҲ’18%, T2 вҲ’37% вң“

| Body Weight / Lipids | VAT/SAT; lipolysis; FFAвҶ’TGвҶ’LDLвҶ’sdLDLвҶ’ox-LDL; CETP; ketone bodies; caloric deficit from UGE |

**ODE System (25 state variables):**

| Module | States | Key Equations |
|--------|--------|---------------|
| Drug PK | MET_C, MET_P, EMPA_C, SEMA_SC, SEMA_C, DPP4I_C, SU_C, INS_SC, INS_C, PIOG_C | 2-cmpt metformin; SC depot for sema/insulin; 1-cmpt for rest |
| Glucose | Gp, Gt | `dGp/dt = (EGPвҲ’Rd)/(VgГ—BW) вҲ’ SgГ—(GpвҲ’90) вҲ’ UGE_loss/(VgГ—BW)` |
| Insulin | Ip, X_action | `dIp/dt = (GSISвҲ’CLГ—Ip)/Vi/BW`; `dX/dt = вҲ’p2Г—X + p2Г—SIГ—Ip` |
| Glucagon | Gc | `dGc/dt = koutГ—(Gc_ss вҲ’ Gc)`; Gc_ss = f(Gp, Ip, GLP-1RA) |
| GLP-1 | GLP1 | `dGLP1/dt = kin + kGpГ—(GpвҲ’90) вҲ’ (kDPP4Г—(1вҲ’DPP4i) + kout)Г—GLP1` |
| ОІ-cell | beta_mass | `dM/dt = (k_prolifГ—f(Gp) вҲ’ k_apopГ—f(FFA,Gp,GLP1)) / 24Г—365` |
| IR | IR_H, IR_P | FFA/glucose-driven increase; metformin/pioglitazone recovery |
| Lipid/Weight | FFA, BW_t | Anti-lipolytic insulin effect; UGE caloric loss; GLP-1RA weight |
| Endpoints | HbA1c_cmpt, eGFR_cmpt, UACR_cmpt | First-order equilibration; eGFR protected by SGLT2i |

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Dietary Input & Gut-Liver Axis | Dietary fat/fructose/CHO вҶ’ intestinal absorption вҶ’ chylomicron вҶ’ portal FFA/TG; fructolysis вҶ’ DNL; enterohepatic circulation; LPS translocation |
| Gut Microbiome | Dysbiosis (Firmicutes:Bacteroidetes вҶ‘); SCFA/LPS/TMAO/ETOH production; tight junction loss; bile acid transformation (BSH) |
| Hepatic Lipid Metabolism | DNL (SREBP-1c/ChREBP/FASN); FAO (PPARОұ/CPT1A); TG accumulation; VLDL assembly/secretion; ceramide/DAG lipotoxicity; steatosis (NAS) |
| Mitochondrial & Oxidative Stress | ETC leak вҶ’ ROS; lipid peroxidation (4-HNE/MDA); ER stress (ATF6/IRE1/PERK/UPR); Nrf2/antioxidant; mPTP вҶ’ apoptosis |
| Inflammatory Signaling (NASH) | TLR4/TLR2/NF-ОәB; NLRP3 inflammasome вҶ’ IL-1ОІ/IL-18; Kupffer cell M1/M2; TNF-Оұ/IL-6/IL-8/IL-10; neutrophil/macrophage recruitment; hepatocyte ballooning (NAS) |
| Fibrosis Pathway | TGF-ОІ1 вҶ’ ALK5/SMAD2/3 вҶ’ COL1A1/COL3A1/CTGF; HSC activation (quiescentвҶ’myofibroblast); PDGF proliferation; MMP-2/TIMP-1 balance; ECM accumulation вҶ’ F0вҶ’F4 |
| Insulin Resistance & Adipose-Liver Axis | VAT lipolysis вҶ’ portal FFA; adiponectin/leptin; IR (HOMA-IR) вҶ’ SREBP-1cвҶ‘/FOXO1вҶ’gluconeogenesis; PI3K/Akt; AMPK/SIRT1; DAG-PKCОө-IR |
| Drug PK/PD | Resmetirom (2-cmpt+OATP1B hepatic uptake, THRОІ Ki=0.9nM, вҶ“DNL/вҶ‘FAO); OCA (1-cmpt, FXR/SHP/CYP7A1вҶ“, anti-fibrotic); Semaglutide (SC depot QW, GLP-1R appetite+IR); Empagliflozin (oral, SGLT2 inhibition вҶ’ UGE вҶ’ weight loss) |
| Biomarkers & Clinical Endpoints | ALT/AST, MRI-PDFF, FibroScan LSM, NAS (0вҖ“8), FIB-4, ELF score, PRO-C3, LDL-C/TG/HDL-C, HbA1c, HOMA-IR, hs-CRP; NASH resolution, cirrhosis, HCC |
| Systemic Metabolic Context | BMI/obesity; hyperglycemia; dyslipidemia; hypertension; MetS; PCOS association; T2DM comorbidity; CVD risk; weight loss/fibrosis regression |

**ODE System (21 state variables):**

| Module | States | Key Equations |
|--------|--------|---------------|
| Resmetirom PK | RSM_GUT, RSM_CENT, RSM_PERI, RSM_LIVER | 2-cmpt oral + OATP1B hepatic uptake; Cl_liver = 0.7Г—CLГ—Cp/V |
| OCA PK | OCA_GUT, OCA_CENT | 1-cmpt high-hepatic-clearance; E_OCA = EmaxГ—Cp/(EC50+Cp) |
| Semaglutide PK | SEM_SC, SEM_CENT | SC depot (ka=0.0045 hвҒ»В№, tВҪвүҲ7d); E_SEM drives weight loss + IR |
| Empagliflozin PK | EMP_GUT, EMP_CENT | 1-cmpt oral; SGLT2 inhibition вҶ’ urinary glucose excretion |
| Liver fat | LIVER_FAT | `dLF/dt = KLINГ—DNLГ—(BW/BWвӮҖ) вҲ’ KOUTГ—LFГ—(1+0.6Г—E_RSM)(1+0.15Г—E_SEM)` |
| Insulin resistance | INS_RES | IR_ss = IRвӮҖГ—(1 + FFA-effect + TNF-effect вҲ’ adiponectin-protection)Г—(1 вҲ’ drug-effect) |
| Kupffer cell | KUPFFER | `dKUP/dt = (KOUTГ—KUPвӮҖ + KLIPГ—Lipotox)/(1 + drug-inh) вҲ’ KOUTГ—KUP` |
| Cytokines | TNFA, IL6C, TGFB | First-order; production вҲқ Kupffer activation + lipotoxicity; drug inhibition of TGF-ОІ |
| Fibrosis | HSC, COLLAGEN | `dHSC/dt = (KOUTГ—HSCвӮҖ + KTGFГ—TGFB)/(1+OCA/RSM-inh) вҲ’ KOUTГ—HSC` |
| ALT | ALT_CMT | `dALT/dt = KREL + KAPOPГ—TNFГ—Lipotox вҲ’ KOUTГ—ALT` |
| Adipokines/Weight | ADIPONECTIN, BODY_WT | Weight вҶ“ with semaglutide (KOUTГ—(WT_target вҲ’ WT)); adiponectin вҶ‘ with weight loss |

**Treatment Scenarios (6 arms, 72-week simulation):**

| # | Regimen | Expected О”Liver Fat | О”FIB Score | О”ALT |
|---|---------|---------------------|------------|------|
| 1 | Placebo | 0% | 0 | 0 U/L |
| 2 | Resmetirom 100 mg QD | вҲ’37% (MAESTRO-NASH) | вҲ’0.3 stage | вҲ’25 U/L |
| 3 | OCA 25 mg QD | вҲ’22% | вҲ’0.4 stage | вҲ’15 U/L |

| 6 | Triple (RSM + OCA + Sema) | вҲ’60% (est.) | вҲ’0.7 stage | вҲ’42 U/L |

**Calibration landmarks:**
- MAESTRO-NASH Phase 3 (Harrison 2024, *NEJM*): Resmetirom вҶ’ 25.9% NASH resolution, вҲ’37% liver fat, вҲ’24% LDL-C вң“
- REGENERATE (Friedman 2023, *Lancet*): OCA 25mg вҶ’ 23% вүҘ1 fibrosis stage improvement вң“
- ESSENCE Phase 3 (Newsome 2021, *NEJM*): Semaglutide вҶ’ 59% histological response, вҲ’31% liver fat вң“

### Heart Failure with Reduced Ejection Fraction (HFrEF)

> Directory: [`heart-failure-hfref/`](heart-failure-hfref/)

**Disease Overview**

Heart failure with reduced ejection fraction (HFrEF, LVEF < 40%) affects over 26 million people worldwide and carries a 5-year mortality of ~50%. The cardinal feature is neurohumoral activation вҖ” a vicious cycle in which impaired cardiac output triggers compensatory but ultimately maladaptive RAAS and SNS up-regulation, driving progressive ventricular remodeling, fibrosis, and further pump failure.

**Key Mechanistic Axes**

| Pathway | Core Biology |
|---------|-------------|
| RAAS | Reduced MAP вҶ’ renin release вҶ’ AngI вҶ’ ACE вҶ’ AngII вҶ’ AT1R вҶ’ vasoconstriction, aldosterone, Na retention, TGF-ОІ1, hypertrophy |
| ACE2 / Ang(1-7) axis | Counter-regulatory: ACE2 converts AngIвҶ’Ang1-7 вҶ’ MasR вҶ’ NOвҶ‘, vasodilation, anti-fibrotic |
| SNS | Low CO вҶ’ baroreceptor blunting вҶ’ CNS вҶ’ NEвҶ‘ вҶ’ ОІ1AR вҶ’ cAMP/PKA вҶ’ acute inotropy (short-term) вҶ’ ОІ1AR downregulation, apoptosis, RAAS stimulation (long-term) |
| NPS | Wall stress вҶ’ BNP/ANP вҶ’ NPR-A вҶ’ cGMP вҶ’ PKG вҶ’ vasodilation, natriuresis, anti-fibrotic |
| Cardiac Remodeling | AngII + Aldo + TNF-Оұ вҶ’ TGF-ОІ1 вҶ’ fibroblast вҶ’ myofibroblast вҶ’ ColI/ColIII + TIMPвҶ‘ вҶ’ ECM fibrosis; wall stress вҶ’ MAPK/NFAT/PI3K вҶ’ CM hypertrophy; CM apoptosis via ROS/caspase |
| Inflammation | NF-ОәB вҶ’ TNF-Оұ/IL-6/IL-1ОІ вҶ‘ (cardiodepressant cytokines); NLRP3 inflammasome; NOX2-ROS; iNOS peroxynitrite |
| Hemodynamics | LVEDVвҶ‘, SVвҶ“, COвҶ“, SVRвҶ‘, PCWPвҶ‘ вҶ’ congestion (dyspnea, edema) + forward failure (fatigue, exercise intolerance) |

**Drug PK/PD (GDMT 4+1 Pillars)**

| Drug Class | Agent | Mechanism | Key Trial |
|-----------|-------|-----------|-----------|
| ARNI | Sacubitril/Valsartan (Entresto) | NEP inhibition (вҶ‘BNP/Ang1-7/ANP plasma) + AT1R block | PARADIGM-HF: CV death/HF-hosp вҶ“20% vs enalapril |
| ОІ-Blocker | Metoprolol succinate / Carvedilol | ОІ1AR competitive antagonism вҶ’ вҶ“HR, вҶ“cAMP/PKA, reverse remodeling | MERIT-HF: all-cause mortality вҶ“34% |
| MRA | Spironolactone / Eplerenone / Finerenone | MR competitive block вҶ’ вҶ“Na retention, вҶ“TGF-ОІ1/fibrosis, вҶ‘K+ | RALES: mortality вҶ“30%; EMPHASIS-HF: CV death/HF-hosp вҶ“37% |
| SGLT2i | Dapagliflozin / Empagliflozin | Osmotic diuresis (вҶ“preload) + direct cardiac effects (NHE1вҶ“, mitochondriaвҶ‘, AMPKвҶ‘) | EMPEROR-Reduced: primary endpoint вҶ“25%; DAPA-HF: вҶ“26% |
| Ivabradine | Ivabradine | HCN/If channel block вҶ’ вҶ“HR (no inotropy) | SHIFT: CV death/HF-hosp вҶ“18% in HR вүҘ70 bpm |

### Chronic Kidney Disease (CKD)

> Directory: [`chronic-kidney-disease/`](chronic-kidney-disease/)

**Disease Overview**

Chronic Kidney Disease (CKD) affects ~850 million people worldwide and is defined by persistent abnormalities in kidney structure or function (eGFR < 60 mL/min/1.73mВІ or albuminuria вүҘ 30 mg/g) for more than 3 months. CKD is a major cause of cardiovascular disease, anemia, mineral bone disease, and ESKD requiring dialysis or transplantation. The pathophysiology is a self-amplifying cycle: initial injury (diabetes, hypertension, glomerulonephritis) вҶ’ nephron loss вҶ’ compensatory hyperfiltration вҶ’ podocyte injury вҶ’ glomerulosclerosis вҶ’ interstitial fibrosis вҶ’ further nephron loss вҶ’ eGFR decline.

**Key Mechanistic Axes**

| Pathway | Core Biology |
|---------|-------------|
| RAAS | Ang II вҶ’ AT1R вҶ’ glomerular hypertension + NF-ОәB + TGF-ОІ1 вҶ’ proteinuria + fibrosis; Aldosterone вҶ’ MR вҶ’ Na retention + cardiac/renal fibrosis |
| Inflammation | Uremic toxins/DAMPs вҶ’ NF-ОәB вҶ’ M1 macrophages/Th17 вҶ’ IL-6/TNF-Оұ/IL-17 вҶ’ podocyte injury + tubular atrophy |
| Fibrosis | TGF-ОІ1/Smad2-3 вҶ’ EMT + myofibroblast activation вҶ’ Collagen I/III + CTGF вҶ’ ECM accumulation; Smad7 inhibitory brake |
| CKD-MBD | eGFRвҶ“ вҶ’ PhosphateвҶ‘ + KlothoвҶ“ вҶ’ FGF-23вҶ‘ вҶ’ CYP27B1 inhibition вҶ’ CalcitriolвҶ“ вҶ’ PTHвҶ‘ вҶ’ secondary hyperparathyroidism вҶ’ bone disease + vascular calcification |
| Anemia | Peritubular cell loss вҶ’ EPOвҶ“; Inflammation вҶ’ HepcidinвҶ‘ вҶ’ Ferroportin degradation вҶ’ functional iron deficiency; PHD active вҶ’ HIF degraded вҶ’ blunted EPO response |
| Cardiovascular | Uremia вҶ’ ADMA вҶ’ eNOSвҶ“ вҶ’ NOвҶ“ вҶ’ endothelial dysfunction; BPвҶ‘ + Aldo вҶ’ LVH + cardiac fibrosis; Phosphate/PTH/uremic toxins вҶ’ vascular calcification вҶ’ arterial stiffness |

**Drug PK/PD (Treatment Landscape)**

| Drug Class | Agent | Mechanism | Key Trial |
|-----------|-------|-----------|-----------|
| ACE Inhibitor | Ramipril | ACE inhibition вҶ’ вҶ“Ang II вҶ’ вҶ“AT1R вҶ’ вҶ“UACR вҶ“BP | Lewis 1993 (NEJM) |
| ARB | Losartan | AT1R blockade вҶ’ вҶ“glomerular hypertension | RENAAL (NEJM 2001) |
| nsMRA | Finerenone 10вҖ“20 mg | Non-steroidal MR blockade вҶ’ вҶ“UACR вҲ’31%, вҶ“CV events | FIDELIO-DKD (NEJM 2020) |
| SGLT2i | Dapagliflozin 10 mg | SGLT2 block вҶ’ вҶ“TGF вҶ’ вҶ‘macula densa NaCl вҶ’ вҶ“glomerular hypertension | DAPA-CKD (NEJM 2020) |
| SGLT2i | Empagliflozin 10 mg | Same; effective to eGFR 20 mL/min | EMPA-KIDNEY (NEJM 2023) |
| ESA | Epoetin alfa / Darbepoetin | EPOR stimulation вҶ’ erythropoiesis вҶ’ вҶ‘Hb | Drueke et al. NEJM 2006 |
| HIF-PHI | Roxadustat 3Г—/week | PHD inhibition вҶ’ HIF-1Оұ stabilization вҶ’ вҶ‘endogenous EPO | DOLOMITES (JASN 2021) |
| Phosphate Binder | Sevelamer | GI phosphate binding вҶ’ вҶ“serum Phos вҶ’ вҶ“FGF-23 | Block JASN 2004 |
| Calcimimetic | Cinacalcet | CaSR allosteric activator вҶ’ вҶ“PTH | EVOLVE (NEJM 2012) |

**Mechanistic Map** (130+ nodes, 10 pathway subgraphs):

[![CKD QSP Map](chronic-kidney-disease/ckd_qsp_model.png)](chronic-kidney-disease/ckd_qsp_model.svg)

*Click image to open interactive SVG. Clusters: CKD Pathophysiology В· RAAS & Hemodynamics В· Inflammation & Immune Activation В· Renal Fibrosis Cascade В· CKD-MBD В· Anemia of CKD В· Cardiovascular Complications В· Drug PK В· Drug PD В· Clinical Endpoints*

**ODE Model Summary** (22 disease states + 13 drug PK compartments = 35 total ODEs)

| State Group | Variables |
|-------------|-----------|
| Kidney Function (3) | Nephron mass, eGFR, UACR |
| RAAS (3) | Ang II, Aldosterone, BP |
| Inflammation (3) | IL-6, TNF-Оұ, Macrophage infiltration |
| Fibrosis (2) | TGF-ОІ1, Collagen/fibrosis index |
| CKD-MBD (5) | FGF-23, Klotho, Phosphate, PTH, Active VitD |
| Anemia (3) | EPO, Hepcidin, Hemoglobin |
| Cardiovascular (2) | LVH index, Vascular calcification index |
| Drug PK (13) | ACEi (2), ARB (2), Finerenone (3), SGLT2i (2), ESA (2), HIF-PHI (2) |

**Treatment Scenarios (5)**

| Scenario | Regimen | 2-Year eGFR Slope | UACR Reduction | CV Risk |
|----------|---------|-------------------|----------------|---------|
| 1 | Natural History | вҲ’3.5 mL/min/yr | вҖ” | High |
| 2 | ACEi Monotherapy (Ramipril 10mg) | вҲ’2.1 mL/min/yr | вҲ’35% | Moderate |
| 3 | ACEi + Finerenone 20mg | вҲ’1.5 mL/min/yr | вҲ’50% | Low-Moderate |
| 4 | ACEi + SGLT2i (DAPA-CKD) | вҲ’1.3 mL/min/yr | вҲ’55% | Low-Moderate |
| 5 | Triple Therapy (ACEi + Dapa + Finerenone) | вҲ’0.8 mL/min/yr | вҲ’65% | Low |

| 5. Clinical Endpoints | 5-scenario comparison table; eGFR%/UACR% change plots; CKD stage timeline; CV risk composite |
| 6. CV Risk & CKD-MBD | SBP, LVH, vascular calcification, PTH, FGF-23/Klotho axis, active Vitamin D |

### Bronchial Asthma

> Directory: [`bronchial-asthma/`](bronchial-asthma/)

> м•Ңл ҲлҘҙкІҗ л“ұ нҷҳкІҪ мһҗк·№м—җ мқҳн•ҙ кё°лҸ„ мғҒн”јм—җм„ң л¶„л№„лҗҳлҠ” м•ҢлқјлҜј(TSLP/IL-25/IL-33)мқҙ ILC2В·мҲҳм§ҖмғҒм„ёнҸ¬лҘј нҷңм„ұнҷ”н•ҳкі , Th2 л¶„нҷ”(IL-4/IL-5/IL-13)В·IgE мғқм„ұВ·л№„л§Ңм„ёнҸ¬ нғҲкіјлҰҪВ·нҳёмӮ°кө¬ м№ЁмңӨВ·кё°лҸ„нҸүнҷңк·ј мҲҳм¶•В·м җм•Ў кіјл¶„л№„В·кё°лҸ„ лҰ¬лӘЁлҚёл§ҒмңјлЎң мқҙм–ҙм§ҖлҠ” Type-2 м—јмҰқ мӨ‘мӢ¬мқҳ л§Ңм„ұ кё°лҸ„ м§Ҳнҷҳ.

**Mechanistic Map** (110+ nodes, 16 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Environmental Triggers | Allergen (HDM/pollen/cat/mold), RV/RSV, PM2.5/O3, cold air, NSAID, tobacco |
| Airway Epithelium & Innate Barrier | TSLP, IL-25, IL-33/ST2, EGFR, TJ barrier disruption, IFN-О», ROS |
| ILC2 & Innate Lymphoid | ILC2 activation, GATA3, PGD2/CRTH2, KLRG1 inhibition; IL-4/IL-5/IL-13 (ILC2-derived) |
| Dendritic Cells | DC maturation, OX40L, MHC-II presentation, Th2 polarization |
| Th2 / Adaptive Immunity | Th2/Th1/Th17/Treg; GATA3/T-bet/RORОіt; IL-4/IL-5/IL-13/IL-9/IL-17A; STAT6/STAT5 |
| B Cell & IgE | GC reaction, plasma cell, IgE class-switch (AID), FcОөRI/CD23, total/free IgE |
| Mast Cell & Basophil | FcОөRI cross-linking, Syk/PLCОі/PI3K, histamine/PGD2/LTC4/tryptase release |
| Eosinophil Biology | BM вҶ’ blood вҶ’ tissue; IL-5RОұ; CCR3/eotaxin; MBP/ECP granule; Siglec-8 apoptosis |
| Airway Smooth Muscle | Ca2+/MLCK/MLC, RhoA/ROCK, cAMP/PKA, ОІ2AR, M3R, H1R, CysLT1/2, TRPA1 |
| Mucus & Goblet Cell | IL-13 вҶ’ SPDEF вҶ’ MUC5AC/MUC5B; CLCA1; submucosal gland hypertrophy |
| Airway Remodeling | TGF-ОІ1/SMAD2/3 вҶ’ fibroblastвҶ’myofibroblast вҶ’ collagen; VEGF; FGF-2; periostin; MMP-2/9 |
| Neurogenic Inflammation | SP/CGRP/NK1R, vagal reflex, ACh/M3, NGF вҶ’ sensory nerve plasticity |
| Lung Function & Clinical | FEV1, FVC, PEF, AHR, exacerbation rate, ACQ-5/7, AQLQ, symptom score, FeNO, PC20 |
| Biomarkers | Blood/tissue Eos, FeNO (ppb), serum IgE, periostin, tryptase, T2-high vs T2-low endotype |
| Drug PK | 2-compartment SC model for 5 biologics; ICS lung/systemic; LABA/LAMA; Omalizumab TMDD |
| Drug Mechanisms | Omalizumab (anti-IgE TMDD), Mepolizumab (IL-5вҶ“), Benralizumab (IL-5RОұ ADCC), Dupilumab (IL-4RОұ), Tezepelumab (TSLP), ICS/LABA/LAMA/Montelukast |

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment Group | ODE States | Description |
|-------------------|-----------|-------------|
| Mepolizumab PK | MEPO_SC, MEPO_C1, MEPO_C2 | 2-cmt SC; ka=0.0067/h, F=77% |
| Benralizumab PK | BENZ_SC, BENZ_C1, BENZ_C2 | 2-cmt SC; q4wГ—3 вҶ’ q8w; F=59% |
| Dupilumab PK | DUPIL_SC, DUPIL_C1, DUPIL_C2 | 2-cmt SC; ka=0.0042/h; tВҪвүҲ21 d |
| Tezepelumab PK | TEZE_SC, TEZE_C1, TEZE_C2 | 2-cmt SC; ka=0.0072/h; tВҪвүҲ26 d |
| Omalizumab + TMDD | OMAL_SC, OMAL_C1, IgE_FREE, IgE_RC | TMDD: kon/koff/kdeg; IgE_ss=2.25 nM |
| ICS / LABA | ICS_LUNG, ICS_SYS, LABA_C | GR-mediated cytokine suppression |
| TSLP | TSLP_PD | Alarmin hub; Tezepelumab neutralisation |
| IL-5 | IL5_PD | Eos growth/survival; Mepolizumab |
| IL-13 | IL13_PD | Goblet/ASM/remodeling; Dupilumab |
| Blood Eosinophil | EOS_B | IL-5-driven BM production/release |
| Tissue Eosinophil | EOS_T | Blood вҶ’ airway influx (IL-13/eotaxin) |
| ASM Tone | ASM_TONE | IL-13 + EOS_T driven; LABA relaxation |
| Mucus | MUCUS | IL-13 вҶ’ goblet вҶ’ MUC5AC |
| FEV1 | FEV1_ODE | Target driven by ASM/Mucus/EOS_T |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dIL5/dt = ksyn_IL5 Г— (1 + 0.5 Г— TSLP_rel) Г— (1 вҲ’ E_ICS) Г— (1 вҲ’ E_Mepo) вҲ’ kdeg_IL5 Г— IL5`
- `dEOS_B/dt = kprod Г— IL5_rel Г— (1 вҲ’ E_Mepo) Г— (1 вҲ’ E_Benz) вҲ’ kin Г— EOS_B`
- `dFEV1/dt = kFEV1 Г— (FEV1_target вҲ’ FEV1)` where `FEV1_target = 78 вҲ’ 30 Г— (0.5В·f_ASM + 0.3В·f_Mucus + 0.2В·f_EOS_T)`

**Treatment Scenarios (5):**

| # | Scenario | FEV1 О” (wk 52) | Blood Eos О” | AER О” |
|---|----------|-----------------|------------|-------|
| 1 | ICS/LABA only | +10вҖ“12% | вҲ’10% | baseline |
| 2 | + Mepolizumab 100 mg q4w | +16вҖ“18% | вҲ’70вҖ“80% | вҲ’50% |
| 3 | + Benralizumab 30 mg q4wвҶ’q8w | +17вҖ“19% | вҲ’90вҖ“97% | вҲ’51% |
| 4 | + Dupilumab 300 mg q2w | +18вҖ“20% | transient вҶ‘ then вҶ“ | вҲ’48% |
| 5 | + Tezepelumab 210 mg q4w | +19вҖ“21% | вҲ’65вҖ“75% | вҲ’56% |

### COPD (Chronic Obstructive Pulmonary Disease)

> Directory: [`copd/`](copd/)

> нқЎм—° л“ұ мң н•ҙ к°ҖмҠӨм—җ мқҳн•ң л§Ңм„ұм Ғ кё°лҸ„ м—јмҰқ л°Ҹ нҸҗнҸ¬ мңөн•©(нҸҗкё°мў…)мңјлЎң л№„к°Җм—ӯм Ғ кё°лҘҳ м ңн•ңмқҙ л°ңмғқн•ҳлҠ” м§Ҳнҷҳ. м „ м„ёкі„ м•Ҫ 3м–ө 8мІңл§Ң лӘ… мқҙнҷҳ, мӮ¬л§қ мӣҗмқё 3мң„(2019 GBD).

**Mechanistic Map** (110+ nodes, 12 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Environmental Triggers & Oxidative Stress | CS, AP, biomass; ROS/RNS; NRF2/HO-1/GSH; SIRT1/HDAC2вҶ“; oxidative inactivation of Оұ1-AT |
| Airway Epithelium & Mucociliary Clearance | Ciliated/goblet/club cells; tight junction loss; EMT; MUC5AC/MUC5BвҶ‘; PCLвҶ“; DAMPs (HMGB1, S100A8/9); TLR2/4/7/9; NLRP3 |
| Innate Immunity вҖ” Macrophage & Neutrophil | Alveolar macrophage M1; NF-ОәB / AP-1; IL-8/IL-1ОІ/IL-6/TNF-Оұ; MMP-12/MMP-9; NLRP3 inflammasome; Neutrophil/CXCR1-2; NE / PR3 / MPO / NETs |
| Adaptive Immunity | CD8+ Tc1 (dominant in COPD); Th1/Th17/Treg; IL-17A вҶ’ neutrophil amplification; B cells / lymphoid follicles; GM-CSF |
| Protease-Antiprotease Imbalance & ECM | NE / MMP-12/9 / Cathepsins vs Оұ1-AT / SLPI / TIMP; Elastin/collagen degradation вҶ’ Emphysema; Air trapping; FEV1вҶ“ |
| Small Airway Disease & Fibrotic Remodeling | TGF-ОІ1/SMAD2/3; myofibroblast; collagen I/III; ASM hypertrophy; EGFR; airway wall thickening; FEV1/FVCвҶ“ |
| Pulmonary Vasculature, RV & Comorbidities | HPV вҶ’ ET-1вҶ‘/NOвҶ“ вҶ’ PVRвҶ‘ вҶ’ PH (WHO Group 3) вҶ’ RV hypertrophy/cor pulmonale; V/Q mismatch; systemic inflammation/sarcopenia/CV/T2DM/osteoporosis |
| Clinical Endpoints & GOLD Classification | FEV1/FVC (GOLD 1-4); mMRC; CAT; BODE; 6MWT; SGRQ; AECOPD; GOLD ABE group |
| Drug PK вҖ” LAMA/LABA/ICS/PDE4i | Tiotropium / Umeclidinium / Glycopyrrolate; Salmeterol / Formoterol / Indacaterol; Budesonide / Fluticasone; Roflumilast N-oxide; NAC; Azithromycin |
| Drug PD Mechanisms | M3 mAChR вҶ’ ACh/IP3/Ca2+/ROCK вҶ’ broncho; ОІ2-AR вҶ’ cAMP/PKA вҶ’ relaxation; GR вҶ’ NF-ОәB/AP-1 transrepression; PDE4 вҶ’ cAMPвҶ‘ вҶ’ NF-ОәBвҶ“ |
| AECOPD Pathophysiology & Biomarkers | RV/Flu/RSV viral; H.flu/S.pneumo/P.aerug bacterial; CRP/PCT/Eos; SpO2вҶ“; AE treatment (SABA+SAMA+CS+AB+NIV) |
| Biomarkers (Multi-compartment) | Blood: CRP/IL-6/IL-8/NE/Eos/CC16/SP-D/fibrinogen; Sputum: neutrophil%/IL-8/NE/MUC5AC; Exhaled: FeNO/8-isoprostane/CO; Imaging: HRCT LAA-950/Pi10 |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![COPD QSP Map](copd/copd_qsp.png)](copd/copd_qsp.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary (26 ODE states):**

| Compartment Group | States | Description |
|-------------------|--------|-------------|
| LAMA PK (Tiotropium) | LAMA_LUNG, LAMA_C, LAMA_P | Inhaled 2-compartment; lung depot вҶ’ systemic (F_sys 3%); CL 3.92 L/h; tВҪ 5-6 days |
| LABA PK (Salmeterol) | LABA_LUNG, LABA_C, LABA_P | Lung depot; CYP3A4/2D6; CL 23 L/h |
| ICS PK (Budesonide) | ICS_LUNG, ICS_C, ICS_P | Lung F=22%; first-pass extraction 90%; CL 78 L/h; tВҪ 2.8h |
| PDE4i PK (Roflumilast) | PDE4i_C | Oral F=80%; CL 9.1 L/h; tВҪ 17h (N-oxide 30h) |
| Inflammation PD | IL8, NE_sput, CRP, Eos | Turnover ODEs; ICS/PDE4i Emax suppression; Eos-gated ICS response |
| Lung Function | FEV1, Emph | FEV1: natural decline + BD gain + inflam penalty + AE step-loss; Emphysema: NE-driven irreversible |
| Pulmonary Vascular | PVR | HPV-driven PVR increase with FEV1 decline |
| Exacerbation | AE_cum, AE_rate_ann | Poisson rate; ICS/PDE4i reduction; post-AE amplification |

**Key ODE Equations:**
- `dFEV1/dt = 0.05Г—(FEV1_target вҲ’ FEV1) вҲ’ k_decГ—FEV1 вҲ’ k_inflamГ—(IL8/IL8вӮҖвҲ’1)Г—FEV1 вҲ’ k_AEГ—О»_AEГ—FEV1`
- `dEmph/dt = k_progГ—(NE_sput/NEвӮҖ)Г—(1вҲ’E_ICSГ—0.05)Г—(100вҲ’Emph)` вҖ” irreversible, NE-driven
- `dPVR/dt = k_PVRГ—(FEV1вӮҖ/FEV1вҲ’1)Г—PVRвӮҖ вҲ’ k_PVRГ—0.1Г—(PVRвҲ’PVRвӮҖ)` вҖ” hypoxia-driven remodeling
- `E_LAMA = Emax_LAMAГ—C_lung/(EC50_LAMA + C_lung)` вҖ” Emax bronchodilation model

**Clinical Trial Calibration:**

| Trial | Treatment | n | Key Result | Model Calibrated Parameter |
|-------|-----------|---|------------|---------------------------|
| UPLIFT 2008 | Tio 18Вөg qd | 5,993 | FEV1 +87 mL, AE RR 0.86 | k_FEV1_dec, Emax_LAMA |
| TORCH 2007 | SFC 50/500Вөg bid | 6,112 | AE RR 0.75, PneumoniaвҶ‘ | Emax_ICS, lambda_AE |
| FLAME 2016 | IND/GLY vs SFC | 3,362 | LABA/LAMA > ICS/LABA for AE | E_LAMA+E_LABA > E_ICS |
| IMPACT 2018 | FF/UMEC/VI triple | 10,355 | AE RRвҶ“ 25% vs LABA/LAMA | Triple interaction terms |
| ETHOS 2020 | BUD/GLY/FORM | 8,509 | EosвүҘ300 вҶ’ strongest ICS effect | Eos_thresh, Eos_factor |
| EINSTEIN 2009 | Roflumilast 500Вөg | 3,091 | AE rateвҶ“ 15-17% | Emax_PDE4i, EC50_PDE4i |
| HIACE 2013 | NAC 600mg bid | 120 | AE rateвҶ“ 24% | NAC antioxidant pathway |
| Albert 2011 | Azithromycin 250mg/d | 1,142 | AE rateвҶ“ 27% | Azithro NF-ОәB pathway |

**Treatment Scenarios (6 arms, 1-year simulation):**
1. Placebo вҖ” Natural history (FEV1 decline ~50 mL/yr in GOLD 2-3)
2. LAMA monotherapy вҖ” Tiotropium 18Вөg qd (UPLIFT calibrated)
3. LABA/LAMA dual вҖ” Salmeterol 50Вөg bid + Tiotropium (FLAME/POET-COPD)
4. ICS/LABA dual вҖ” Budesonide 400Вөg bid + Salmeterol (TORCH; Eos-gated)
5. Triple therapy вҖ” LAMA+LABA+ICS (IMPACT/ETHOS)
6. Triple + Roflumilast вҖ” Severe COPD + chronic bronchitis (EINSTEIN)

**Shiny App (7 tabs):**

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| 1. Patient Profile | GOLD stage gauge, FEV1/Eos/CAT value boxes, GOLD ABE framework table |
| 2. Pharmacokinetics | Lung vs systemic Cp-time curves (48h); steady-state Css + PD effect table |
| 3. Lung Function | FEV1 trajectory, GOLD stage bar, emphysema index, PVR time course |
| 4. Inflammatory Biomarkers | IL-8, NE, CRP, Eosinophils with threshold lines; ICS Eos-guidance rationale |
| 5. Clinical Endpoints | CAT score, cumulative AEs, annualized AE rate, SpO2, mPAP |
| 6. Scenario Comparison | All 6 arms overlay; end-of-year DT summary table with GOLD color coding |
| 7. Exacerbation Risk | Risk calculator (FEV1/Eos/history вҶ’ rate); pathogen guide (PCT); RR waterfall chart |

### Crohn's Disease (CD)

**Disease Overview:** Crohn's disease is a chronic, transmural inflammatory bowel disease affecting any segment of the GI tract (most commonly terminal ileum and colon). It is driven by a dysregulated mucosal immune response to luminal antigens in genetically susceptible individuals, characterized by non-caseating granulomas, Th1/Th17 dominance, and NOD2/CARD15 mutations in ~20% of patients.

**Mechanistic Map (134 nodes, 10 clusters):**

[![Crohn's Disease QSP Map](crohn-disease/cd_qsp_model.png)](crohn-disease/cd_qsp_model.svg)

| Cluster | Key Nodes |
|---------|-----------|
| Luminal / Microbiome | Dysbiosis (вҶ‘Proteobacteria, вҶ“Firmicutes), PAMPs (LPS/Flagellin), SCFAs, Secretory IgA, Bile acids, FMT |
| Epithelial Barrier | Enterocyte, Goblet cell (MUC2), Paneth cell (Defensins), M-cell (antigen sampling), Tight junctions (Claudin/Occludin/ZO-1), MLCK, NOD2 |
| Innate Immunity | Macrophage M1/M2, DC (CD103+), Neutrophil, ILC1/ILC3, NETs, TLR2/4/9, NOD2, NLRP3 inflammasome, Complement (C3/C5a), Mast cell |
| T Cells (Adaptive) | NaГҜve CD4+, Th1 (IFN-Оі/TNF-Оұ, T-bet), Th17 (IL-17A/F/21, RORОіt), Th2, Treg (FoxP3+), CD8+ CTL, Memory T, JAK1/2вҖ“STAT signaling |
| B Cells (Adaptive) | B cell activation (CD40L/CD40), Germinal center, Plasma cell, pANCA, Mucosal IgA, Memory B |
| Cytokine Network | TNF-Оұ, IL-1ОІ, IL-6, IL-12, IL-23, IL-17A/F, IL-21, IL-10, IL-22, TGF-ОІ, IFN-Оі, IL-18, IL-33, CXCL8/10, CCL2, NF-ОәB |
| Tissue Remodeling | Myofibroblast, Fibrocyte, Collagen I/III, MMP-3/9, TIMP-1, VEGF, Intestinal stricture, Non-caseating granuloma |
| Drug PK/PD | IFX (2-cpt IV), ADA (SC depot), UST (2-cpt), VDZ (1-cpt), 6-TGN (AZA metabolite), Upadacitinib, Prednisone, Budesonide, MTX |
| Clinical Endpoints | CDAI, HBI, SES-CD, CDEIS, CRP, Fecal calprotectin, Clinical remission, Mucosal healing, Deep remission |
| Systemic Complications | Anemia, Malnutrition, Bone loss (BMD), PSC, Skin/Eye/Joint EIM, VTE risk, Growth failure (pediatric) |

**mrgsolve ODE Model (22 states):**

| Compartment Group | States | Description |
|-------------------|--------|-------------|
| IFX PK | A1_IFX, A2_IFX | 2-compartment IV; Vc=4.0 L, Vp=3.5 L, CL=0.55 L/day, Q=1.40 L/day (Fasanmade 2011, Ordas 2012) |
| ADA PK | ADA_dep, A_ADA | SC depotвҶ’central; V=7.8 L, CL=0.35 L/day, ka=0.38/day, F=0.64 (Ternant 2008) |
| UST PK | A1_UST, A2_UST | 2-compartment; Vc=3.5 L, Vp=7.3 L, CL=0.19 L/day; IV inductionвҶ’SC maintenance (Adedokun 2018) |
| VDZ PK | A_VDZ | 1-compartment IV; Vc=3.3 L, CL=0.49 L/day (Rosario 2017) |
| 6-TGN from AZA | A_TGN | RBC-distributed; therapeutic range 235вҖ“450 pmol/8Г—10вҒё RBC (Osterman 2006) |
| Prednisone | A_PRED | 1-compartment; V=45 L, CL=7.2 L/day, tВҪвүҲ4.4 h |
| Upadacitinib (JAK1i) | A_UPA | 1-compartment oral; V=85 L, CL=24 L/day, F=0.79 |
| TNF-Оұ | TNF | pg/mL; SS=100 (active CD); kprod feedback on MI; Emax IFX/ADA 93вҖ“90% |
| IL-12/23 composite | IL1223 | pg/mL; SS=80; UST Emax=88%; UPA partial suppression |
| IL-17A | IL17 | pg/mL; SS=60; Th17- and IL-23-driven; JAKi-sensitive |
| Th17 / Th1 cells | Th17, Th1 | Normalized; IL-23-driven expansion; Treg-mediated suppression; VDZ/TGN/JAKi block |
| Treg | Treg | Normalized; TGF-ОІ/SCFA-dependent; mild expansion with treatment |
| Mucosal neutrophils | Neut | Normalized; IL-17A + TNF-Оұ recruitment; disease driver |
| Mucosal Inflammation | MI | 0вҖ“100 score; composite of TNF/IL-17/Neut/Treg signals; maps to CDAI/SES-CD |
| CRP | CRP | mg/L; SS=25 (active); IL-6 proxy; target <5 mg/L (STRIDE-II) |
| Fecal Calprotectin | FC | Ојg/g; SS=800; neutrophil + mucosal inflammation driven; target <150 Ојg/g |
| Bone Mineral Density | BMD | Normalized; TNF-Оұ + steroid accelerated loss |
| Hemoglobin | Hgb | g/dL; SS=10.5 (mild ACD); suppressed by hepcidin/IL-6 via MI |

**Key ODE Equations:**
- `dxdt_TNF = kprod_TNF Г— (1 + 0.4Г—(MI/MIвӮҖвҲ’1)) Г— (1вҲ’E_antiTNF) вҲ’ kdeg_TNF Г— TNF`
- `dxdt_IL17 = kprod_IL17 Г— (1 + kIL23_IL17Г—(IL1223/IL12230вҲ’1)) Г— (Th17/Th17вӮҖ) Г— (1вҲ’E_JAKi) вҲ’ kdeg_IL17 Г— IL17`
- `dxdt_Th17 = kprol_Th17 Г— Th17 Г— (1 + kIL23_Th17Г—(IL1223/IL12230вҲ’1)) Г— (1вҲ’kTreg_Th17Г—(Treg/TregвӮҖ)) Г— (1вҲ’E_VDZ) вҲ’ kdeg_Th17 Г— Th17`
- `dxdt_MI = kprod_MI Г— (1 + MI_stim вҲ’ MI_supp) Г— (1вҲ’E_combined) вҲ’ kdeg_MI Г— MI`
- `dxdt_CRP = kprod_CRP Г— MI вҲ’ kdeg_CRP Г— CRP`
- `dxdt_BMD = kform_BMD Г— BMD вҲ’ (kresorb_BMD + kTNF_BMDГ—TNF/TNFвӮҖ + kPRED_BMDГ—C_PRED) Г— BMD`

**Clinical Trial Calibration:**

| Trial | Treatment | n | Key Result | Model Calibrated Parameter |
|-------|-----------|---|------------|---------------------------|
| ACCENT I (Hanauer 2002) | IFX 5 mg/kg | 573 | Remission 39% w54 | CL_IFX, Emax_IFX_TNF |
| CHARM (Colombel 2007) | ADA 40 mg q2w | 854 | Remission 36% w26 | CL_ADA, Emax_ADA_TNF |
| UNIFI (Feagan 2016) | UST 6 mg/kg IV | 741 | Remission 21% w8 (IV) | CL_UST, Emax_UST |
| GEMINI II (Sandborn 2013) | VDZ 300 mg | 814 | Remission 39% w52 | CL_VDZ, Emax_VDZ_MI |
| U-ACHIEVE (Loftus 2023) | UPA 45 mg QD | 526 | Remission 39.5% w12 | CL_UPA, Emax_UPA |
| SONIC (Colombel 2010) | IFX+AZA combo | 508 | Remission 56.8% w26 | 6-TGN synergy, ATI suppression |

**Treatment Scenarios (7 arms, 78-week simulation):**
1. No Treatment вҖ” Natural history; CDAI ~280, CRP ~25 mg/L, FC ~800 Ојg/g
2. Infliximab 5 mg/kg IV вҖ” w0/2/6 induction вҶ’ q8w maintenance
3. Adalimumab 160/80/40 mg SC вҖ” q2w maintenance
4. Ustekinumab 6 mg/kg IV вҶ’ 90 mg SC q8w
5. Vedolizumab 300 mg IV вҖ” w0/2/6 вҶ’ q8w (gut-selective)
6. Upadacitinib 45 mg QD вҶ’ 30 mg QD maintenance (oral JAK1i)
7. IFX + Azathioprine 150 mg/day вҖ” combination (anti-immunogenicity)

**Shiny App (7 tabs):**

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| 1. Patient Profile | Demographics, disease location/behaviour, baseline CDAI/CRP/FC, prior biologic history, disease severity radar |
| 2. Pharmacokinetics | IFX/ADA/UST/VDZ Cp-time curves, VDZ Оұ4ОІ7 receptor occupancy, 6-TGN RBC levels with therapeutic range annotation, PK summary table |
| 3. Cytokines & PD | TNF-Оұ, IL-17A, IL-12/23, Th17/Treg ratio, Mucosal Inflammation Score, CRP & Fecal Calprotectin time courses |

| 5. Scenario Comparison | All 7 arms overlay (CDAI/CRP/FC/MI); Week 52 DT summary table with response/remission/mucosal healing rates |
| 6. Biomarker Correlations | Population PK/PD sim (N=150, IIV via log-normal); CRP vs CDAI, FC vs SES-CD, drug trough vs CRP, TNF vs MI scatter plots |
| 7. Dosing Optimizer | DoseвҖ“response curves (CRP/CDAI at Week 52 vs dose); optimal trough concentration analysis; drug comparison |

### Ankylosing Spondylitis (AS)

**Disease Overview:** Ankylosing Spondylitis (AS) is a chronic, progressive inflammatory arthritis affecting primarily the axial skeleton (sacroiliac joints and spine). It is strongly associated with HLA-B27 (>90% positive). The hallmark pathology is dual: inflammatory bone erosion at entheses AND pathological new bone formation (syndesmophytes вҶ’ ankylosis). The gutвҖ“joint axis (subclinical IBD in ~60%, ILC3-driven IL-17 amplification) and IL-17/IL-23/TNF cytokine network are central to pathogenesis.

**Mechanistic Map (162 nodes, 10 clusters):**

[![Ankylosing Spondylitis QSP Map](ankylosing-spondylitis/as_qsp_model.png)](ankylosing-spondylitis/as_qsp_model.svg)

| Cluster | Key Nodes |
|---------|-----------|
| 1. Genetic & Environmental | HLA-B27 (misfolding вҶ’ UPR вҶ’ IL-23), ERAP1, IL-23R variant, CARD9, ER stress, HLA-B27 homodimers (KIR3DL2), Mechanical stress, Microbial trigger |
| 2. Innate Immunity & Enthesis | Enthesis (primary lesion), Fibrocartilage, DAMPs (HSP60/HMGB1/S100), TLR2/4/9, NF-ОәB, Macrophage M1, DC (pDC/cDC), Neutrophil, Mast cell, ILC3, ОіОҙ/MAIT T cells, NLRP3/IL-1ОІ/IL-18, ROS/NET |
| 3. Adaptive Immunity | Naive CD4+, Th17 (RORОіt/IL-17A вҳ…/IL-17F/IL-22), Th1 (IFN-Оі/TNF), Treg, CD8+ T (HLA-B27), NK, JAK-STAT3, RORC/T-bet, STAT4 |
| 4. Inflammatory Signaling | TNF-Оұ (total), TNFR1/R2, NF-ОәB hub, MAPK/p38, AP-1, JAK1/2/3, STAT1/3, IL-6 (total), gp130, CRP, SAA, MMP-3/9, COX-2/PGE2 |
| 5. Bone Remodeling | Osteoclast (erosion), Osteoblast (new bone), RANKL/RANK/OPG ratio вҳ…, M-CSF, Wnt/LRP5-6 pathway, DKK1, Sclerostin (SOST), BMP-2/4/7, Smad1/5/8, Hedgehog, TGF-ОІ1, Syndesmophyte, mSASSS |
| 6. Target Organs & Clinical | SIJ (primary), Spine (thoracolumbar), Uveitis (EIM 27%), IBD (EIM), Hip, BASDAI, ASDAS-CRP, BASFI, BASMI, ASAS 20/40 |
| 7. Drug PK | ADA (40mg SC q2w), ETA (50mg SC qw), IFX (5mg/kg IV), CZP, GLM, SEC (150/300mg SC), IXE, Bimekizumab, GUS, RIS, TOF (5mg BID), UPA (15mg QD), NSAIDs |
| 8. Drug PD | TNFi (TNF neutralization), IL-17Ai (IL-17A Вұ F block), Bimekizumab (IL-17A+F dual), IL-23i (p19 subunit), JAKi (JAK1-selective), NSAID/COX-2 inhibition |
| 9. GutвҖ“Joint Axis | Gut microbiome dysbiosis (вҶ“Lachnospiraceae, вҶ‘Prevotella), gut ILC3, Gut DC IL-23 production, Subclinical IBD (60%), Portal circulation, Molecular mimicry |
| 10. PK/PD Outputs | Free TNF/IL-17/IL-23, Disease activity (composite), BASDAI/ASDAS-CRP simulated, mSASSS progression, ASAS20/40, Trial calibration (ATLAS/MEASURE/COAST-V/SELECT-AXIS/GUIDE) |

**mrgsolve ODE Model (22 states):**

| Compartment Group | States | Description |
|-------------------|--------|-------------|
| Adalimumab PK | ADA_SC, ADA_C | 1-cmpt SC; ka=0.019/h, F=0.64, CL=9.6 mL/h, V=7600 mL, tВҪвүҲ14 d |
| Etanercept PK | ETA_SC, ETA_C | 1-cmpt SC; ka=0.048/h, F=0.76, tВҪвүҲ4 d |
| Secukinumab PK | SEC_SC, SEC_C, SEC_P | 2-cmpt SC; ka=0.015/h, F=0.73, CL=4.8 mL/h, Vc=3600, Vp=2800, Q=1.2 mL/h, tВҪвүҲ27 d |
| Tofacitinib PK | TOF_C | 1-cmpt oral; ka=1.5/h, F=0.74, CL=3500 mL/h, V=87000 mL, tВҪвүҲ3 h |
| Upadacitinib PK | UPA_C | 1-cmpt oral; ka=1.2/h, F=0.79, CL=8500 mL/h, V=96000 mL, tВҪвүҲ15 h |
| NSAID PK | NSAID_C | 1-cmpt oral; naproxen proxy, tВҪвүҲ12вҖ“14 h |
| Cytokine PD | TNF, IL17A, IL23, IL6 | pg/mL; IL-17/IL-23 cross-drive; JAKi partial suppression of all; TNFi Emax=85%, IL-17Ai Emax=90% |
| Acute Phase | CRP | mg/L; IL-6-driven hepatic production; tВҪвүҲ19 h; ASDAS component |
| Bone remodeling | RANKL, OPG | AU; TNF upregulates RANKL, downregulates OPG; TNFi partially reverses |
| Osteoclast | OC | Activity (AU); driven by RANKL/OPG ratio Г— TNF; TNFi inhibits |
| Bone formation | BF | Syndesmophyte index; IL-17A + Wnt/BMP driven; TNF-DKK1 paradox modeled |
| Structural outcome | Erosion, mSASSS | Cumulative scores; mSASSS rate: IL-17Ai > TNFi inhibition |
| Composite disease | DiseaseAct | 0вҖ“1 continuous; Kout model; maps to BASDAI/ASDAS |

**Key ODE Equations:**
- `dxdt_TNF = kprod_TNF Г— TNF_base Г— IL17_amp Г— HLA_factor вҲ’ kdeg_TNF Г— TNF Г— (1 + Inh_TNFi + 0.3Г—Inh_JAKi)`
- `dxdt_IL17A = kprod_IL17 Г— IL17_base Г— (1 + 0.6Г—IL23_drv) Г— HLA_factor вҲ’ kdeg_IL17 Г— IL17A Г— (1 + Inh_IL17i + 0.2Г—Inh_JAKi)`
- `dxdt_BF = kform_BF Г— (1 + 0.5Г—IL17A/IL17_base) Г— (1 вҲ’ 0.4Г—Inh_TNFi) вҲ’ kdeg_BF Г— BF` вҶҗ TNF-DKK1 paradox
- `dxdt_mSASSS = 0.00015 Г— BF Г— (1 вҲ’ 0.5Г—Inh_IL17i вҲ’ 0.3Г—Inh_TNFi)` вҶҗ IL-17Ai > TNFi for bone
- `BASDAI_sim = BASDAI_ss Г— DiseaseAct / 0.68`

**Clinical Trial Calibration:**

| Trial | Drug | n | Primary Endpoint | Observed | Model |
|-------|------|---|-----------------|---------|-------|
| ATLAS wk 24 | Adalimumab 40mg q2w | 208 | ASAS20 | 59% vs 22% PBO | вң“ |
| MEASURE 1 wk 16 | Secukinumab 150mg | 371 | ASAS20 | 61% vs 29% PBO | вң“ |
| GO-RAISE wk 24 | Golimumab 50mg q4w | 356 | ASAS20 | 59% vs 22% PBO | вң“ (ADA proxy) |
| COAST-V wk 16 | Ixekizumab 80mg q4w | 341 | ASAS20 | 52% vs 18% PBO | вң“ (SEC proxy) |
| SELECT-AXIS 1 wk 14 | Upadacitinib 15mg QD | 187 | ASAS40 | 52% vs 26% PBO | вң“ |
| GUIDE | Guselkumab 100mg q8w | 474 | ASAS20 | active vs PBO | вң“ (IL-23i class) |

**Treatment Scenarios (7 arms, 52-week simulation):**
1. Placebo вҖ” Natural history; BASDAI ~6.8, ASDAS ~3.9, CRP ~15 mg/L
2. Adalimumab 40mg SC q2w вҖ” TNFi; Inh_TNFi Emax=0.85
3. Etanercept 50mg SC qw вҖ” TNFi (shorter tВҪ=4d); similar efficacy
4. Secukinumab 150mg SC (loading wk0вҖ“4 then q4w) вҖ” IL-17Ai; superior mSASSS suppression
5. Tofacitinib 5mg BID oral вҖ” JAK1/3; ASAS40 ~40%; rapid onset (tВҪ 3h)
6. Upadacitinib 15mg QD oral вҖ” JAK1-selective; superior vs tofacitinib on bone
7. NSAID (naproxen equivalent) вҖ” Symptom relief only; partial CRP reduction

**Shiny App (7 tabs):**

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| 1. Patient Profile | Demographics (WT, sex, HLA-B27), BASDAI/CRP/IL-17A baseline, prior TNFi history, disease severity classification, drug suitability radar chart |
| 2. Drug PK | ConcentrationвҖ“time profiles (Ојg/mL for biologics, ng/mL for JAKi), 2-cmpt SEC peripheral compartment, PK parameter table, Cmax/Tmax/AUC summary |
| 3. Disease Activity | BASDAI & ASDAS-CRP dual-axis plot, threshold annotations (BASDAI<4, ASDAS<2.1), CRP dynamics, TNF-Оұ and IL-17A suppression side-by-side |
| 4. Structural Progression | mSASSS cumulative plot, bone formation vs erosion trajectories, RANKL:OPG ratio, TNF-DKK1 paradox bone interpretation |
| 5. Clinical Endpoints | ASAS20/40 probability over time, BASDAI50 milestone, response table at wk 4/12/16/24/52, trial benchmark comparison (ATLAS/MEASURE) |
| 6. Scenario Comparison | All 7 drugs overlay (BASDAI, TNF, mSASSS), Week-24 DT summary with BASDAI/ASDAS/CRP/ASAS20/40 by scenario |
| 7. Biomarker Dashboard | Selectable biomarkers (TNF, IL-17A, IL-23, IL-6, CRP, RANKL, OPG), drug efficacy inhibition % plot, osteoclast & bone formation time course |

### Atrial Fibrillation (AF)

> Directory: [`atrial-fibrillation/`](atrial-fibrillation/)

**Disease Summary**

Atrial fibrillation is the most common sustained cardiac arrhythmia, affecting >37 million people worldwide. AF arises from complex interactions among electrical remodeling (shortened ERP, conduction slowing), CaВІвҒә handling disturbances (RyR2 leak вҶ’ DADs), structural fibrosis (AngII/TGF-ОІ1/SMAD), inflammation (NLRP3/IL-1ОІ/ROS), and autonomic nervous system dysregulation. The resulting wavelength shortening allows reentry circuits and focal pulmonary vein triggers to maintain AF ("AF begets AF"). Atrial stasis creates a prothrombotic state (Virchow's triad: stasis + endothelial dysfunction + hypercoagulability) that drives stroke risk. Management involves rate control (beta-blockers), rhythm control (antiarrhythmics), anticoagulation (DOACs), and upstream RAAS therapy.

**Key Pathways Modeled**

| Cluster | Key Nodes |
|---------|-----------|
| Risk Factors | HTN, HF, obesity, OSA, T2DM, genetic variants (PITX2, ZFHX3), atrial stretch |
| Electrical Remodeling | Nav1.5 (INa), Cav1.2 (ICaL), Kv1.5 (IKur), IKACh (Kir3.1/3.4), hERG (IKr), Cx40/43 gap junctions, ERP shortening, wavelength shortening, reentry circuits, focal PV triggers |
| CaВІвҒә Handling | SERCA2a/PLN, RyR2 leak, NCX1, CaMKII oxidation, SR CaВІвҒә overload, SOICR вҶ’ DADs/EADs |
| Structural Remodeling | AngII/AT1R/ACE, TGF-ОІ1/TGFОІR/SMAD2/3, myofibroblast, collagen I/III, MMP/TIMP, LAA enlargement, atrial fibrosis |
| Inflammation & ROS | NLRP3/caspase-1/IL-1ОІ, NF-ОәB, NOX2/mitochondrial ROS, superoxide/peroxynitrite, eNOS uncoupling, CRP |
| Autonomic NS | ОІ1AR/cAMP/PKA, M2R/IKACh, ganglionated plexi, NE/ACh, sympatho-vagal remodeling |
| Thromboembolism | LAA stasis, TF/FVIIa/FXa/thrombin/fibrin cascade, platelet activation, protein C/AT-III, stroke |
| Drug PK | Amiodarone (3-cmt, tВҪ ~40-55d, fat depot V2=4200L), Apixaban (2-cmt, tВҪ 12h), Metoprolol (2-cmt, tВҪ 3.5h), Flecainide, Rivaroxaban, Dabigatran, Warfarin, Digoxin |
| Drug PD | Class IвҖ“IV antiarrhythmics, IKur/IKACh blockade (atrial-selective), FXa/FIIa/VKA inhibition, ERP prolongation, QTc monitoring |
| Clinical Endpoints | AF burden (%), ERP (ms), QTc (ms), HR (bpm), NT-proBNP, CRP, LA diameter, stroke risk (%/year), fibrosis score |

**Drug PK/PD (Treatment Landscape)**

| Drug Class | Agent | Mechanism | Key Trial / Calibration |
|-----------|-------|-----------|------------------------|
| Class III Antiarrhythmic | Amiodarone 200mg/day (after loading) | IKr + ICaL + INa + IKACh block вҶ’ ERPвҶ‘ + rate вҶ“ | Roy et al. NEJM 2000; AFFIRM arm |
| Class II (Rate Control) | Metoprolol 50mg BID | ОІ1AR blockade вҶ’ HRвҶ“ | AFFIRM (NEJM 2002; PMID:12466506); RACE (NEJM 2002; PMID:12466507) |
| Direct FXa Inhibitor | Apixaban 5mg BID | Competitive FXa inhibition вҶ’ вҶ“thrombin generation | ARISTOTLE (NEJM 2011; PMID:21870978); RRR 21% vs warfarin |
| Direct Thrombin Inhibitor | Dabigatran 150mg BID | Direct FIIa inhibition | RE-LY (NEJM 2009; PMID:19717844) |
| Direct FXa Inhibitor | Rivaroxaban 20mg QD | Competitive FXa inhibition | ROCKET-AF (NEJM 2011; PMID:21830957) |
| Vitamin K Antagonist | Warfarin (INR 2вҖ“3) | VKORC1 inhibition вҶ’ вҶ“F II/VII/IX/X synthesis | AVERROES (NEJM 2011; PMID:21309657) |
| Early Rhythm Control | Multiple agents | Earlier sinus rhythm вҶ’ structural prevention | EAST-AFNET 4 (NEJM 2020; PMID:32865375) |

### Myasthenia Gravis (MG)

**мӨ‘мҰқ к·јл¬ҙл ҘмҰқ** | Autoimmune / Neuromuscular Junction

**Mechanistic Map**

[![MG QSP Map](myasthenia-gravis/mg_qsp_model.png)](myasthenia-gravis/mg_qsp_model.svg)

*Click image to open interactive SVG. 16 pathway clusters: Thymus & Immune Priming В· B Cell & Plasma Cells В· Autoantibody (AChR/MuSK/LRP4) В· FcRn-IgG Homeostasis В· NMJ Structure В· ACh Neurotransmission В· Complement Cascade В· NMJ Damage В· Pyridostigmine PK/PD В· Corticosteroid/IS PK В· Biologic Drug PK В· Drug PD on Immune System В· Non-drug Interventions (PLEX/IVIG/Thymectomy) В· Muscle Physiology В· Clinical Endpoints В· Biomarker Panel*

**Key Pathways Modeled**

| Cluster | Key Nodes |
|---------|-----------|
| Thymus & Immune Priming | Thymoma, Thymic Hyperplasia, Myoid Cells (AChR+), Thymic DC, AIRE dysfunction, Naive T, Tfh (CXCR5+), Th1/Th17, Treg failure, Thymic GC reaction, HLA-DR3 |
| B Cell & Plasma Cells | Naive B, GC-B (affinity maturation/CSR), Memory B, SL-PC, LL-PC (BM niche), CD20+ B (Rituximab target), BCR specificity, CD40L-CD40, IL-21 signaling |
| Autoantibodies | Anti-AChR IgG (~85%, IgG1/3), Anti-MuSK IgG (~5-8%, IgG4), Anti-LRP4 (~1-3%), Titin/RyR Ab, IGG pool, NMJ-bound Ab |
| FcRn & IgG Homeostasis | FcRn (FCGRT/ОІ2m), endosome pH cycling, IgG recycling vs lysosomal degradation; Efgartigimod + Rozanolixizumab block FcRn вҶ’ 75% IgG reduction |
| NMJ Structure | Оұ-motor neuron, axon terminal, presynaptic/postsynaptic membranes, junctional folds, AChR clusters (~10^7/NMJ, Оө-subunit adult), MuSK, LRP4, Agrin, Rapsyn, ColQ, Dystrophin complex |
| ACh Neurotransmission | CHT1/choline uptake, ChAT, VAChT, synaptic vesicles, Nav1.6 AP, VGCC (P/Q-type Cav2.1), SNARE complex, exocytosis, ACh-AChR binding (2 sites, Оұ-subunit), AChE hydrolysis (kcat~1.4Г—10вҒҙ/s); Pyridostigmine reversible carbamylation |
| Classical Complement | C1q recognition вҶ’ C1r/C1s вҶ’ C4b/C2a (C3 convertase) вҶ’ C3a/C3b вҶ’ C5 convertase вҶ’ C5 cleavage (eculizumab/ravulizumab/zilucoplan target) вҶ’ C5a (inflammation) + C5b вҶ’ C6-C9 вҶ’ MAC (C5b-9) вҶ’ NMJ pore |
| NMJ Damage | Ab crosslinking вҶ’ AChR internalization, complement MAC вҶ’ junctional fold destruction, ACh binding blockade (MuSK-Ab), AChR density вҶ“, NMJ safety factor вҶ“ (normal 3-5Г—), EPP amplitude вҶ“ вҶ’ subthreshold вҶ’ muscle AP failure вҶ’ fatigable weakness |
| Drug PK | Pyridostigmine (1-cmt oral, F~18%, Vd=1.3L/kg, ke=0.37/h); Prednisolone (2-cmt, F=82%, CL=0.3L/h/kg, CYP3A4); AZAвҶ’6-MPвҶ’6-TGN (TPMT/HGPRT, tВҪ(TGN)~5d); Eculizumab (2-cmt IV, Vss=7.7L, tВҪ=11d); Efgartigimod (2-cmt + FcRn binding, CL=0.15L/h) |
| Non-drug Interventions | Plasmapheresis (PLEX): acute IgG removal (days); IVIG: FcRn saturation вҶ’ вҶ“IgG tВҪ; Thymectomy: removes intrathymic GC source (MGTX: +5-year CSR benefit) |
| Muscle EC Coupling | Nicotinic ion channel opening вҶ’ muscle AP (Nav1.4) вҶ’ DHPR (T-tubule) вҶ’ RyR1 (SR CaВІвҒә release) вҶ’ Troponin-C вҶ’ Tropomyosin shift вҶ’ Myosin-Actin crossbridge вҶ’ Contraction; SERCA CaВІвҒә reuptake |
| Clinical Endpoints | QMG (0-39), MG-ADL (0-24), MGAS, MGFA class I-V, Myasthenic Crisis (FVC<50%), Ptosis, Diplopia, Dysphagia, Dysarthria, Respiratory failure; CSR, MMS |
| Biomarkers | Anti-AChR titer (nmol/L, RIA), Anti-MuSK (CBA/ELISA), Total IgG, SFEMG jitter (Вөs), RNS decrement (>10%), sC5b-9, Blood Tfh %, CH50, Thymus CT |

**Drug PK/PD Summary**

| Drug | Class | Mechanism | Calibration Trial |
|------|-------|-----------|-------------------|
| Pyridostigmine 60mg q6h | AChEI (symptomatic) | Reversible AChE carbamylation вҶ’ вҶ‘cleft ACh вҶ’ вҶ‘NMJ safety factor | Huang et al. 2017 (PopPK); Breyer-Pfaff 1990 |
| Prednisolone 0.5вҖ“1.5mg/kg/d | Corticosteroid | GR nuclear вҶ’ вҶ“NF-ОәB/IL-2/IL-17 вҶ’ вҶ“Tfh/GC-B/SLPC | Palace et al. Neurology 1998 |
| Azathioprine 2вҖ“3mg/kg/d | Antimetabolite (IMPDH/DNA) | 6-TGN вҶ’ IMPDH inhibition + DNA incorporation вҶ’ вҶ“lymphocyte proliferation | TPMT pharmacogenomics |
| Eculizumab 900mg q2w IV | Anti-C5 (complement) | Blocks C5 cleavage вҶ’ вҶ“C5a + вҶ“MAC вҶ’ NMJ protection | REGAIN (Howard et al. Lancet Neurol 2017; вҲ’4.2 QMG vs placebo) |
| Ravulizumab 3000mg q8w IV | Anti-C5 (long-acting) | Same as eculizumab; recycled by FcRn вҶ’ tВҪ~49d | CHAMPION-MG (Vu et al. NEJM Evid 2022) |
| Zilucoplan 0.3mg/kg SC qd | Anti-C5 (peptide) | Subcutaneous C5 inhibitor; rapid onset | RAISE (Howard et al. JAMA Neurol 2023) |
| Efgartigimod 10mg/kg IV qw | Anti-FcRn | Competes for FcRn вҶ’ вҶ“IgG recycling вҶ’ ~75% total IgG вҶ“ in 4 wk | ADAPT (Howard et al. Lancet Neurol 2021) |
| Rozanolixizumab 1mg/kg SC qw | Anti-FcRn (mAb) | FcRn blockade вҶ’ IgG catabolism вҶ‘ | MycarinG (Bril et al. Lancet Neurol 2023) |
| Rituximab 375mg/mВІ IV Г—4 | Anti-CD20 | ADCC + CDC + apoptosis вҶ’ B cell depletion; esp. effective in MuSK-MG | Tandan et al. Muscle Nerve 2017 (systematic review) |
| Thymectomy (VATS/robot) | Surgery | Removes intrathymic GC; long-term вҶ“SL-PC/LL-PC source | MGTX (Wolfe et al. NEJM 2016): QMG вҲ’2.85, CSRвҶ‘ at 5yr |

**ODE Model Summary** (20 compartments)

| State Group | Variables |
|-------------|-----------|
| Pyridostigmine PK (2) | GUT\_PYR, CENT\_PYR вҶ’ C\_PYR вҶ’ AChE\_INH (Emax, EC50=50ng/mL, Оі=1.5) |
| Prednisolone PK (3) | GUT\_PRED, CENT\_PRED, PERIPH\_PRED вҶ’ GR activation вҶ’ immunosuppression |
| Azathioprine/6-TGN (3) | GUT\_AZA вҶ’ SIXMP (TPMT/HGPRT) вҶ’ SIXTGN (tВҪ~5d) вҶ’ IMPDH inh |
| Eculizumab PK (2) | CENT\_ECUL, PERIPH\_ECUL вҶ’ C5 inhibition (EMAX=0.99, EC50=100ng/mL) |
| Efgartigimod PK (2) | CENT\_EFGAR (free) + FCRN\_EFGAR (bound) вҶ’ FcRn occupancy вҶ’ вҶ‘IgG degradation |
| Immune compartment (4) | TFH, GCB (logistic growth Г— Tfh), SLPC (tВҪ~17h), LLPC (tВҪ years) вҶ’ suppressed by GR/6-TGN |
| AChR-Ab pool (1) | ACHR\_AB\_C: secreted by SL+LL PC, degraded via FcRn (K\_AB\_EFF = f[FcRn\_OCC]) |
| NMJ AChR density (1) | ACHR\_DEN: synthesized (K\_ACHR\_IN) вҲ’ degraded (K\_ACHR\_D) вҲ’ Ab-mediated downregulation |
| Complement activity (1) | COMP\_ACT: driven by ACHR\_AB\_C, decays, inhibited by eculizumab |
| NMJ Safety Factor (1) | NMJ\_SF = f(AChR\_DEN Г— 0.8 + ACh\_Avail Г— 0.2) вҶ’ drives QMG/MG-ADL |

**Treatment Scenarios (7)**

| Scenario | Regimen | QMG at 52wk | AChR-Ab | NMJ Safety Factor |
|----------|---------|:-----------:|:-------:|:-----------------:|
| S1 | Natural history (untreated) | ~30 (severe) | High (вҶ‘) | <0.5 (severelyвҶ“) |
| S2 | Pyridostigmine 60mg q6h | ~22 (moderate) | Unchanged | ~0.85 (вҶ‘AChE inh) |

| S6 | Efgartigimod + Pyridostigmine | ~8 (mild) | ~75% вҶ“ | ~0.92 |
| S7 | Rituximab + Pyridostigmine | ~9 (mild) | GCB/SL-PC вҶ“вҶ“ | ~0.88 |

## Primary Biliary Cholangitis (PBC)

**Date added:** 2026-06-17 | **Directory:** [`primary-biliary-cholangitis/`](primary-biliary-cholangitis/)

[![PBC Mechanistic Map](primary-biliary-cholangitis/pbc_qsp_model.png)](primary-biliary-cholangitis/pbc_qsp_model.svg)

### Disease Overview

Primary Biliary Cholangitis (PBC) is a chronic, autoimmune, cholestatic liver disease characterized by progressive destruction of small intrahepatic bile ducts. It predominantly affects women (9:1 F:M ratio) and is hallmarked by anti-mitochondrial antibodies (AMA вүҘ1:40; вүҘ95% sensitivity) directed against the pyruvate dehydrogenase complex E2 subunit (PDC-E2). Without treatment, PBC progresses from bile duct inflammation (florid duct lesion) through ductopenia to biliary fibrosis, cirrhosis, and liver failure requiring transplantation.

### Key Pathophysiological Cascade

```
Genetic susceptibility (HLA-DRB1, IL12A/IL12RB2, STAT4)
+ Environmental triggers (xenobiotics, infection/molecular mimicry)
         вҶ“
pDC вҶ’ TLR7/9 вҶ’ IFN-Оұ вҶ’ Type I IFN signaling
         вҶ“
CD4+ Th1 вҶ’ IFN-Оі В· CD8+ CTL вҶ’ Perforin/Granzyme B
         вҶ“
BEC apoptosis (FasL/TRAIL/CTL) + Impaired GSH secretion вҶ’ PDC-E2 apotope
         вҶ“
AMA (IgM вҶ’ IgG class switch) В· BEC senescence вҶ’ SASP
         вҶ“
Ductopenia (vanishing bile duct syndrome) вҶ’ ALPвҶ‘вҶ‘
         вҶ“
Cholestasis: Hydrophobic BA poolвҶ‘ вҶ’ NLRP3/IL-1ОІ вҶ’ Hepatocyte damage
         вҶ“
TGF-ОІ1 / HSC activation вҶ’ Collagen I/III вҶ’ Fibrosis (Metavir F0вҶ’F4)
         вҶ“
Portal hypertension В· Cirrhosis В· HCC (>15Г— risk)
```

### Drug Mechanisms Modeled

| Drug | Target | Mechanism | Key Trial | ALP Response |
|------|--------|-----------|-----------|:------------:|
| **UDCA** 13-15 mg/kg/d | FXR (partial) / BSEP / AE2 | Enriches hydrophilic BA pool; bicarbonate umbrella; BSEP/MRP2 induction; hepatoprotection | Lindor 1994, NEJM | 30-40% вҶ“ |
| **Obeticholic acid (OCA)** 5-10 mg/d | FXR agonist (100Г— vs UDCA) | FXR вҶ’ FGF19вҶ‘ вҶ’ CYP7A1вҶ“; BSEPвҶ‘ вҶ’ BA exportвҶ‘; ASBTвҶ“ вҶ’ BA reabsorptionвҶ“ | POISE (Nevens 2016, NEJM) | 38% вҶ“ |
| **Elafibranor** 80 mg/d | PPARОұ/Оҙ dual agonist | BA detoxification (UGT1A3вҶ‘ glucuronidation; SULT2A1вҶ‘ sulfation; CYP4A11вҶ‘ Пү-oxidation); anti-inflammatory; ABCG5/8вҶ‘ | ELATIVE (Kowdley 2024, Lancet) вҖ” **FDA Jun 2024** | **51% ALP normalization** |
| **Seladelpar** 10 mg/d | PPARОҙ selective | BA sulfationвҶ‘; GGTвҶ“; pruritusвҶ“ (autotaxinвҶ“); HMGCRвҶ“ | RESPONSE (Bowlus 2024, Lancet) вҖ” **FDA Aug 2024** | **25% ALP normalization** |
| **Bezafibrate** 400 mg/d | pan-PPAR (Оұ>Оҙ>Оі) | Broad BA detoxification; anti-fibrotic | BEZURSO (Corpechot 2018, NEJM) | **67% ALP normalization** |

### Clinical Endpoints

| Endpoint | Definition | Clinical Significance |
|----------|-----------|----------------------|
| ALP response | ALP <1.67Г—ULN + Bilirubin вүӨULN at 12m | Primary endpoint POISE; GLOBE-derived threshold |
| ALP normalization | ALP вүӨULN | Primary endpoint ELATIVE/RESPONSE |
| Paris II criteria | ALP <1.5Г—ULN + AST вүӨ2Г—ULN + Bilirubin вүӨULN | Best validated biochemical surrogate |
| GLOBE score | 5-year transplant-free survival | Validated in 4,800 patients |
| UK-PBC score | 5/10-year liver-related mortality | Complementary to GLOBE |
| Pruritus NRS | 0-10 numeric rating scale | Key symptom endpoint; OCA limits |

### ODE Model Architecture (20 states)

| State Group | Variables | Biological Meaning |
|-------------|-----------|-------------------|
| Drug PK (10) | UDCA/OCA/ELF/SEL/BEZ (gut + central) | 1-compartment with EHC for UDCA |
| Immunology (3) | AMA, Th1, BEC_dmg | Core disease drivers |
| Bile acid axis (2) | BA_toxic, FGF19 | FXR-FGF19-CYP7A1 feedback loop |
| Biomarkers (4) | ALP, BILI, GGT, IgM | Primary clinical endpoints |
| Disease state (1) | Fibrosis (Metavir 0-4) | Long-term progression |

### Treatment Scenarios (7)

| Scenario | Regimen | ALP at M12 | ALP Normalization | Pruritus Effect |
|----------|---------|:----------:|:-----------------:|:---------------:|
| S1 | No treatment | ~3.5Г—ULN | 0% | Moderate |
| S2 | UDCA monotherapy | ~2.1Г—ULN | ~15% | Mild benefit |
| S3 | UDCA + OCA 5mg | ~1.5Г—ULN | ~30% | Worsened (dose-limiting) |
| S4 | UDCA + OCA 10mg | ~1.3Г—ULN | ~38% | Severely worsened |
| S5 | UDCA + Elafibranor 80mg | ~1.1Г—ULN | **~51%** | Improved |
| S6 | UDCA + Seladelpar 10mg | ~1.4Г—ULN | **~25%** | Improved |
| S7 | UDCA + Bezafibrate 400mg | ~1.0Г—ULN | **~55%** | Neutral |

### Shiny Dashboard (6 Interactive Tabs)

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| в‘  Patient Profile | Baseline ALP/Bilirubin/GGT/fibrosis stage; disease overview; drug information table; 4 KPI value boxes |
| в‘Ў PK Profiles | 72h drug concentration profiles (all 5 drugs); steady-state Css and PD parameter summary table |
| в‘ў PD Biomarkers | ALP/Bilirubin/GGT (all Г—ULN); IgM; FGF19 induction by OCA; Pruritus NRS (with OCA warning) |
| в‘Ј Disease Biology | AMA titer; Th1 cell activity; BEC damage index (0-1); Toxic BA pool; Metavir fibrosis score |
| в‘Ө Clinical Endpoints | Paris II response; ALP normalization flag; GLOBE surrogate score; 12-month summary table |
| в‘Ҙ Scenario Comparison | 7-scenario ALP/fibrosis/pruritus comparison plots; month-12 results DataTable |
