## Hypertrophic Cardiomyopathy (HCM)

> **Category:** л§Ңм„ұм§Ҳнҷҳ / мӢ¬нҳҲкҙҖ В· Chronic Disease / Cardiovascular
> **Directory:** [`hypertrophic-cardiomyopathy/`](hypertrophic-cardiomyopathy/)
> **Date added:** 2026-06-17

### Disease Overview

Hypertrophic cardiomyopathy (HCM) is the most prevalent inherited cardiac disease (~1:500 globally), caused primarily by pathogenic variants in sarcomere protein genes вҖ” most commonly **MYH7** (ОІ-myosin heavy chain) and **MYBPC3** (cardiac myosin-binding protein C), together accounting for ~80% of genotype-positive cases. The hallmark pathology is unexplained left ventricular hypertrophy with non-dilated ventricle, typically asymmetric septal hypertrophy (ASH).

### Mechanistic Map

[![HCM QSP Model](hypertrophic-cardiomyopathy/hcm_qsp_model.png)](hypertrophic-cardiomyopathy/hcm_qsp_model.svg)

*Click image to open the full-resolution SVG. 200+ nodes, 12 subgraph clusters.*

### Pathophysiology Summary

```
Sarcomere Gene Mutations (MYH7/MYBPC3/TNNT2/TNNI3/TPM1/MYL2)
         вҶ“
вҶ“ SRX fraction (MYBPC3 stabilizes SRX) + вҶ‘ DRX fraction
         вҶ“
вҶ‘ Duty Ratio (myosin heads in power stroke)
    вҶ’ Hypercontractility вҶ’ Venturi effect вҶ’ SAM вҶ’ LVOT obstruction
    вҶ’ вҶ‘ ATP hydrolysis / MVOвӮӮ вҶ’ Microvascular ischemia
         вҶ“
Calcineurin-NFAT + CaMKII/HDAC4/MEF2 + ERK1/2 (mechano-signaling)
         вҶ“
Fetal gene reactivation вҶ’ Asymmetric LVH (IVSвҶ‘вҶ‘, LV massвҶ‘)
         вҶ“
TGF-ОІ1/SMAD2/3 вҶ’ FibroblastвҶ’Myofibroblast вҶ’ Collagen I/IIIвҶ‘
         вҶ“
Interstitial fibrosis (ECVвҶ‘) + Replacement fibrosis (LGE+)
         вҶ“
вҶ“ LV compliance вҶ’ LVEDPвҶ‘ вҶ’ LA pressureвҶ‘ вҶ’ AF (25вҖ“30% lifetime)
         вҶ“
RyR2 diastolic leak (DADs) + Myocyte disarray (reentry) + Scar substrate
         вҶ“
VT вҶ’ VF вҶ’ Sudden Cardiac Death (SCD, 0.5вҖ“1%/yr; вүҘ6% 5-yr = ICD)
```

### Drug Mechanisms Modeled

| Drug | Class | Mechanism | Key Trial | Primary Effect |
|------|-------|-----------|-----------|:-------------:|
| **Mavacamten** 2.5вҖ“15 mg QD | Cardiac myosin inhibitor | Shifts myosin from DRX вҶ’ SRX state (stabilizes super-relaxed); вҶ“ duty ratio; вҶ“ ATPase activity; CYP2C19-metabolized | EXPLORER-HCM (NEJM 2020) | LVOT вҶ“36 mmHg |
| **Aficamten** | Next-gen cardiac myosin inhibitor | Competitive cardiac myosin ATPase inhibitor; shorter tВҪ (~7h vs 6вҖ“9d); more titratable | SEQUOIA-HCM (Lancet 2024) | LVOT вҶ“36 mmHg |
| **Metoprolol / Bisoprolol** | ОІвӮҒ-Blocker | вҶ“ HR вҶ’ вҶ“ dynamic LVOT obstruction + вҶ“ contractility; вҶ“ CaВІвҒә leak (PKA/PLB pathway) | Empirical use (no RCT) | HRвҶ“, symptomвҶ“ |
| **Verapamil** | Non-DHP CCB | ICaL blockade вҶ’ HRвҶ“ + contractilityвҶ“ + LVOT gradientвҶ“ | Small RCTs | SymptomвҶ“ |
| **Disopyramide** | Class Ia antiarrhythmic | NaвҒә channel blockade вҶ’ вҶ“ SAM вҶ’ вҶ“ LVOT gradient; negative inotrope | Sherrid 2005 (JACC) | LVOT вҶ“40% |
| **Furosemide/Torsemide** | Loop diuretic | Volume reduction вҶ’ вҶ“ LVEDP вҶ’ вҶ“ LA pressure вҶ’ вҶ“ congestion | Supportive | SymptomвҶ“ |
| **Surgical Myectomy / ASA** | Septal Reduction Therapy (SRT) | Direct removal/ablation of obstructing septum вҶ’ LVOTвҶ“вҶ“вҶ“ | Ommen 2005 (JACC) | LVOT вҶ“вҶ“вҶ“ |
| **NOAC / Warfarin** | Anticoagulation | Thrombin/FXa inhibition вҶ’ stroke prevention in AF | ARISTOTLE, RE-LY | Stroke riskвҶ“ |

### ODE Model Architecture (18 State Variables)

| Compartment Group | Variables | Biology |
|-------------------|-----------|---------|
| Mavacamten PK (3) | A_gut_m, A_c_m, A_p_m | 3-compartment PK; CYP2C19 EM/PM/UM adjustment |
| Beta-blocker PK (1) | A_bb | 1-compartment; metoprolol equivalents |
| Calcium dynamics (2) | Ca_cyt, Ca_SR | Cytosolic CaВІвҒә (nM); SR CaВІвҒә load (ОјM) |
| Signaling (3) | Calcineurin, NFAT_nuc, ERK_act | Calcineurin-NFAT hypertrophy axis; ERK1/2 stress |
| Structural remodeling (4) | IVS, LVmass_rel, TGFb1, Collagen | IVS (mm); LV mass (relative); fibrosis drivers |
| Hemodynamics (3) | LVOT, LVEDP, HR_state | Key clinical hemodynamic endpoints |
| Biomarkers (2) | NT_proBNP, TroponinI | Wall stress biomarker; myocardial injury |
| AF risk (1) | AF_hazard | Cumulative AF incidence hazard |

### Treatment Scenarios (7)

| Scenario | Regimen | Key Effect at 52 Weeks |
|----------|---------|------------------------|
| S1 | Untreated HCM | Progressive LVOTвҶ‘, NT-proBNPвҶ‘, IVSвҶ‘ |
| S2 | Mavacamten 5 mg QD (CYP2C19 EM) | LVOT вҶ“~18 mmHg, NT-proBNP вҶ“~35%, NYHA improved |
| S3 | Mavacamten 10 mg QD (EM) | LVOT вҶ“~26 mmHg, NT-proBNP вҶ“~50% |
| S4 | Mavacamten 2.5 mg QD (CYP2C19 PM) | Similar exposure to 10mg EM (вҶ‘exposure due to вҶ“CL) |
| S5 | Beta-blocker 200 mg QD (metoprolol) | HRвҶ“~28%, LVOT вҶ“~12 mmHg (rate-dependent) |
| S6 | Mavacamten 5 mg + BB 100 mg | Additive: LVOT вҶ“~22 mmHg, HRвҶ“, symptom improvement |
| S7 | Post-SRT (Myectomy, IVS reset=11mm) | LVOT normalises (<10 mmHg), long-term fibrosis persists |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| в‘  Patient Profile | Patient demographics, genotype, HCM phenotype, baseline hemodynamic parameters; mechanistic map thumbnail |
| в‘Ў Drug PK | Mavacamten/BB plasma concentration-time curves; CYP2C19 genotype comparison (EM/PM/UM); PD effect (duty ratio suppression) |
| в‘ў Cardiac Mechanics | LVOT gradient, LVEDP, LVEF, cardiac output, HR вҖ” all over simulation period; 4 real-time value boxes |
| в‘Ј Hypertrophy & Fibrosis | IVS thickness, collagen content, TGF-ОІ1, NFAT nuclear fraction, estimated CMR ECV (%) |
| в‘Ө Clinical Endpoints | NT-proBNP, Troponin I, NYHA class, peak VOвӮӮ; monthly results datatable |
| в‘Ҙ Scenario Comparison | 7-scenario head-to-head comparison; primary outcome selector; 52-week summary table |
| в‘Ұ Risk Assessment | HCM Risk-SCD calculator (O'Mahony 2014 formula); AF cumulative hazard; ICD indication tracker; risk factor contribution chart |

## Graves' Disease

> **Directory:** [`graves-disease/`](graves-disease/)

**ICD-10:** E05.0 В· **Category:** Autoimmune Endocrine Disease В· **Prevalence:** ~0.5% (F:M = 7вҖ“10:1)

### Pathophysiology

Graves' disease is the most common cause of hyperthyroidism (~80% of cases). Thyroid-stimulating autoantibodies (TSAb) bind and constitutively activate the TSH receptor (TSHR) on thyroid follicular cells, bypassing normal HPT axis regulation.

| Module | Key Components |
|--------|---------------|
| **HPT Axis** | Hypothalamus вҶ’ TRH вҶ’ Pituitary вҶ’ TSH; dual T4/T3 Hill-kinetics negative feedback; circadian pulsatility; TSH suppression by high fT4/fT3 |
| **Autoimmune Pathogenesis** | CD4+/CD8+ T cells; Th1/Th2/Th17/Treg polarization; B-cell germinal center reaction; plasma cells вҶ’ TSAb (stimulating) / TBAb (blocking) / TBII; CTLA-4/HLA-DR3 genetic risk; CD40вҖ“CD40L costimulation |
| **Thyroid Follicular Cell** | TSHR/Gs-Оұ/cAMP/PKA/CREB signaling; NIS-mediated iodide uptake; DUOX2/HвӮӮOвӮӮ; TPO organification; MIT+DIT coupling вҶ’ T3/T4 synthesis; colloid storage; WolffвҖ“Chaikoff effect + escape; goiter (VEGF/bFGF) |
| **Hormone PK/PD** | TBG/albumin/transthyretin binding; D1 (T4вҶ’T3 ~60%), D2 (local brain T3), D3 (T4вҶ’rT3 inactivation); TR-Оұ/TR-ОІ nuclear signaling; enterohepatic recirculation (~20%) |
| **Drug PK** | MMI (F=93%, tВҪ=4-6h, high thyroid concentration); PTU (F=75%, tВҪ=1-2h, 75% protein-bound); В№ВіВ№I (FвүҲ100%, NIS-mediated thyroid uptake ~60-80%); Propranolol (F=26%, first-pass, tВҪ=4h); LT4 replacement |
| **Drug PD** | MMI вҶ’ irreversible TPO inhibition + immunosuppression (TRAbвҶ“); PTU вҶ’ TPO + D1 inhibition; В№ВіВ№I вҶ’ ОІ-radiation thyroid cell death вҶ’ atrophy вҶ’ hypothyroidism; Propranolol вҶ’ ОІвӮҒ-blocker (HRвҶ“) + D1 inhibition; Rituximab вҶ’ anti-CD20 B-cell depletion вҶ’ TRAbвҶ“ (delayed); Teprotumumab вҶ’ IGF-1R blockade вҶ’ GOвҶ“ |
| **Graves' Ophthalmopathy** | TSHR+IGF-1R on orbital fibroblasts; TRAb activation вҶ’ HAS1/HAS2 (hyaluronanвҶ‘) + PPAR-Оі adipogenesis; orbital inflammation (TNF-Оұ/IL-6/Th1); EOM fibrosis вҶ’ proptosis + diplopia; CAS score; optic nerve compression |
| **Target Organ Effects** | Cardiovascular: tachycardia (HRвҶ‘20-40 bpm), AF risk (5-15%), вҶ‘cardiac output, вҶ“SVR; Bone: osteoclastвҶ‘ вҶ’ BMD loss (cortical > trabecular) вҶ’ fracture riskвҶ‘; CNS: anxiety/tremor/insomnia/hyperreflexia; Metabolic: BMRвҶ‘20-60%, weight loss, heat intolerance |
| **Clinical Endpoints** | TSH (suppressed <0.01), fT4вҶ‘, fT3вҶ‘, TRAb (>1.75 IU/L diagnostic), RAIUвҶ‘; Burch-Wartofsky score (thyroid storm); CAS score (GO); Hertel exophthalmometry; BMD Z-score |

### Model Specifications

| Feature | Detail |
|---------|--------|
| ODE Compartments | **18** (HPT axis + thyroid mass + T4/T3/fT4/fT3/rT3 pools + TRAb + B cells + bone resorption + heart rate + GO score + TPO inhibition) |
| Treatment Scenarios | **6**: Untreated В· MMI 30mg/day В· Radioiodine 15 mCi В· MMI+Propranolol В· Block-and-Replace (MMI+LT4) В· Rituximab+MMI |
| Virtual Population | n=200 with lognormal TRAbвӮҖ and ICвӮ…вӮҖ_MMI variability |
| Calibration | MMI PK: Walter 2012 (J Clin Pharmacol); TRAb dynamics: Eisenberg 2008; HPT feedback: Leow 2007 |
| Key Trials | CATS trial (MMI vs PTU safety); MINGO trial (rituximab+MP vs MP); OPTIC trial (teprotumumab) |

### Key Equations

```
TSHR_act  = E_TSH Г— TSH/(EC50_TSH + TSH) + E_TRAb Г— TRAb/(EC50_TRAb + TRAb)
T4_synth  = ksyn_T4 Г— ThyMass Г— TSHR_act Г— (1 вҲ’ TPO_inh)
TSH_prod  = ksyn_TSH / mean[(fT4/fT4_norm)^n, (fT3/fT3_norm)^n]
dTRAb/dt  = kprod_TRAb Г— Bcell вҲ’ kel_TRAb Г— TRAb
dGO/dt    = kGO_TRAb Г— TRAb Г— (1 вҲ’ GCS) вҲ’ kGO_kel Г— GO
```

| File | Description |
|------|-------------|
| [`gd_qsp_model.dot`](graves-disease/gd_qsp_model.dot) | Graphviz DOT source (9 clusters: HPT axis В· autoimmune В· thyroid follicular cell В· hormone PK В· drug PK В· drug PD В· ophthalmopathy В· target organs В· clinical endpoints) |
| [`gd_qsp_model.svg`](graves-disease/gd_qsp_model.svg) | Vector mechanistic map |
| [`gd_qsp_model.png`](graves-disease/gd_qsp_model.png) | Raster mechanistic map (150 dpi) |
| [`gd_references.md`](graves-disease/gd_references.md) | 43 curated references (10 sections); Morshed 2015 (Endocr Rev) В· Smith 2016 (NEJM) В· Douglas 2020 (NEJM teprotumumab) В· Ross 2016 (ATA guidelines) |
| [`gd_mrgsolve_model.R`](graves-disease/gd_mrgsolve_model.R) | 18-state mrgsolve ODE; 6 treatment scenarios; VPop n=200; sensitivity analysis; calibrated to Walter 2012 / Eisenberg 2008 |
| [`gd_shiny_app.R`](graves-disease/gd_shiny_app.R) | 6-tab shinydashboard: Patient Profile В· Drug PK В· Thyroid Hormone PD В· Cardiovascular & Bone В· Immune & Ophthalmopathy В· Scenario Comparison |

## Idiopathic Pulmonary Fibrosis (IPF)

> **Directory:** [`idiopathic-pulmonary-fibrosis/`](idiopathic-pulmonary-fibrosis/)

**ICD-10:** J84.112 В· **Category:** л§Ңм„ұм§Ҳнҷҳ / нҳёнқЎкё° м„¬мң нҷ” В· **Prevalence:** 13вҖ“20 per 100,000; incidence rising with age (peak 60вҖ“70 yrs)

### Pathophysiology

Idiopathic pulmonary fibrosis is a progressive, irreversible, and fatal fibrotic interstitial lung disease characterized by the **usual interstitial pneumonia (UIP)** histological pattern. The prevailing hypothesis centers on **repetitive alveolar epithelial injury** followed by aberrant wound healing driven by TGF-ОІ1.

[![IPF QSP Model](idiopathic-pulmonary-fibrosis/ipf_qsp_model.png)](idiopathic-pulmonary-fibrosis/ipf_qsp_model.svg)

| Module | Key Components |
|--------|---------------|
| **Alveolar Epithelium (AEC I/II)** | AEC-II injury/senescence (ROS, ER stress, telomere shortening, MUC5B variant, TERT/SFTPC mutations) вҶ’ DAMP release вҶ’ ОұvОІ6 integrin + TSP-1 activate latent TGF-ОІ1; KL-6 and SP-D biomarkers; Wnt/ОІ-catenin blocks AEC-II repair; EGF/HGF support regeneration (reduced in IPF) |
| **TGF-ОІ1/SMAD Signaling** | TGFОІ1 (central driver): TGFОІRI/II вҶ’ pSMAD2/3 вҶ’ SMAD4 nuclear complex вҶ’ CTGF/PAI-1/fibronectin/Col1A1/TIMP-1 transcription; SMAD7 (negative feedback); non-SMAD (PI3K/AKT/MAPK/Rho) вҶ’ fibroblast proliferation/migration; LOX (collagen crosslinking) вҶ’ matrix stiffness вҶ’ mechanotransduction вҶ’ more TGF-ОІ |
| **Macrophage Biology** | DAMP вҶ’ TLR4/TLR9 вҶ’ NLRP3 inflammasome вҶ’ IL-1ОІ/IL-18; AM вҶ’ M1 (TNF-Оұ/IL-6/MMP-12) or M2 (IL-4/IL-13/IL-10) polarization; M2 вҶ’ TGF-ОІ1/CTGF/osteopontin; CCL-18 as M2 biomarker |
| **Fibroblast/Myofibroblast** | Quiescent вҶ’ activated (TGF-ОІ/PDGF) вҶ’ myofibroblast (Оұ-SMA+); IPF fibroblasts epigenetically reprogrammed (bcl-2вҶ‘, apoptosis-resistant); YAP/TAZ/FAK/Rho-ROCK; CXCL12/SDF-1 recruits circulating fibrocytes (CD45+/Collagen+); senescent fibroblasts (SASP) amplify TGF-ОІ |
| **ECM Remodeling** | Collagen I/III overproduction; MMP-1/-2/-7/-9/-13 (degradation) vs TIMP-1/-2 (inhibition) вҖ” TGF-ОІ tips balance toward TIMPвҶ‘ вҶ’ fibrosis; MMP-7 serum biomarker; periostin stabilizes collagen; HA activates TLR4; matrix stiffness вҶ’ YAP/TAZ mechanotransduction feedback loop |
| **Growth Factors & Angiogenesis** | PDGF-AA/BB вҶ’ PDGFRОұ/ОІ вҶ’ fibroblast proliferation; FGF-2 вҶ’ FGFR1/2 вҶ’ fibroblast survival; VEGF-A вҶ’ VEGFR2 вҶ’ abnormal neovascularization; ET-1 вҶ’ ETA/ETB вҶ’ myofibroblast differentiation; platelet activation вҶ’ TGF-ОІ release |
| **Oxidative Stress** | NOX4 (TGF-ОІ-induced) + mitochondrial ROS вҶ’ AEC-II damage + TGF-ОІ activation; Nrf2/GSH/SOD defense; mTORвҶ‘ вҶ’ fibroblast proliferation; mtDNA damage вҶ’ NLRP3; autophagy impairment |
| **Drug PK вҖ” Pirfenidone** | F=81%, ka=1.74/h, tВҪ=2.4h, CL=8.4 L/h, V1=20.4 L; food delays Tmax (3h fed vs 1h fasted); CYP1A2 (85%) + CYP2C9/3A4 (15%); renal elimination (80%); EC50 ~30 Вөg/mL (TGF-ОІ inhibition) |
| **Drug PK вҖ” Nintedanib** | F=4.7% (P-gp/BCRP efflux limits absorption), ka=0.8/h, tВҪ=10h, CL=22 L/h, V1=730 L; CYP3A4 + UGT glucuronidation; biliary elimination (93%); IC50 ~20 nM (FGFR1); BIBF1202 active metabolite |
| **Drug PD Targets** | Pirfenidone: TGF-ОІ1вҶ“ / TNF-ОұвҶ“ / PDGFвҶ“ / FGFвҶ“ / ROSвҶ“; Nintedanib: VEGFR-1/2/3 / PDGFRОұ/ОІ / FGFR-1/2/3 / Src/Lck/RET competitive TKI |
| **Clinical Endpoints** | FVC% predicted (primary), DLCO%, TLC%, 6MWD, AE-IPF, HRCT honeycombing/GGO score, GAP index (Gender-Age-Physiology), all-cause mortality |
| **Comorbidities** | GERD/microaspiration, OSA, pulmonary hypertension, emphysema (CPFE), lung cancer (2вҖ“3Г— risk), smoking (major risk) |

### Drug Mechanisms

| Drug | Dose | Mechanism | Key Trial | Primary Outcome |
|------|------|-----------|-----------|-----------------|
| **Pirfenidone** | 801 mg TID oral | Anti-fibrotic/anti-inflammatory: вҶ“TGF-ОІ1 secretion, вҶ“PDGF, вҶ“TNF-Оұ, antioxidant (вҶ‘GSH) | ASCEND (NEJM 2014) | вҲ’47.9% FVC decline reduction vs placebo (p<0.001) |
| **Nintedanib** | 150 mg BID oral | Triple tyrosine kinase inhibitor: FGFR-1/2/3, VEGFR-1/2/3, PDGFRОұ/ОІ | INPULSIS-1/2 (NEJM 2014) | вҲ’50.1% FVC decline reduction vs placebo (p<0.001) |
| **Combination** | Both agents | Additive/complementary mechanisms (different targets) | INJOURNEY (2018) | Numerically greater FVC preservation vs monotherapy |
| **N-Acetylcysteine** | 600 mg TID | GSH precursor вҶ’ antioxidant | PANTHER-IPF (NEJM 2012) | No benefit over placebo (monotherapy) |
| **Nintedanib (SSc-ILD)** | 150 mg BID | FGFR/VEGFR/PDGFR inhibition in systemic sclerosis-ILD | SENSCIS (NEJM 2019) | FVC decline reduced вҲ’44% |

### Model Specifications

| Feature | Detail |
|---------|--------|
| ODE Compartments | **17** (Pirfenidone PK Г—3 + Nintedanib PK Г—3 + AEC2 + TGF-ОІ + M2 + ROS + Fibroblast + Myofibroblast + Collagen + MMP + TIMP + FVC + DLCO) |
| Treatment Scenarios | **5**: Placebo В· Pirfenidone 801 mg TID В· Nintedanib 150 mg BID В· Combination В· Pirfenidone Low Dose (267 mg TID) |
| Clinical Calibration | ASCEND: вҲ’47.9% FVC decline reduction; INPULSIS: вҲ’50.1% FVC decline reduction; Natural history ~200 mL/yr |
| PK Sources | Pirfenidone: Rubino 2009 (J Clin Pharmacol); Nintedanib: Stopfer 2011 (Clin Pharmacokinet) |
| Biomarkers Tracked | MMP-7 (serum, proxy), KL-6 (proxy, U/mL scale), Periostin (proxy), TGF-ОІ1, collagen, MMP:TIMP ratio |
| Dose-Response | 4-dose pirfenidone (267вҖ“1068 mg TID) Г— 4-dose nintedanib (50вҖ“200 mg BID) |

### Key Equations

```
dAEC2/dt   = k_rep Г— (1 вҲ’ AEC2) вҲ’ k_AEC Г— ROS Г— AEC2
dTGFb/dt   = [kprod + kactГ—(1вҲ’AEC2) + 0.06Г—M2 + 0.04Г—Myofib] Г— (1вҲ’inh_P) вҲ’ kdegГ—TGFb
inh_P      = Emax_P Г— Cp / (EC50_P + Cp)          // Pirfenidone Hill inhibition
inh_N      = Emax_N Г— Cn_nM / (EC50_N + Cn_nM)    // Nintedanib Hill inhibition
dMYOFIB/dt = kdiff Г— FIBRO Г— TGFb Г— (1 вҲ’ 0.5Г—inh_N) вҲ’ 0.006Г—MYOFIB
dCOL/dt    = kprod_col Г— MYOFIB вҲ’ kdeg_col Г— MMP/(TIMP+0.1) Г— COL
dFVC/dt    = вҲ’k_FVC Г— (COLвҲ’1)вӮҠ Г— FVC              // FVC loss from collagen excess
GAP Score  = G(sex) + A(age) + P(FVC%) + P(DLCO%)  // O'Mahony 2014
```

### Shiny App (6 Interactive Tabs)

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| в‘  Patient Profile | Patient FVC/DLCO input; GAP score calculator (O'Mahony 2014 formula); natural history FVC trajectory; severity classification table |
| в‘Ў Drug PK | Pirfenidone 72h plasma Cp (Вөg/mL) vs EC50; Nintedanib 72h Cn (nM) vs IC50; PK parameter table; population PK variability (n=50 Monte Carlo, CV~30%) |
| в‘ў Lung Function | FVC% and DLCO% time-course; real-time value boxes (52-wk FVC, DLCO, decline, treatment response %); spirometry severity zones; annualized decline rate |
| в‘Ј Biomarkers | TGF-ОІ1 & myofibroblast trajectories; ECM collagen/MMP/TIMP dynamics; serum MMP-7/KL-6/Periostin proxies; ROS & AEC-II integrity; biomarker correlation heatmap |
| в‘Ө Scenario Comparison | 5-scenario head-to-head FVC plot; summary datatable (Week 0/13/26/39/52); treatment effect bar chart vs placebo; pirfenidone & nintedanib dose-response curves |
| в‘Ҙ Mechanistic Map | Full IPF mechanistic map PNG (130+ nodes, 12 clusters); pathway interaction table; drug mechanism target summary |

### Systemic Sclerosis (SSc)

> Directory: [`systemic-sclerosis/`](systemic-sclerosis/)

**Date added:** 2026-06-17  
**Category:** мһҗк°Җл©ҙм—ӯм§Ҳнҷҳ / кІ°н•©мЎ°м§Ғ (Autoimmune / Connective Tissue Disease)

**Disease Overview:**  
Systemic sclerosis (SSc) is a rare systemic autoimmune disease defined by three hallmark pathological processes: **(1) autoimmunity** вҖ” T/B cell dysregulation producing disease-specific autoantibodies (anti-Scl-70, anti-centromere, anti-RNA Pol III); **(2) vasculopathy** вҖ” Raynaud's phenomenon, endothelial injury, ET-1 overproduction, digital ulcers, SSc-associated PAH; **(3) fibrosis** вҖ” TGF-ОІ/SMAD2-3-driven myofibroblast activation, ECM accumulation causing skin (mRSSвҶ‘), lung (ILD/FVCвҶ“), kidney (SRC), and GI tract fibrosis.

| Subtype | Skin | Key Ab | Organ Risk |
|---------|------|--------|------------|
| dcSSc (diffuse) | Proximal limbs + trunk | Anti-Scl-70 | ILD, SRC, cardiac |
| lcSSc (limited/CREST) | Hands + face | Anti-centromere | PAH, GAVE |
| SSc sine scleroderma | None | Variable | Internal organs only |

**Mechanistic Map** (15 clusters, >100 nodes):

[![SSc QSP Map](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_qsp_model.png)](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_qsp_model.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Layer | State Variables | Key Equations |
|-------|----------------|---------------|
| Drug PK | 5 drugs: Nintedanib (2-cpt), TCZ (2-cpt IV), MPA/MMF (1-cpt), Bosentan (1-cpt), Iloprost (inhaled 1-cpt) | Multi-compartment ODEs with Hill PD effects |
| Cytokines | TGF-ОІ1, IL-6, Th17, Bnv | Production/degradation + drug inhibition |
| Fibrosis | FAct, Myo, Col1, Col3, ECM | Sequential activation cascade |
| Skin | mRSS (0-51) | ECM-driven logistic growth |
| Lung ILD | FVC %, DLCO % | FVC loss rate = kFVC Г— ECM Г— (1 вҲ’ E_NINT) |
| Vascular | ET-1, NO, PGI2, Endo, PVR, 6MWD | Bosentan: вҠЈ ETAR; Iloprost: вҶ‘ PGI2 analog |

**Treatment Scenarios (6):**
1. Untreated (natural history)
2. Nintedanib 150 mg BID вҖ” SENSCIS (NEJM 2019; вҲ’41% FVC decline)
3. Tocilizumab 8 mg/kg IV q4w вҖ” focuSSced (Lancet RM 2020)
4. MMF 3000 mg/day вҖ” SLS II (Lancet RM 2016)
5. Bosentan 125 mg BID вҖ” ERA for PAH (RAPIDS-2: вҲ’48% digital ulcers)
6. Full combination: Nintedanib + Tocilizumab + MMF

**Files:**

| File | Description |
|------|-------------|
| [`ssc_qsp_model.dot`](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_qsp_model.dot) | Graphviz mechanistic map (>100 nodes, 15 subgraph clusters) |
| [`ssc_qsp_model.svg`](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_qsp_model.svg) | Vector image |
| [`ssc_qsp_model.png`](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_qsp_model.png) | Raster image (150 dpi) |
| [`ssc_mrgsolve_model.R`](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_mrgsolve_model.R) | mrgsolve ODE model + 5 scenarios + virtual population (N=200) |
| [`ssc_shiny_app.R`](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_shiny_app.R) | 6-tab Shiny dashboard (PK, fibrosis, ILD, vascular, comparison) |
| [`ssc_references.md`](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_references.md) | 50 PubMed references (10 sections) |

## Gout

> Directory: [`gout/`](gout/)

**Date added:** 2026-06-17  
**Category:** л§Ңм„ұм§Ҳнҷҳ / лҢҖмӮ¬ (Chronic Disease / Metabolic)

**Disease Overview:**  
Gout is the most prevalent inflammatory arthritis worldwide, caused by chronic hyperuricemia (serum urate >6.8 mg/dL) leading to monosodium urate (MSU) crystal deposition in joints and periarticular tissues. The disease progresses through four stages: **(1) asymptomatic hyperuricemia**, **(2) acute gouty arthritis flares** (NLRP3-driven IL-1ОІ release), **(3) intercritical gout**, and **(4) chronic tophaceous gout** (visible crystal deposits, joint destruction). Gout is strongly associated with metabolic syndrome, CKD, cardiovascular disease, and hypertension.

### Key Pathophysiological Cascade

```
Dietary purines + Fructose + Endogenous synthesis
         вҶ“  [Xanthine Oxidase (XO)]
    Hypoxanthine вҶ’ Xanthine вҶ’ Uric Acid
         вҶ“
   Serum Urate Pool  вҶҗвҶ’  URAT1 (reabsorption, 88%)
                          OAT1/OAT3 (secretion)
                          ABCG2 (gut + renal secretion)
         вҶ“ [>6.8 mg/dL in synovial fluid]
    MSU Crystal Nucleation & Growth
         вҶ“ [Phagocytosis by macrophages/neutrophils]
   NLRP3 Inflammasome Assembly (Signal 1: NF-ОәB; Signal 2: cathepsin B)
         вҶ“ [Caspase-1 activation]
    Pro-IL-1ОІ вҶ’ Mature IL-1ОІ (+ IL-18, Gasdermin D/pyroptosis)
         вҶ“
   Neutrophil recruitment вҶ’ NETosis вҶ’ Joint inflammation
         вҶ“
    Acute Flare (pain NRSвҶ‘, swelling, warmth, CRPвҶ‘)
         вҶ“ [chronic course]
    Tophus formation вҶ’ Cartilage/bone erosion
```

### Drug Mechanisms Modeled

| Drug Class | Agents | Target | Clinical Evidence |
|-----------|--------|--------|-------------------|
| XO Inhibitors | Allopurinol (oxypurinol) | XO competitive inhibition | CONFIRMS trial (Becker 2005/2010) |
| XO Inhibitors | Febuxostat | XO non-purine selective | CONFIRMS: 80mg вҶ’~70% sUAвҶ“ |
| Uricosurics | Probenecid | URAT1 blockade | Classical agent |
| Uricosurics | Lesinurad | URAT1 + OAT4 | CLEAR 1&2: +add-on 37% target |
| Colchicine | Low-dose colchicine | Tubulin / NLRP3 assembly | AGREE trial (Terkeltaub 2010) |
| NSAIDs | Indomethacin | COX-1/COX-2 | Acute flare standard |
| IL-1 biologics | Anakinra (IL-1Ra) | IL-1 receptor | Refractory flares |
| IL-1 biologics | Canakinumab (anti-IL-1ОІ) | Neutralizes IL-1ОІ | CANTOS / So 2010 |

### Mechanistic Map

[![Gout QSP Map](gout/gout_qsp_model.png)](gout/gout_qsp_model.svg)

> **13 subgraph clusters В· 120+ nodes В· 100+ edges**  
> Purine Metabolism В· XO-Inhibitor PK В· Uricosuric PK В· Renal Transport (URAT1/OAT/ABCG2) В· Systemic Urate Distribution В· Crystal Formation & Synovial Compartment В· NLRP3 Inflammasome В· Inflammatory Mediators В· Cellular Response В· Anti-inflammatory Drug PK В· IL-1 Biologic PK В· Clinical Endpoints В· Comorbidities & Genetics

### ODE Model Architecture (33 state variables)

| Compartment | States | Key Equations |
|-------------|--------|---------------|
| Urate Distribution | A_UA_cent, A_UA_peri, A_UA_syn | Production (XO) вҲ’ Renal CLr вҲ’ Gut ABCG2 вҲ’ Distribution |
| Crystal & Tophus | A_Crystal, A_Tophus | Crystal = k_formВ·(sUAвҲ’sat)вҒә вҲ’ k_diss вҲ’ PMN clearance |
| Inflammasome | A_IL1b, A_TNFa, A_PMN, A_Pain | NLRP3 activation вҶ’ Caspase-1 вҶ’ IL-1ОІ; Neutrophil influx |
| Disease Outcomes | A_JointDmg, A_eGFR | Linear damage accumulation; Urate-nephropathy eGFR decline |
| Allopurinol/Oxypurinol | A_Allo_gut, A_Allo_cent, A_Oxy_cent, A_Oxy_peri | 2-cpt + metabolite; XO inhibition: I=C/(C+Ki) |
| Febuxostat | A_Febu_gut, A_Febu_cent, A_Febu_peri | 2-cpt; Ki=1 nM (potent non-purine XO inhibitor) |
| Probenecid | A_Prob_gut, A_Prob_cent, A_Prob_peri | 2-cpt; URAT1 IC50=5 mg/L |
| Lesinurad | A_Lesi_gut, A_Lesi_cent | 1-cpt; URAT1/OAT4 IC50=0.1 mg/L |
| Colchicine | A_Colch_gut, A_Colch_cent, A_Colch_peri | 2-cpt; NLRP3 assembly вҠЈ Emax=85% |
| Indomethacin | A_Indo_gut, A_Indo_cent, A_Indo_tiss | 2-cpt; COX inhibition |
| Anakinra | A_Ana_SC, A_Ana_cent, A_Ana_peri | SC 2-cpt; IL-1Ra receptor blockade |
| Canakinumab | A_Cana_SC, A_Cana_cent, A_Cana_peri, A_IL1b_Cana | SC TMDD; IL-1ОІ neutralization + catabolism |

### Treatment Scenarios (8)

| # | Scenario | Rationale |
|---|----------|-----------|
| 1 | Untreated hyperuricemia | Natural history baseline |
| 2 | Allopurinol 300 mg/day | Standard first-line ULT |
| 3 | Febuxostat 80 mg/day | Potent XO inhibitor (non-purine) |
| 4 | Allopurinol 300mg + Lesinurad 200mg | Dual mechanism combo (CLEAR studies) |
| 5 | Colchicine 1.2mg + 0.6mg (low-dose) | Acute flare: AGREE regimen |
| 6 | Indomethacin 50mg TID | Acute flare: NSAID regimen |
| 7 | Canakinumab 150mg SC | Refractory flares / biologic |
| 8 | Febuxostat 80mg + Colchicine prophylaxis 0.5mg/day | ULT + flare prevention |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** вҖ” Demographics, diet/alcohol, CKD, ABCG2 Q141K polymorphism, drug dose sliders
2. **Serum Urate (sUA)** вҖ” sUA trajectory, target attainment, XO inhibition %, crystal burden, tophus volume
3. **Inflammation & Pain** вҖ” IL-1ОІ dynamics, neutrophil influx, NRS pain score, flare duration
4. **Clinical Endpoints** вҖ” eGFR trajectory, joint damage accumulation, flare risk, outcomes table
5. **Scenario Comparison** вҖ” Up to 5 pre-defined treatment scenarios plotted side by side
6. **Biomarkers & Genetics** вҖ” CRP proxy, ABCG2/URAT1/GLUT9 genetics, NLRP3 pathway summary, HLA-B*58:01
7. **References** вҖ” Pivotal trials, guidelines, CPIC pharmacogenomics

## SjГ¶gren's Syndrome (pSS)

> **мһҗк°Җл©ҙм—ӯм§Ҳнҷҳ / мҷёл¶„л№„м„  (Autoimmune / Exocrine Glands)**  
> л‘җ лІҲм§ёлЎң нқ”н•ң м „мӢ  мһҗк°Җл©ҙм—ӯм§Ҳнҷҳ (F:M = 9:1; мң лі‘лҘ  ~0.1вҖ“0.4%)

### Mechanistic Map

[![pSS QSP Map](sjogrens-syndrome/ss_qsp_model.png)](sjogrens-syndrome/ss_qsp_model.svg)

> **12 subgraph clusters В· 180+ nodes В· 200+ edges**  
> Genetic Triggers В· Innate Immune Activation (pDC/TLR7/9/cGAS-STING/NETs/NLRP3) В· T-cell Compartment (Th1/Th17/Tfh/Treg) В· B-cell Activation & Autoantibody (Anti-SSA/SSB/M3R/AQP5 + BAFF/APRIL/GC) В· Salivary Gland Pathology (AQP5/M3R/CaВІвҒә/UWSF) В· Lacrimal/Ocular Surface В· Systemic Extraglandular Manifestations В· Lymphoproliferation & MALT Lymphoma (FFS score) В· Intracellular Signaling (JAK-STAT/NF-ОәB/PI3K/BTK) В· Drug PK Compartments В· Drug PD Mechanisms В· Biomarkers & Clinical Outcomes

### Pathophysiology Summary

```
Genetic susceptibility (HLA-DR3, IRF5, STAT4, BLK, TNFAIP3)
+ Environmental trigger (EBV/UV/oxidative stress)
         вҶ“
Apotope release (Ro52/Ro60 on apoptotic blebs)
         вҶ“
pDC: TLR7/9 + cGAS-STING вҶ’ IRF7/IRF3 вҶ’ Type I IFN (IFN-Оұ/ОІ)
         вҶ“ [ISG signature in 75% of pSS patients]
IFN-I вҶ’ BAFFвҶ‘ (BEC/macrophage) + mDC maturation
         вҶ“
T-cell priming: Th1 (IFN-Оі/TNF-Оұ) + Th17 (IL-17A/IL-21) + Tfh
         вҶ“                                        вҶ“
Glandular infiltration вҶҗв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ B-cell activation
(CD4+ periductal foci)              BAFF-R + CD40/CD40L + BCR
(focus score вүҘ1/4mmВІ)              вҶ“
         вҶ“              GC formation вҶ’ Anti-SSA/Ro52(>95%) + Anti-SSB/La
Acinar apoptosis (FasL)  + Anti-M3R вҶ’ M3R blockade вҶ’ cAMP/CaВІвҒә вҶ“
AQP5 downregulation                 вҶ’ AQP5 internalization вҶ“
         вҶ“                                    вҶ“
UWSF вҶ“ (<1.5 mL/15 min)     Lacrimal: Schirmer вүӨ5 mm/5 min
Xerostomia (dental caries,    Keratoconjunctivitis sicca
dysphagia, oral candida)      MMP-9вҶ‘, tear osmolarityвҶ‘
         вҶ“ [chronic course; 40вҖ“50Г— lymphoma risk]
Ectopic GC (CXCL13/CXCL12) вҶ’ B-cell clonal expansion
         вҶ“
MALT lymphoma вҶ’ DLBCL (MYC rearrangement)
FFS score: low C4 + ОІвӮӮ-MGвҶ‘ + cryos + parotid enlargement
```

### Drug Mechanisms Modeled

| Drug | Target | Mechanism | Key Trial |
|------|--------|-----------|-----------|
| Hydroxychloroquine (HCQ) | TLR7/9 (lysosomal) | pHвҶ‘ вҶ’ pDC inhibition вҶ’ IFN-IвҶ“ | JOQUER (Ann Rheum Dis 2014) |
| Pilocarpine (Salagen 5 mg QID) | M3-muscarinic receptor | Cholinergic agonist вҶ’ CaВІвҒә/cAMPвҶ‘ вҶ’ UWSF/tearвҶ‘ | Papas 2004 (J Rheumatol) |
| Cevimeline (Evoxac 30 mg TID) | M3R (selective) | Selective M3R agonist | Fife 2002 (J Rheumatol) |
| Rituximab (2Г—1g IV) | CD20 (B cells) | CDC/ADCC вҶ’ B-cell depletion | TEARS trial (Devauchelle-Pensec 2014) |
| Ianalumab (300 mg SC q4w) | BAFF-R | B-cell depletion via BAFF-R blockade | TWINSS Phase 3 (Bowman 2022, Lancet) |
| Iscalimab (anti-CD40) | CD40 (B cell) | TвҖ“B interactionвҶ“ вҶ’ GC disruption | Fisher 2020 (Ann Rheum Dis) |
| Baricitinib (2вҖ“4 mg QD) | JAK1/2 | IFN-I/IL-6 signalingвҶ“ вҶ’ ESSDAIвҶ“ | Bowman 2023 (Arthritis Rheumatol) |
| Topical CsA 0.05% | Calcineurin | NFATвҶ“ вҶ’ corneal T-cellвҶ“ | Sall 2000 (Ophthalmology) |
| Lifitegrast 5% drops | LFA-1/ICAM-1 | T-cell corneal adhesionвҶ“ | OPUS-3 (Holland 2017) |

### ODE Model Architecture (19 state variables)

| Compartment Group | States | Key Equations |
|-------------------|--------|---------------|
| HCQ PK (3-cmt) | DEPOT_HCQ, C1_HCQ, C2_HCQ | F=0.74, Ka=0.05/h, Vd=750 L/kg; tВҪвүҲ40 d (tissue accumulation) |
| Pilocarpine PK | DEPOT_PIL, C_PIL | 1-cmt oral; EC50_PIL=80 ng/mL вҶ’ UWSF increase |
| Rituximab PK | C1_RTX, C2_RTX | 2-cmt; CL=0.20 L/h; Hill: E=(CвҒҝ)/(EC50вҒҝ+CвҒҝ); EMAX=90% |
| Ianalumab PK | C1_IAN, C2_IAN | IgG1 mAb; CL=0.18 L/h; EC50=8 mcg/mL; EMAX=88% |
| Prednisolone PK | DEPOT_PRD, C_PRD | 1-cmt; GRвҶ’NF-ОәBвҶ“; max 50% cytokine suppression |
| Type I IFN (PD) | IFN | KIN_IFN Г— STIM Г— (1вҲ’HCQ_inh) вҲ’ KOUT Г— IFN |
| BAFF (PD) | BAFF_pd | KIN Г— (1+(STIM_BAFвҲ’1)Г—IFN) Г— (1вҲ’PRD) вҲ’ KOUTГ—BAFF |
| B cells (PD) | BCELL | KIN Г— (1+(STIM_BCвҲ’1)Г—BAFF) Г— (1вҲ’RTX_depвҲ’IAN_dep) вҲ’ KOUTГ—BC |
| Plasma cells | PLASMA_C | Input from BC Г— (1вҲ’0.3Г—RTX) вҲ’ KOUT_PC Г— PC |
| Anti-SSA titer | AB_SSA | KIN Г— (1+(STIM_ABвҲ’1)Г—PC) вҲ’ KOUT_AB Г— AB; tВҪвүҲ96 d |
| Salivary function | SAL | KIN Г— SAL_tgt Г— (1+PIL_stim) вҲ’ KOUT Г— SAL |
| Lacrimal function | LAC | KIN Г— LAC_tgt Г— (1+0.4Г—PIL_stim) вҲ’ KOUT Г— LAC |
| ESSDAI (proxy) | ESSDAI_pd | Driven by BCELL+IFN+AB; scaled to clinical 0вҖ“123 |
| Lymphoma risk | LYMPHOMA | dLR/dt = k_LR Г— BCELL Г— BAFF (cumulative integrator) |

### Treatment Scenarios (5)

| # | Scenario | Key Effect | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|-----------|-------------------|
| 1 | No treatment | Progressive glandular loss, lymphoma risk вҶ‘ | Natural history |
| 2 | HCQ 400 mg/day | IFN-IвҶ“ via TLR7/9 block; modest ESSDAIвҶ“ | JOQUER 2014 |
| 3 | HCQ + Pilocarpine 5 mg QID | Symptomatic UWSFвҶ‘ + SchirmerвҶ‘; no systemic effect | Papas 2004 |
| 4 | HCQ + Rituximab 2Г—1g | B-cell depletion вҶ’ BAFFвҶ“ + Anti-SSAвҶ“ + ESSDAIвҶ“ | TEARS 2014 |
| 5 | HCQ + Ianalumab 300 mg q4w | BAFF-RвҖ“mediated B-cell depletion; ESSDAI response вүҘ3 | TWINSS 2022 (Lancet) |

### Shiny Dashboard (6 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** вҖ” ESSDAI/ESSPRI info boxes; Schirmer & UWSF; ACR/EULAR classification criteria table
2. **Drug PK Profiles** вҖ” HCQ steady-state, pilocarpine single-dose, rituximab 2-dose, ianalumab q4w concentration-time plots
3. **Disease Biomarkers** вҖ” IFN-I index, BAFF pg/mL, B-cell pool %, Anti-SSA EU; biomarker summary table at weeks 24/52
4. **Glandular Function** вҖ” UWSF, Schirmer, pilocarpine on/off comparison, glandular function table
5. **Scenario Comparison** вҖ” ESSDAI, B cells, Anti-SSA, UWSF for all 5 scenarios; endpoint comparison table at week 24
6. **Lymphoma Risk** вҖ” FFS score calculator, cumulative risk plot, CXCL13/B-cell ectopic GC dynamics, FFS component table

## Type 1 Diabetes Mellitus (T1DM)

> Directory: [`type1-diabetes/`](type1-diabetes/)

**Mechanistic Map** (12 clusters, 130+ nodes):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic & Environmental Susceptibility | HLA-DR3/DR4, PTPN22, CTLA4, IL2RA, INS-VNTR, IFIH1/MDA5; enterovirus/CVB, gut dysbiosis, early nutrition, vitamin D |
| Innate Immunity | pDC вҶ’ IFN-Оұ/ОІ (Type I IFN); mDC maturation; macrophage M1; NK; NLRP3/IL-1ОІ; TLR3/7; RIG-I/MDA5/cGAS-STING; CXCL10 |
| Adaptive Immunity (T cells) | Naive CD4+вҶ’Th1/Tfh; Naive CD8+вҶ’CTLвҶ’Memory; TCR activation; IFN-Оі/TNF-Оұ/IL-2; Perforin/GrB; FasL/TRAIL; CTLA-4/PD-1 coinhibition; Treg (FoxP3+) |
| B Cells & Autoantibodies | Naive BвҶ’GC BвҶ’Plasma cell; BAFF/APRIL; IAA (1st Ab) + GADA + IA-2A + ZnT8A; multi-Ab staging (Stage 1вҖ“3) |
| Beta-cell Insulitis & Destruction | Islet infiltration; MHC-I upregulation (IFN-Оі); ER stress (BiP/IRE1Оұ/PERK); ROS/RNS; mitochondrial dysfunction; Caspase-3 apoptosis; Bm decline |
| Beta-cell Biology & GSIS | GLUT2/GCK вҶ’ ATP/ADP вҶ’ KATP closure вҶ’ depolarisation вҶ’ VGCC вҶ’ CaВІвҒә вҶ’ exocytosis; GLP-1R/GIP-R вҶ’ cAMP вҶ’ amplification; proinsulin вҶ’ C-peptide |
| Glucose Homeostasis | Gut Ra; plasma glucose [G]; hepatic EGP + GU + glycogen; muscle/adipose GLUT4; brain; renal SGLT2; glucagon (Оұ-cell); IR signalling (IRS1/PI3K/Akt); HbA1c; AGEs |
| Insulin PK (Therapeutic) | SC depot (hexamerвҶ’monomer); central + peripheral compartments; hepatic/renal clearance; basal (Glargine/Degludec) + bolus (Aspart/Lispro/Fiasp); CSII pump; CGM вҶ’ APC/HCL |
| Disease-Modifying Immunotherapy | Teplizumab (anti-CD3, TN-10); Abatacept (CTLA4-Ig); Rituximab (anti-CD20); ATG+G-CSF; Baricitinib (JAK1/2, BANDIT); Low-dose IL-2; CAR-Treg; Islet Tx; SC-islets (VX-880) |
| Adjunctive Pharmacotherapy | SGLT2i (sotagliflozin/empagliflozin); GLP-1RA (semaglutide); Pramlintide (amylin); Metformin; ACEi; Statin |
| Chronic Complications | AGE/RAGE вҶ’ PKC/polyol/hexosamine вҶ’ ROS; Nephropathy (TGF-ОІ1/SMAD); Retinopathy (VEGF/pericyte loss); Neuropathy (axonal); CVD; Hypoglycaemia unawareness |
| Clinical Endpoints & Biomarkers | HbA1c (<7%); TIR 70вҖ“180 (>70%); TBR <70 (<4%); TAR >180 (<25%); C-peptide AUC (MMTT); insulin TDD; eGFR/UACR; LDL-C; DQOL/PAID |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![T1DM QSP Map](type1-diabetes/t1dm_qsp_model.png)](type1-diabetes/t1dm_qsp_model.svg)

### ODE Compartments (20 states)

| Compartment | State | Description |
|-------------|-------|-------------|
| Beta-cell & Immune | Bm, CTL, Treg | Normalised beta-cell mass; pathogenic CTL; regulatory T cells |
| C-Peptide | Cpep | Endogenous secretion marker (pmol/L) |
| Glucose kinetics | Gp, Gt | Plasma and tissue glucose (mg/dL) |
| Insulin PK | SC1, SC2, Ic, Ip | SC hexamer, monomer depots; central + peripheral plasma |
| Insulin action | X_ins | Remote effect compartment (Akt/GLUT4 proxy) |
| Glucagon | Gcg | Оұ-cell glucagon (pg/mL); EGP counter-regulation |
| HbA1c | HbA1c | Running-mean glycation proxy (ADAG equation) |
| Teplizumab PK | Ctep | IV anti-CD3 mAb (Ојg/mL); CTLвҶ“/TregвҶ‘ MOA |
| CGM / APC | CGM_comp, APC_integral | Interstitial glucose (10-min lag); PID integral state |
| Meal absorption | Qsto1, Qsto2, Qgut | Dalla Man 3-compartment gut model |
| Mean glucose | MG_avg | 30-day running average for HbA1c / complication risk |

### Treatment Scenarios (6)

| # | Scenario | Key Modelled Effect | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|---------------------|-------------------|
| 1 | Untreated T1DM | Progressive BmвҶ“, HbA1cвҶ‘ >10%, DKA risk | Natural history |
| 2 | MDI (Basal + Bolus) | HbA1c target ~7%; TIR ~50вҖ“60% | DCCT 1993 (intensive arm) |
| 3 | CSII (Insulin Pump) | HbA1c вҲ’0.3% vs. MDI; TIR +8% | TREAT trial 2019 |
| 4 | Hybrid Closed-Loop (HCL/APC) | TIR +11%, TBR вҲ’1%, HbA1c вҲ’0.5% | NEJM Breton 2020 |
| 5 | Teplizumab (Stage 2 prevention) | Bm stabilised, T1DM onset delayed ~3 yrs | TN-10 (Herold NEJM 2019) |
| 6 | Teplizumab + MDI (Stage 3 onset) | C-peptide preserved; insulin TDD вҶ“ ~30% | AT-RISK 2023, Sims 2021 |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** вҖ” Disease stage value boxes (HbA1c/C-peptide/Bm); autoantibody prevalence bar chart; T1DM natural history curve (ОІ-cell + glucose)
2. **Insulin PK** вҖ” Insulin type selector (5 types); SC concentrationвҖ“time plot; PK parameter table (Tmax, duration, CL, ka)
3. **Glucose & CGM** вҖ” Full glucose trace with TIR band; Ambulatory Glucose Profile (percentiles); CGM metric table; glucose zone histogram
4. **Beta-cell & Immunity** вҖ” Beta-cell mass trajectory; CTL & Treg dynamic panels; C-peptide AUC plot; kDest sensitivity analysis
5. **Scenario Comparison** вҖ” 6-scenario HbA1c + Bm traces; CGM metric comparison table (TIR/TBR/TAR/GMI)
6. **Biomarkers & Complications** вҖ” Cumulative complication risk (nephropathy/retinopathy/neuropathy); 10-yr risk table; HbA1c vs. complication probability curves
7. **About** вҖ” Model description, clinical trial calibration table, technical references

| Cytokine Network | IL-17A/F В· IL-22 (KC hyperplasia) В· TNF-Оұ В· IL-1ОІ В· IL-6 В· IL-8/CXCL8 В· IL-18 В· IL-10 В· IL-36Оұ/ОІ/Оі В· IFN-Оі В· TGF-ОІ1 В· VEGF В· MMP-3 В· S100A8/9 В· CXCL10 В· CCL20 (CCR6вҶ’Th17) В· OSM |

| Skin Pathology | Keratinocyte вҶ’ KC activated (IL-17/IL-22/TNF/IL-36); LL-37/ОІ-defensin AMPs вҶ’ TLR7/9 auto-DNA loop; Acanthosis + parakeratosis вҶ’ PASI; Neutrophil Munro microabscess; VEGF angiogenesis; Hair follicle pDC reservoir |

| Bone Remodeling | RANKL/RANK/OPG; M-CSF; DKK1 (Wnt inhibitor, TNF/IL-17 вҶ‘); BMP2/4/6 + Wnt/ОІ-catenin вҶ’ osteoblast + periostitis; dual pathology: erosion + new bone; mTSS/SHS structural damage |
| GutвҖ“SkinвҖ“Joint Axis | Dysbiosis (AkkermansiaвҶ“/FirmicutesвҶ‘) вҶ’ barrier permeability вҶ’ LPS вҶ’ TLR4 вҶ’ Macrophage M1; ILC3 gut trafficking; sIgA; IBD association (~7%); CRP/fibrinogen acute phase |
| Nail Disease & Comorbidities | NAPSI score (nail matrix enthesis); Uveitis (~7%); MetSyn; CV risk вҶ‘1.3Г—; Depression/Anxiety 37%; Obesity вҶ’ LeptinвҶ‘/AdiponectinвҶ“; NAFLD ~47% |
| Drug PK | ADA 2-cmt SC+TMDD; IXE/GUS 1-cmt SC+TMDD; UPA/APR oral 1-cmt; FcRn recycling (IgG); ka/CL/Vd/F parameters from population PK analyses |
| Drug Mechanisms | TNFi (ADA/ETN/IFX/CZP/GOL) В· IL-17Ai (IXE/SEC/BIM) В· IL-23i (GUS/RIS/TIL) В· IL-12/23i (UST/p40) В· JAKi (UPA/TOF/BAR/FIL: JAK1/2/3/TYK2) В· PDE4i (Apremilast: cAMPвҶ‘вҶ’NF-ОәBвҶ“) В· CTLA4-Ig В· NSAIDs В· MTX В· SSZ |
| Biomarkers & Endpoints | CRP В· ESR В· IL-17A/IL-6 serum В· Calprotectin (S100A8/9) В· MMP-3 В· VEGF; ACR20/50/70 В· PASI75/90/100 В· DAPSA (remission вүӨ4/LDA вүӨ14) В· MDA (5/7 criteria) В· VLDA В· CASPAR В· HAQ-DI В· SF-36/PsAID В· mTSS/SHS |

## Ulcerative Colitis (UC)

> Directory: [`ulcerative-colitis/`](ulcerative-colitis/)

**Mechanistic Map** (12 clusters, 204 nodes, 222 edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic & Environmental Risk | HLA-DQ, IL10 locus, IL23R, NOD2, TNFSF15, JAK2 variant, HNF4A, CDH1, IBD loci; Smoking (protective in UC), NSAIDs risk, antibiotics in early life, Western diet, HPA stress axis |
| Epithelial Barrier | Colonocyte, goblet cell (MUC2/MUC5AC), tight junctions (ZO-1, Occludin, Claudin-1), HBD-2 defensin, IEC apoptosis, ER stress/UPR, EGF/IGF-1 receptors, LGR5 crypt stem cell, Paneth cell metaplasia, tuft cellвҖ“IL-25 axis, MLCK activation |
| Gut Microbiome & Dysbiosis | F. prausnitziiвҶ“, BifidobacteriumвҶ“, RoseburiaвҶ“, E. coli AIECвҶ‘, C. difficile; butyrate/SCFA; LPS/MAMPs вҶ’ TLR4; secretory IgA; mucus penetration; dysbiosis index; TLR2/NOD2вҖ“MDP sensing |
| Innate Immune Activation | Resident macrophage M1/M2, recruited monocyte, neutrophil influx (CXCL8 gradient), mDC, pDCвҖ“IFN-Оұ, ILC1/2/3, NKT cell, mast cell, NLRP3 inflammasome вҶ’ Caspase-1 вҶ’ mature IL-1ОІ/IL-18; complement C3/C5a; ROS/NOX2; MPO |
| Adaptive Immunity | CD4 naive вҶ’ Th1/Th2 (UC Th2-dominant)/Th17/Treg/CD8 CTL; B cell вҶ’ plasma cell вҶ’ IgG/sIgA; mesenteric LN; Peyer's patches; Оұ4ОІ7вҖ“MAdCAM-1 gut-homing axis; CCR9/CCL25; LPAM-1; Tfh; memory T cells |
| Cytokine Network | TNF-Оұ В· IL-6 В· IL-1ОІ В· IL-17A/F В· IL-22 В· IL-12/IL-23 В· IL-4 В· IL-5 В· IL-13 (Th2-skewed) В· IL-10 В· TGF-ОІ1 В· CXCL8 В· CCL2 В· IFN-Оі В· TSLP В· IL-25/IL-33 alarmins В· OSM В· VEGF В· MMP-1/3/9 |
| JAK-STAT / NF-ОәB / S1P Signaling | JAK1/2/3/TYK2 вҶ’ STAT1/3/4/6; NF-ОәB/IОәBОұ/IKKОІ; AP-1/p38 MAPK/ERK; mTOR/PI3K-Akt; S1PR1 lymphocyte egress вҶ” S1P gradient; PDE4/cAMP/PKA; RORОіt вҶ’ Th17; T-bet вҶ’ Th1; GATA3 вҶ’ Th2; Foxp3 вҶ’ Treg |
| Colon Pathology | Cryptitis; crypt abscesses; goblet cell depletion; ulceration/erosion; pseudopolyps; submucosal edema; crypt distortion; muscularis propria; toxic megacolon risk; basal plasmacytosis; colorectal cancer risk (APC/Wnt/ОІ-catenin; p53; MSI) |
| Extraintestinal Manifestations | Primary sclerosing cholangitis (PSC); peripheral arthropathy; axial spondyloarthropathy; uveitis; episcleritis; erythema nodosum; pyoderma gangrenosum; thromboembolic disease; chronic anemia; steroid-induced osteopenia; oral aphthous ulcer |
| Drug PK | IFX (2-cmt IV + TMDD / TNF-Оұ); VDZ (1-cmt IV + TMDD / Оұ4ОІ7); TOF oral (1-cmt); OZA oral (1-cmt + CC112273 active metabolite); UST IV induction + SC maintenance; Mesalamine (oral/rectal local); Prednisolone (oral) |
| Drug Mechanisms | Anti-TNF (IFX/ADA/GOL/CZP) вҶ’ TNF-Оұ neutralization; Anti-Оұ4ОІ7 (VDZ) вҶ’ gut-selective lymphocyte trafficking blockade; Anti-IL-12/23p40 (UST) вҶ’ Th1/Th17 suppression; JAKi (TOF: JAK1/3) вҶ’ STAT3/6вҶ“; S1P1 modulator (OZA) вҶ’ lymphocyte retention; 5-ASA (COX-2/NF-ОәBвҶ“, local); Steroids (GR вҶ’ NF-ОәBвҶ“); AZA/6-TGN (purine synthesis inhibition); FMT (microbiome restoration) |
| Biomarkers & Clinical Endpoints | CRP В· ESR В· Fecal calprotectin (FC) В· albumin В· hemoglobin В· Mayo total (0вҖ“12) В· partial Mayo (0вҖ“9) В· UCEIS endoscopic score В· Geboes histological score В· Mucosal healing В· Deep remission (clinical + endoscopic) В· Steroid-free remission В· Colectomy rate В· EIM activity |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

5. **Mucosal Healing** вҖ” mucosal healing index (0вҖ“1) time-course with 0.7 threshold; endoscopic subscore proxy; histological activity proxy (Geboes); deep remission rate vs week
6. **Scenario Comparison** вҖ” multi-scenario toggle; endpoint selector (Mayo/MH/CRP/FC/TNF/IL13); comparative 52-week plot; response summary table at wk8 and wk52 (% clinical remission, % mucosal healing, % deep remission, % steroid-free remission)
7. **Biomarkers & Safety** вҖ” CRP/FC time-courses for each drug; anemia risk (hemoglobin proxy); infection risk (neutrophil change vs baseline); thromboembolic risk flag for tofacitinib (JAKi class effect); lipid change note; PSC progression note

## Polycystic Ovary Syndrome (PCOS)

> Directory: [`polycystic-ovary-syndrome/`](polycystic-ovary-syndrome/)

**Mechanistic Map** (9 clusters + 6 drug subgraphs, 175+ nodes, 200+ edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| HPO Axis | KNDy neurons (Kisspeptin/NKB/Dynorphin) вҶ’ GnRH pulse frequency вҶ‘вҶ‘; GnRHR вҶ’ LH вҶ‘вҶ‘ / FSH (normal-low); LH:FSH ratio >2вҖ“3; Inhibin B / Inhibin A / Activin A feedback; E2 negative feedback (impaired); P4 negative feedback (absent, anovulatory); Prolactin; GH |
| Ovarian Steroidogenesis | Theca cells (вҶ‘LH вҶ’ cAMP/PKA вҶ’ StAR/CYP11A1/CYP17A1 вҶ‘вҶ‘ вҶ’ О”4/О”5 androgens); Granulosa cells (FSH вҶ’ cAMP/PKA вҶ’ CYP19A1 вҶ“ per follicle); DHEA/Androstenedione/Testosterone (ovarian вҶ‘вҶ‘); Estradiol E2 (tonic moderate вҶ‘); Estrone E1; Progesterone P4 (вҶ“вҶ“ anovulatory); AMH вҶ‘вҶ‘ (3вҖ“8Г— normal); HSD17B1/3; INSL3 theca marker |
| Folliculogenesis | Primordial вҶ’ Primary вҶ’ Secondary вҶ’ Small antral (2вҖ“5 mm, excess вҶ‘вҶ‘) вҶ’ arrested large antral (6вҖ“9 mm) вҶ’ dominant follicle selection failure; AMH-mediated arrest вҶ’ FSHR desensitization + CYP19A1 inhibition; AFC >12 per ovary; Ovarian volume >10 mL вҶ’ PCOM criterion; Follicle atresia вҶ‘; Anovulation вҶ’ absent corpus luteum вҶ’ P4 deficiency; Endometrial hyperplasia risk |
| Insulin Signaling | ОІ-cell compensatory hyperinsulinemia; IR: IRS1 serine phos (JNK/PKC) вҶ‘, IRS1 tyrosine phos вҶ“; PI3K-AKT вҶ“ (metabolic); GLUT4 translocation вҶ“; FOXO1 active вҶ’ HGP вҶ‘; MAPK-ERK preserved вҶ’ CYP17A1 вҶ‘вҶ‘ (key IR-androgen link); mTOR-S6K feedback; IGF1R potentiates LHR; IGFBP1 вҶ“ (insulin-suppressed); SHBG вҶ“ (hepatic); HOMA-IR вҶ‘ (вүҘ2.5); T2DM risk 6вҖ“10Г— |
| Adrenal Androgen | HPA axis/ACTH вҶ’ Adrenal zona reticularis CYP17A1 вҶ‘ (50% of PCOS) вҶ’ DHEA/DHEAS вҶ‘ + adrenal androstenedione; Insulin upregulates adrenal CYP17A1; Cortisol (normal/mild вҶ‘) |
| Peripheral Androgen | Total T вҶ‘ / Free T вҶ‘вҶ‘ (SHBG вҶ“); SRD5A1 (skin) + SRD5A2 (scalp) вҶ’ DHT вҶ‘; AR in sebaceous glands вҶ’ sebum вҶ‘ вҶ’ acne; AR in terminal hair follicle вҶ’ hirsutism (FG вүҘ8); Scalp miniaturization вҶ’ androgenic alopecia; Hepatic CYP1A2 / UGT вҶ’ 3Оұ-androstanediol glucuronide (5Оұ-RA activity marker); Clinical hyperandrogenism (PCOS criterion 2) |
| Inflammation / Adipokines | Visceral adiposity вҶ’ M1 macrophage вҶ’ TNF-Оұ/IL-6/IL-1ОІ вҶ’ NF-ОәB; TNF-Оұ вҶ’ IRS1-Ser (inflammation-IR loop); ROS/MDA/NOвҶ“ вҶ’ endothelial dysfunction; Leptin вҶ‘ / Adiponectin вҶ“ / Resistin/Visfatin/Chemerin вҶ‘; IL-6 вҶ’ CRP вҶ‘ (>3 mg/L); IL-18 вҶ’ CVD predictor; AMPKвҶ“ in adipose |
| Drug PK/PD | Metformin (2-cmt oral, F=50%, OCT1 liver вҶ’ AMPK вҶ’ PEPCK/G6PaseвҶ“ / CYP17A1вҶ“ / GLP-1вҶ‘); Letrozole (1-cmt oral, F=99%, tВҪ=48h вҶ’ CYP19A1 Ki=11nM вҶ’ E2вҶ“97% вҶ’ FSH вҶ‘ вҶ’ dominant follicle); Clomiphene (central ER block вҶ’ GnRH вҶ‘ вҶ’ LH+FSH вҶ‘, adverse: cervical mucusвҶ“ / endometriumвҶ“); Spironolactone (AR competitive block + SRD5A вҶ“ вҶ’ FGвҶ“30вҖ“40%); Combined OCP (EE вҶ’ SHBG вҶ‘2вҖ“4Г— + LH/FSH вҶ“ вҶ’ T вҶ“); GnRH agonist/antagonist (IVF protocol, pituitary downregulation) |
| Clinical Endpoints | Oligo/amenorrhea (cycle >35 days) В· Anovulation В· Infertility (40вҖ“80%) В· Pregnancy/Live birth rate В· Metabolic syndrome (2вҖ“3Г— risk) В· CVD risk (4Г—) В· T2DM risk В· NASH risk В· Gestational DM (3Г—) В· Preeclampsia (2Г—) В· Sleep apnea В· Depression/anxiety (30вҖ“40%) В· Endometrial hyperplasia В· Rotterdam criteria (2/3: OA + HA + PCOM) |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![PCOS QSP Map](polycystic-ovary-syndrome/pcos_qsp_model.png)](polycystic-ovary-syndrome/pcos_qsp_model.svg)

### ODE Compartments (24 states)

| Group | States | Description |
|-------|--------|-------------|
| HPO Axis | GnRH_drive, LH, FSH | GnRH drive state (elevated baseline in PCOS); LH tВҪвүҲ20 min (k_deg=0.85/day); FSH tВҪвүҲ4 h (k_deg=0.38/day); Inhibin B proxy via AMHГ—0.55+1 suppresses FSH |
| Steroidogenesis | T_total, E2, P4, AMH | Testosterone: LH Г— CYP17A1 activity (up-regulated by insulin, down by metformin) Г— (1вҲ’SPR inhibition); E2: FSH + aromatization of T, suppressed by letrozole (EC50_AI=0.012 mg/L); P4: corpus luteum (DF_stateВІ); AMH: auto-regulated quadratic decay |
| Follicle Dynamics | AFC_state, DF_state | AFC approaches steady-state 19 (PCOS) via first-order regulation; Dominant follicle driven by FSH above threshold (4.8 mIU/mL), inhibited by AMH (k=0.28) |
| Insulin/Metabolic | Insulin, Glucose, IGFBP1 | Glucose-stimulated insulin secretion; Peripheral glucose utilization reduced by k_IRГ—(1вҲ’metformin effect); Hepatic glucose production reduced by metformin 85%; IGFBP1 suppressed by insulin |
| SHBG & Free T | SHBG, FreeT | Hepatic SHBG synthesis: suppressed by insulin, induced by EE (2вҖ“4Г—); FreeT approximated as T Г— (22/SHBG) Г— 0.19 Г— (1вҲ’spiro blockade) |
| Inflammation | CRP, BMI, HirsScore | CRP driven by T and excess BMI; BMI slow drift + metformin reduction; Hirsutism: free T drives FG score increase (blocked by spironolactone AR occupancy) |
| Drug PK | MET_gut, MET_central, MET_periph, LET_plasma, EE_plasma, SPR_plasma, CC_plasma | Metformin 2-compartment (V1=80L, V2=155L, CL=45 L/h, Q=12 L/h, F=50%); Letrozole 1-cmt (V=145L, CL=2.1 L/h, tВҪ=48h); EE 1-cmt (V=250L, CL=38 L/h); Spiro 1-cmt (V=65L, CL=40 L/h); CC 1-cmt (V=105L, CL=1 L/h, tВҪвүҲ5вҖ“7 days) |

### Treatment Scenarios (6)

| # | Scenario | Dose Regimen | Primary Target | Key Trial / Effect |
|---|----------|-------------|----------------|-------------------|
| 1 | Untreated PCOS | вҖ” | вҖ” | Rotterdam ESHRE 2004 baseline; LH=12.5, AMH=10, HOMA-IR=5.2 |
| 2 | Metformin | 500 mg TID (1500 mg/day) | AMPK / CYP17A1 / IR | PPCOS I (Legro 2007): вҶ“androgens ~26%, вҶ“HOMA-IR ~35%; Graham 2011 PK |
| 3 | Letrozole | 2.5 mg/day day 3вҖ“7, q28 days | CYP19A1 (aromatase) | PPCOS II (Legro 2014 NEJM): ovulation 61.7% vs CC 48.3%; live birth 27.5% |
| 4 | Combined OCP | EE 30 Ојg/day Г— 21 days (21/7 cycle) | HPO axis / SHBG | SHBG вҶ‘2вҖ“4Г— (Zimmermann 2014); Free T вҶ“>70% (Odlind 2002) |
| 5 | Metformin + Letrozole | MET 500 mg TID + LET 2.5 mg d3вҖ“7 | AMPK + Aromatase | Additive: вҶ“IR + вҶ‘ovulation; meta-analysis (Palomba 2005); first-line infertility |
| 6 | Spironolactone | 100 mg/day | AR competitive block | FG score вҶ“30вҖ“40% at 6 months (van Zuuren 2015 Cochrane); AR Ki=150 nM |

### Shiny Dashboard (6 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** вҖ” slider inputs (BMI, insulin resistance k_IR, AMH multiplier, AFC); PCOS phenotype classification table (Rotterdam A/B/C/D); baseline biomarker table (LH/FSH/T/E2/SHBG/FAI/AMH/HOMA-IR/CRP/BMI/FG score vs normal ranges)
2. **Hormone Kinetics** вҖ” LH & FSH dynamics (color-coded, dashed threshold); Testosterone & Estradiol (dual-axis); Progesterone (P4, corpus luteum); AMH level; SHBG & Free Testosterone
3. **Metabolic Endpoints** вҖ” HOMA-IR (IR threshold 2.5); Fasting glucose & insulin (dual); BMI trajectory; IGFBP-1; hsCRP (inflammation)
4. **Clinical Endpoints** вҖ” Dominant follicle / ovulation probability (0вҖ“1); Antral follicle count (AFC, threshold 12); Hirsutism FG score (threshold 8); Free Androgen Index (FAI, threshold 4.5%)
5. **Scenario Comparison** вҖ” 6-arm comparison table (DT, conditional color formatting); all-scenario plots for T / HOMA-IR / ovulation probability / FG score
6. **Biomarker Dashboard** вҖ” 8 value boxes (LH, T, HOMA-IR, AMH, FAI, SHBG, CRP, FG score вҖ” green/red status); LH:FSH ratio time-course; risk radar (normalized 6-axis: LH:FSH / T / HOMA-IR / FAI / hsCRP / FG); drug plasma concentration panel

## Dyslipidemia

> Directory: [`dyslipidemia/`](dyslipidemia/)

**Mechanistic Map** (13 subgraph clusters, 211 nodes, 274 edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Hepatic Cholesterol Synthesis | Acetyl-CoA вҶ’ HMG-CoA (HMGCR, rate-limiting) вҶ’ Mevalonate вҶ’ IPP/GPP/FPP вҶ’ Squalene вҶ’ Lanosterol вҶ’ Desmosterol вҶ’ Cholesterol; Side branches: CoQ10, Dolichol, Geranylgeranyl-PP (protein prenylation); ACAT/SOAT1/2 вҶ’ Cholesteryl ester storage |
| LDLR / PCSK9 Regulation | LDLR gene вҶ’ mRNA вҶ’ protein вҶ’ surface receptor вҶ’ LDL endocytosis вҶ’ lysosomal degradation вҶ’ LDLR recycling; PCSK9 gene/mRNA вҶ’ proprotein вҶ’ secretion вҶ’ plasma PCSK9 + LDLR complex вҶ’ lysosomal co-degradation; SREBP-2/SCAP/Insig-1 sterol-sensing loop (ER membrane вҶ’ Golgi вҶ’ nuclear SRE activation вҶ’ LDLR + PCSK9 co-upregulation by statins) |
| Lipoprotein Metabolism | Hepatic ApoB100 synthesis/MTP вҶ’ VLDL1/VLDL2 secretion; LPL (ApoC-II stimulated, ApoC-III inhibited) вҶ’ VLDLвҶ’IDL; HL вҶ’ IDLвҶ’LDL; sdLDL formation; oxLDL (ROS); Lp(a) = LDL + Apo(a)/LPA gene; CETP (CE transfer: HDLвҶ’VLDL/LDL); Chylomicron remnant uptake |
| Reverse Cholesterol Transport (RCT) | Macrophage cholesterol efflux вҶ’ ABCA1вҶ’Pre-ОІ HDL; ABCG1вҶ’HDL3; LCAT (ApoA-I cofactor) вҶ’ HDL3вҶ’HDL2; SR-BI hepatic selective CE uptake; FXR/LXR/PPARОұ transcriptional regulation; ApoA-I synthesis; ApoA-II |
| Intestinal Cholesterol Absorption | Dietary cholesterol + biliary cholesterol вҶ’ Micellar solubilization вҶ’ Enterocyte NPC1L1 uptake; Ezetimibe blocks NPC1L1; ACAT2 вҶ’ CE; ApoB48/MTP вҶ’ Chylomicron assembly; ABCG5/G8 вҶ’ sterol efflux back to lumen |
| Bile Acid Metabolism | CYP7A1 (rate-limiting, FXR-SHP negative feedback); CYP8B1 (CA:CDCA ratio); CYP27A1; FGF19/FGFR4 (intestinal FXRвҶ’hepatic CYP7A1вҶ“); TGR5/GLP-1 axis; BSEP export; Enterohepatic circulation; Bile acid sequestrants bind lumenal BA вҶ’ CYP7A1 upregulation вҶ’ LDLRвҶ‘ |
| Drug Mechanisms | Statin вҶ’ HMGCR inhibition вҶ’ MevalonateвҶ“ вҶ’ SREBP-2 activation вҶ’ LDLRвҶ‘2.5Г— + PCSK9 paradoxвҶ‘; Ezetimibe вҶ’ NPC1L1 block; Evolocumab/Alirocumab вҶ’ PCSK9 neutralization вҶ’ LDLR rescue; Inclisiran вҶ’ PCSK9 mRNA silencing (siRNA/RISC); Bempedoic acid вҶ’ ATP-citrate lyase (ACL) inhibition вҶ’ Acetyl-CoAвҶ“ вҶ’ HMG-CoAвҶ“; Fibrate/PPARОұ вҶ’ LPLвҶ‘/ApoC-IIIвҶ“/TGвҶ“/HDLвҶ‘; Niacin/GPR109A вҶ’ HSL inhibition вҶ’ FFAвҶ“ вҶ’ hepatic TGвҶ“ вҶ’ VLDLвҶ“; Omega-3 FA вҶ’ SREBP-1cвҶ“/DGAT2вҶ“ вҶ’ TGвҶ“; BAS вҶ’ BA sequestration вҶ’ CYP7A1вҶ‘ вҶ’ cholesterol diversion |
| Statin PK | Oral dose вҶ’ GI absorption; Hepatic first-pass (OATP1B1/1B3 uptake transporter); CYP3A4 (atorvastatin/lovastatin/simvastatin) / CYP2C9 (rosuvastatin/fluvastatin) metabolism; Biliary excretion; Active acid form vs lactone form; Myopathy risk (plasma CK, CYP3A4 DDI, hypothyroidism, age >75) |
| Atherosclerosis | Endothelial dysfunction (oxLDL вҶ’ eNOSвҶ“/ROSвҶ‘/ICAM-1/VCAM-1); Monocyte recruitment (MCP-1/CCR2); MonocyteвҶ’Macrophage differentiation; Foam cell formation (SR-A/CD36 oxLDL uptake); NLRP3/IL-1ОІ/IL-18 вҶ’ hsCRP; Vulnerable plaque (thin cap, lipid core, macrophage-rich); Stable plaque (thick cap, smooth muscle cells, collagen); Plaque regression (statin/PCSK9i вҶ’ cholesterol crystal dissolution) |
| Adipose Tissue | Catecholamine/cAMP/PKA вҶ’ HSL + ATGL вҶ’ TG lipolysis вҶ’ FFA + glycerol; Insulin вҶ’ HSL inhibition вҶ’ FFA suppression; Niacin/GPR109A вҶ’ anti-lipolytic; FFA flux to liver вҶ’ hepatic TG synthesis; Adipokines (adiponectin, leptin) |
| Hepatic TG Synthesis | Citrate вҶ’ Acetyl-CoA (ACL); GPAT вҶ’ LPA вҶ’ PA вҶ’ DAG (Lipin-1); DGAT1/2 вҶ’ TG; VLDL1 (TG-rich, insulin resistance) vs VLDL2 (CE-rich, normal); SREBP-1c/ChREBP/Insulin вҶ’ lipogenic gene upregulation; Glucagon вҶ’ opposing effects |
| Biomarkers | LDL-C В· HDL-C В· TG В· ApoB В· ApoA-I В· Non-HDL-C В· Lp(a) В· hsCRP В· PCSK9 plasma В· FFA В· VLDL-C В· sdLDL В· LDL particle number В· LDL particle size |
| Clinical Endpoints | MACE (MI В· stroke В· CVD death В· unstable angina В· revascularization); Plaque regression (REVERSAL/ASTEROID/GLAGOV IVUS trials); CIMT progression; Coronary Artery Calcium (CAC) score; ASCVD 10-year risk (PCE); LDL-C goal attainment; NNT for 5-year MACE prevention |

| Group | States | Description |

| Atorvastatin PK | AT_gut, AT_central, AT_peripheral | 2-cmt with GI absorption (ka=1.2/h); hepatic first-pass via OATP1B1; CL=78 L/h; V1=381 L; tВҪ=14h; F=12% (Lau 2006); HMGCR inhibition Imax model |
| Evolocumab PK | EVO_depot, EVO_central, EVO_peripheral | SC depot + 2-cmt; ka_SC=0.29/day; CL=0.27 L/day; V1=3.0 L; tВҪ=11.5 days (Gibbs 2017 Clin PK); PCSK9 target-mediated binding |
| Ezetimibe PK | EZE_intestinal, EZE_central | Intestinal compartment (NPC1L1 local exposure) + plasma; ka=2.1/h; CL=15 L/h; NPC1L1 inhibition IC50=1.2 nM (Altmann 2004) |
| Inclisiran PK | INC_depot | Single SC depot with mRNA silencing kinetics; dose on days 0, 90, 270, 450; effect tВҪвүҲ10 days from ORION-1 |
| Cholesterol Synthesis | HMGCoA_R, Mevalonate, Hep_Chol | HMG-CoA reductase activity (Emax inhibition by statin); mevalonate pool; hepatic free cholesterol (ACAT equilibrium with CE) |
| Lipoprotein Dynamics | VLDL, IDL, LDL_c, LDL_p, HDL | VLDL production rate (basal 0.32 mmol/L/day); IDL transit (tВҪ=2h); LDL central + peripheral; HDL turnover (tВҪ=5.5 days) |
| LDL Receptor | LDLR_surface, LDLR_internal | LDLR surface density (baseline ~50,000/cell); PCSK9-mediated lysosomal degradation; statin вҶ’ LDLR upregulation (2.5Г— via SREBP-2); LDL clearance proportional to LDLR Г— LDL |
| PCSK9 | PCSK9_liver, PCSK9_plasma, PCSK9_complex | Hepatic PCSK9 synthesis (SREBP-2 co-upregulated by statin +180%); plasma PCSK9 tВҪ=5 days; evolocumab complex (Kd=0.1 nM; tmax-binding 11 days); inclisiran silences PCSK9_liver mRNA |
| Intestinal Absorption | Chol_intestinal | NPC1L1-mediated uptake (baseline ~50% efficiency); ezetimibe reduces by 54% (Altmann 2004) |
| Bile Acid Pool | BA_pool | Enterohepatic circulation with CYP7A1 rate; BAS reduces BA recirculation вҶ’ CYP7A1вҶ‘ вҶ’ hepatic cholesterol diversion вҶ’ LDLRвҶ‘ |
| Atherosclerosis | Foam_cells, Plaque_burden | Foam cell accumulation driven by oxLDL Г— macrophage recruitment; plaque regression when LDL-C < 70 mg/dL sustained; calibrated to REVERSAL/ASTEROID IVUS data |

### Treatment Scenarios (6)

| # | Scenario | Dose Regimen | Primary Target | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|-------------|----------------|-------------------|
| 1 | No treatment | вҖ” | вҖ” | Framingham/UKPDS natural history; LDL-C 160 mg/dL baseline |
| 2 | Atorvastatin 40 mg QD | 40 mg oral once daily | HMG-CoA reductase | ASCOT-LLA (Sever 2003): вҲ’46% LDL-C; TNT (LaRosa 2005): intensive statin reduces MACE 22% |
| 3 | Atorvastatin 40 mg + Ezetimibe 10 mg | Dual oral daily | HMGCR + NPC1L1 | IMPROVE-IT (Cannon 2015, PMID 25405393): additional вҲ’15 mg/dL LDL-C; CV benefit additive |
| 4 | Atorvastatin 40 mg + Evolocumab 140 mg Q2W | Statin + SC biologic Q2W | HMGCR + PCSK9 | FOURIER (Sabatine 2017, PMID 28304224): вҲ’59% LDL-C from statin baseline; 15% MACE RRR |
| 5 | Triple: Statin + Ezetimibe + Evolocumab | Three-drug combination | HMGCR + NPC1L1 + PCSK9 | Combination guideline-recommended; LDL-C reduction >80%; FH management |
| 6 | Atorvastatin 40 mg + Inclisiran 284 mg SC | Statin + siRNA (day 0/90 then Q6M) | HMGCR + PCSK9 mRNA | ORION-1 (Ray 2017): вҲ’51% PCSK9; ORION-3 LTE (2022): sustained вҲ’45% LDL-C |

### Shiny Dashboard (6 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** вҖ” Sliders: age, sex, BMI, baseline LDL-C/HDL-C/TG, diabetes, smoking, blood pressure; Pooled Cohort Equations 10-year ASCVD risk calculator; ACC/AHA and ESC risk category display; LDL-C target based on risk (very high <55 mg/dL, high <70, intermediate <100); Lipid classification table; Risk factor radar chart
2. **Drug PK** вҖ” 14-drug selector (atorvastatin 10/20/40/80 mg, rosuvastatin 10/20/40 mg, evolocumab 140/420 mg, alirocumab 75/150 mg, inclisiran 284 mg, ezetimibe, bempedoic acid); Multi-dose accumulation PK curves over 26 weeks; Hepatic active metabolite panel; Half-life comparison bar chart; OATP1B1/CYP3A4 transporter note
3. **PD вҖ“ Lipid Biomarkers** вҖ” LDL-C, HDL-C, TG, ApoB, non-HDL-C time-courses (52 weeks); PCSK9 plasma dynamics (statin reactive upregulation вҶ‘180% vs PCSK9i suppression вҶ“85%); LDL receptor density trend; % change from baseline toggle; ACC/AHA/ESC target lines; Lp(a) note
4. **Clinical Endpoints** вҖ” CTT RRR model (22% relative risk reduction per 1 mmol/L LDL-C decrease); Cumulative 5-year MACE curves under each treatment; Atherosclerotic plaque regression/progression simulation (IVUS calibrated); NNT vs adherence chart; ARR and NNT summary table
5. **Scenario Comparison** вҖ” 6-arm simultaneous comparison; Grouped bar chart (LDL-C at wk 12/26/52); DataTable with conditional formatting (green = at goal, red = not at goal); Multi-dimension radar: LDL-C reduction / HDL-C change / TG change / MACE risk reduction / cost-effectiveness score
6. **Biomarker Dashboard** вҖ” PCSK9 genetic variant slider (GOF вҶ’ higher LDL; LOF вҶ’ lower baseline); Statin myopathy risk gauge (0вҖ“14 pt score: age, CK, hypothyroid, DDI, renal function, statin dose); CYP3A4 DDI checker (13 interacting drugs: amiodarone, diltiazem, amlodipine, cyclosporine, erythromycin, fluconazole, itraconazole, clarithromycin, HIV PIs, grapefruit); Guideline LDL-C target reference lines; Real-time NNT calculation

## Behcet's Disease (BD)

> Directory: [`behcet-disease/`](behcet-disease/)

**Mechanistic Map** (10 subgraph clusters, 130+ nodes, 200+ edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic & Environmental Factors | HLA-B51 (primary risk allele, OR 5-6Г—), ERAP1 (antigen trimming), IL-10 gene polymorphism (вҲ’1082G/A вҶ’ IL-10вҶ“), TNFSF4/OX40L, STAT4/IRF8 variants, CCR1/CCR3 haplotypes; Gut/oral microbiome dysbiosis; Streptococcus sanguinis molecular mimicry via HSP60/HSP70 cross-reactive epitopes; Silk Road geography |
| Innate Immunity | Neutrophil hyperactivation (HLA-B51 dependent priming); NETs (NETosis вҶ’ coagulation cascade activation + endothelial damage); ROS/MPO/elastase; Monocyte M1 polarization (TNF-Оұ/IL-1ОІ/IL-6/IL-12/IL-23); mDC (IL-12/IL-23 вҶ’ Th1/Th17 priming); NK cells (IFN-Оі early); Mast cell degranulation; NLRP3 inflammasome (ASC complex вҶ’ Caspase-1 вҶ’ IL-1ОІ/IL-18 cleavage); NOD1/2 signaling; ER stress/UPR; cGAS-STING pathway; PAMPs/DAMPs; GM-CSF myeloid survival |
| Adaptive Immunity | Th1 (IFN-Оі, TNF-Оұ dominant in BD); Th17 (IL-17A, IL-17F, IL-22, IL-21); Th22; CD8+ CTL (anti-HSP cross-reactive cytotoxicity at mucosal sites); Treg dysfunction (FoxP3+ suppression insufficient); Tfh вҶ’ IL-21 вҶ’ B cell germinal center; ОіОҙ T cells (IL-17A innate-like); NKT (CD1d restricted); ILC3 (IL-22/IL-17); B cell вҶ’ memory вҶ’ plasma вҶ’ AECA IgG (anti-endothelial cell antibodies) + IgA (mucosal) |
| Cytokine Network | TNF-Оұ (central mediator вҖ” monocyte/macrophage/Th1/neutrophil source); IL-1ОІ (NLRP3 product вҖ” drives oral ulcers + fever); IL-6 (pleiotropic; APR induction; Th17 polarization); IL-8/CXCL8 (neutrophil chemoattractant); IL-17A/F (Th17 + ОіОҙT + ILC3; epithelial/endothelial damage); IL-23 (Th17 maintenance вҖ” IL-12p40 shared with IL-12); IFN-Оі (Th1/CD8T/NK; M1 macrophage polarization); IL-10вҶ“ (anti-inflammatory deficit); TGF-ОІ/Treg; VEGF (angiogenesis/permeability); MCP-1/CCL5/CXCL10 (leukocyte chemokines); IL-18 (NK/Th1 amplifier); IL-33 (alarmin, ST2 вҶ’ mast cell); GM-CSF |
| Intracellular Signaling | NF-ОәB (p65/p50 вҖ” TNF-Оұ/IL-1ОІ/IL-17A вҶ’ ICAM-1/VCAM-1/E-selectin transcription); JAK/STAT cascade (IL-6вҶ’STAT3вҶ’RORОіtвҶ’Th17; IL-12вҶ’STAT4вҶ’T-betвҶ’Th1; IFN-ОівҶ’STAT1); MAPK/ERK + p38 MAPK (TNF-Оұ mRNA stabilization); PI3K/AKT вҶ’ mTORC1 (Th17 expansion); Notch signaling (T cell fate); PDE4 вҶ’ cAMP (apremilast target: cAMPвҶ‘ вҶ’ NF-ОәBвҶ“ вҶ’ TNF-ОұвҶ“/IL-17AвҶ“/IL-10вҶ‘); RORОіt (Th17 master TF); T-bet (Th1 master TF) |
| Vascular Pathology & Thrombosis | Endothelial cell activation (TNF-Оұ/IL-1ОІ/IL-17A/IFN-Оі вҶ’ TNFR1/R2/IL-1R/IL-17R signaling); ICAM-1/VCAM-1/E-selectin upregulation вҶ’ leukocyte adhesion; vWF exocytosis (Weibel-Palade bodies) вҶ’ platelet GPIbОұ binding; Tissue factor expression вҶ’ extrinsic coagulation pathway вҶ’ thrombin вҶ’ fibrin; eNOS uncoupling вҶ’ NOвҶ“ вҶ’ coagulationвҶ‘; PGI2вҶ“ вҶ’ anti-thrombotic protection lost; PAI-1вҶ‘ вҶ’ fibrinolysis inhibition; Platelet activation (PAR-1/4, GP IIb/IIIa); Venous thrombosis (Budd-Chiari / cerebral vein); Arterial thrombosis; Pulmonary/systemic aneurysm (vasculitis вҶ’ wall destruction); AECA IgG вҶ’ EC activation amplification |
| Organ Manifestations | Oral aphthous ulcers (>95%; IL-17A/TNF-Оұ/IL-1ОІ + CD8 CTL вҶ’ mucosal ulcerogenesis; IL-22 repair attempt); Genital ulcers (Th1/CD8/IL-17A); Anterior + posterior uveitis + retinal vasculitis вҶ’ optic atrophy/vision loss (25% blindness untreated); Pseudofolliculitis + erythema nodosum (skin Th17/TNF-Оұ/IL-1ОІ); Pathergy reaction (neutrophil hyperinflux to needlestick); GI ulcers (ileocecal, punched-out); Neuro-Behcet (parenchymal BD or cerebral vein thrombosis); Non-destructive polyarthritis; Epididymo-orchitis; Budd-Chiari syndrome; Pulmonary infarction |
| Drug Pharmacokinetics | Colchicine: gut depot вҶ’ central (F=44%, CL=17 L/h, Vd=588 L=21 L/kg, tВҪ=27h); Prednisolone: 2-CMT oral (F=80%, CL=8.4 L/h, V1=22 L); Adalimumab: 2-CMT SC (F=64%, CL=0.012 L/h, V1=2.8 L, tВҪ~2 wk, Q2W dosing); Apremilast: 1-CMT oral (F=73%, CL=10 L/h, V1=87 L, tВҪ=9h, BID dosing); Canakinumab: 2-CMT SC (F=66%, CL=0.007 L/h, V1=3.0 L, tВҪ~26 d, Q8W dosing); Cyclophosphamide: IV active alkylating form; Thalidomide: oral (F=67%, tВҪ=5-7h) |
| Drug PD Mechanisms | Colchicine: tubulin polymerizationвҶ“ вҶ’ neutrophil migrationвҶ“ + NLRP3 assembly inhibition вҶ’ IL-1ОІвҶ“; Prednisolone: GRВ·NF-ОәB/AP-1 co-repression вҶ’ broad cytokine mRNAвҶ“; Azathioprine: 6-TG вҶ’ DNA damage вҶ’ T/B cell proliferationвҶ“; Adalimumab: mTNF/sTNF neutralization + Treg inductionвҶ‘; Apremilast: PDE4 inhibition вҶ’ cAMPвҶ‘ вҶ’ PKA вҶ’ NF-ОәB phosphorylationвҶ“ вҶ’ TNF-ОұвҶ“/IL-17AвҶ“/IL-10вҶ‘; Canakinumab: high-affinity IL-1ОІ neutralization (Kd~0.3 pM) вҶ’ NLRP3 pathway blockade; Cyclophosphamide: DNA alkylation вҶ’ B/T/plasma cell depletion; Thalidomide: TNF-Оұ mRNA destabilization + IMiD immunomodulation вҶ’ Th1вҶ“ |
| Clinical Endpoints & Biomarkers | BDCAF score (0-12: oral ulcers/genital/ocular/skin/arthritis/neuro/vascular, remission <3); Oral ulcer frequency (per month); Visual acuity (LogMAR/Snellen); Ocular inflammation score; Serum TNF-Оұ, IL-1ОІ, IL-6, IL-17A (normalized disease activity); ESR/CRP (APR driven by IL-6); SAA; Neutrophil:lymphocyte ratio; Quality of life (SF-36/BDQ); Relapse rate (flares/year); Time to remission; Vascular event rate (thrombosis/aneurysm/Budd-Chiari) |

### ODE Compartments (22 states)

| Group | States | Description |
|-------|--------|-------------|
| Colchicine PK | AGUT_COL, ACOL, ACOL_T | Gut depot вҶ’ 2-CMT; ka=1.2/h; F=44%; CL=17 L/h; V1=28 L; V2=5500 L (Vd=21 L/kg); Q=30 L/h; tВҪвүҲ27h; NLRP3 inhibition IC50=1.5 ng/mL; Neutrophil inhibition IC50=0.8 ng/mL |
| Prednisolone PK | APRED, APRED_T | 2-CMT oral; ka=1.0/h; F=80%; CL=8.4 L/h; V1=22 L; V2=50 L; tВҪвүҲ3.5h; NF-ОәB inhibition EC50=50 ng/mL; Emax=0.80 |
| Adalimumab PK | AADA, AADA_P | SC 2-CMT; F=64%; CL=0.012 L/h; V1=2.8 L; V2=3.4 L; Q=0.003 L/h; tВҪ~14 days; TNF-Оұ neutralization EC50=1500 ng/mL; Emax=0.90 |
| Apremilast PK | AAPR | 1-CMT oral; ka=0.58/h; F=73%; CL=10 L/h; V1=87 L; tВҪвүҲ9h; PDE4вҶ’cAMPвҶ’TNF-ОұвҶ“ EC50=200 ng/mL; IL-17AвҶ“ EC50=300 ng/mL |
| Canakinumab PK | ACAN, ACAN_P | SC 2-CMT; F=66%; CL=0.007 L/h; V1=3.0 L; V2=3.2 L; tВҪвүҲ26 days; IL-1ОІ neutralization EC50=800 ng/mL; Emax=0.92 |
| Immune Cells | NEU, TH1, TH17, TREG | Neutrophil activation (TNFA/IL17A driven; colchicine suppressed); Th1 cells (TNF-Оұ amplification; pred suppressed); Th17 cells (IL-6/TREG ratio dependent; apremilast/pred suppressed); Treg (TGFB driven, TNFA opposed) |
| Cytokines | TNFA, IL1B, IL6C, IL17A | TNF-Оұ (Th1+NEU driven; adalimumab/pred/apremilast target); IL-1ОІ (NLRP3/NEU driven; colchicine/canakinumab target); IL-6 (IL-1B/TNFA synergy; pred target); IL-17A (Th17+gdT driven; apremilast target) |
| Organ Activity | EA, OUL, OCI, BDCAF | Endothelial activation (TNFA/IL1B/IL17A driven; resolved by anti-TNF); Oral ulcer index (cytokine + NEU driven; 4-drug sensitivity); Ocular inflammation (EA driven; anti-TNF/steroid target); BDCAF composite score (OUL+OCI+EA+cytokines weighted) |

### Treatment Scenarios (8)

| # | Scenario | Dose Regimen | Primary Target | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|-------------|----------------|-------------------|
| 1 | Untreated | вҖ” | вҖ” | Natural disease course (HLA-B51+ severe BD) |
| 2 | Colchicine monotherapy | 0.5 mg BID oral | Tubulin / NLRP3 | Yurdakul et al. Arthritis Rheum 2001 (PMID 11710724): mucocutaneous flare reduction |
| 3 | Prednisolone monotherapy | 40 mg/day oral | NF-ОәB (broad cytokines) | Standard of care for acute flares; NF-ОәB/AP-1 co-repression |
| 4 | Adalimumab (anti-TNF) | SC 40 mg Q2W | TNF-Оұ (mTNF + sTNF) | Saadoun et al. ADABT trial (PMID 21821622): uveitis remission; Hatemi 2018 EULAR update |
| 5 | Apremilast (PDE4i) | 30 mg BID oral | PDE4 вҶ’ cAMP вҶ’ TNF-Оұ/IL-17AвҶ“ | Hatemi et al. NEJM 2015 (PMID 25853758) + NEJM 2019 (PMID 31722153): oral ulcer NNT=2.4 |
| 6 | Canakinumab (anti-IL-1ОІ) | SC 150 mg Q8W | IL-1ОІ (NLRP3 product) | Vitale et al. Dermatology 2014 (PMID 24577264): refractory oral/genital ulcers |
| 7 | Colchicine + Prednisolone | Combination | NLRP3 + NF-ОәB | Standard combination for moderate BD with mucocutaneous + systemic features |
| 8 | Adalimumab + Apremilast | Combination (refractory) | TNF-Оұ + PDE4 | Combination for refractory multi-organ BD; EULAR 2018 refractory pathway |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** вҖ” Disease demographics (Silk Road geography, HLA-B51 status); ISG diagnostic criteria checklist; organ involvement selector; BDCAF scale reference table with scoring rubric; pathomechanism HTML summary (innate/adaptive/vascular cascade)
2. **Drug PK** вҖ” 5-drug selector (colchicine/prednisolone/adalimumab/apremilast/canakinumab); dose/frequency/duration inputs; concentration-time profile (plotly); PK reference table (F%/tВҪ/Vd/CL/Cmax); summary statistics (Cmax/Cmin/Cavg/AUC)
3. **Cytokine & Immune Dynamics** вҖ” Single-treatment simulation; cytokine panel (TNF-Оұ/IL-1ОІ/IL-6/IL-17A time-course); immune cell dynamics (NEU/Th1/Th17/Treg); Th17/Treg balance ribbon plot (key pathological feature of BD)
4. **Clinical Endpoints** вҖ” BDCAF composite score; oral ulcer activity; ocular inflammation; endothelial activation (vascular risk proxy); Day-90 endpoint summary datatable; remission threshold line (BDCAF < 3)
5. **Scenario Comparison** вҖ” 8-arm simultaneous comparison; BDCAF/oral/ocular plots; color-coded by treatment type; Day-90 summary datatable with conditional formatting (green = remission)
6. **Biomarker & HLA-B51 Stratification** вҖ” HLA-B51+ vs HLA-B51вҲ’ response comparison under selected therapy; serum cytokine biomarker dynamics; time-to-remission bar chart by genotype; clinical reference ranges table (TNF-Оұ/IL-1ОІ/IL-6/IL-17A pg/mL normal vs mild/active/severe BD)
7. **Dose Optimization** вҖ” Drug-specific dose-response analysis (4 drugs); dose-range slider; BDCAF/OUL/OCI at Day-90 curves; optimal dose summary table with remission flag

| HSC Activation | TGF-ОІ1/Smad2/3 (key fibrogenic axis), PDGF-BB, CTGF/CCN2, Оұ-SMA, Wnt/ОІ-catenin, Hedgehog/Shh, YAP/TAZ mechanotransduction, LOXL2, Smad7 negative feedback, HSC senescence (p21/p53) |

| Portal Hypertension | HVPG (mmHg), intrahepatic resistance, eNOS/NO deficit, endothelin-1, RhoA/ROCK, VEGF/angiogenesis, portosystemic collaterals, splenic congestion, esophageal/gastric varices, variceal hemorrhage, hyperdynamic circulation, splanchnic vasodilation |
| Hepatic Synthetic Function | Albumin synthesis, clotting factors (II/V/VII/IX/X), INR/PT, bilirubin conjugation, ammonia detoxification (urea cycle/glutamine), CYP450 drug metabolism, Child-Pugh score (A/B/C), MELD score (6вҖ“40), MELD-Na |
| Ascites & Fluid | Portal pressureвҖ“Starling forces, hepatic lymph formation, RAAS (reninвҶ’AngIIвҶ’Aldosterone), SNS, ADH/AVP, Na+/water retention, hyponatremia, low oncotic pressure |
| Renal Complications | GFR decline (eGFR), renal vasoconstriction, HRS type 1/2, ATN, oliguria, creatinine/BUN rise |
| Hepatic Encephalopathy | Serum ammonia, gut flora/bacterial translocation, portosystemic bypass, BBB permeability, astrocyte swelling, GABA/benzodiazepine enhancement, neuroinflammation, HE grade (West Haven 0вҖ“IV), covert HE |
| Systemic Complications | HPS, portopulmonary HTN, HCC, ACLF, coagulopathy/thrombocytopenia, sarcopenia/malnutrition, cirrhotic cardiomyopathy, QTc prolongation, adrenal insufficiency, portal vein thrombosis, SIRS/sepsis |
| NSBB PK/PD | Propranolol 2-compartment (F=25%, CL=30 L/h), ОІ1/ОІ2-blockade вҶ’ HRвҶ“/HVPGвҶ“; Carvedilol Оұ1 component |
| Diuretic PK/PD | Spironolactone 1-compartment (F=90%, active canrenone), MR blockade вҶ’ Na excretionвҶ‘; Furosemide Na-K-2Cl blockade вҶ’ ascites mobilization |
| Vasoconstrictor PK/PD | Terlipressin effect-compartment (KE0=0.4/h), V1-receptor вҶ’ splanchnic vasoconstriction вҶ’ HVPGвҶ“; Somatostatin/octreotide infusion (SSTR2) |
| Rifaximin PK/PD | Gut-lumen restricted (F<0.4%), microbiome modulation вҶ’ gut NH3вҶ“ вҶ’ serum NH3вҶ“ вҶ’ HE prevention; Lactulose colonic pHвҶ“ mechanism |
| Antifibrotic Therapy | FXR agonists (OCA/Tropifexor вҶ’ SHP вҶ’ TGF-ОІвҶ“); CCR2/CCR5 inhibitor (Cenicriviroc вҶ’ monocyteвҶ“); LOXL2 inhibitor; TGF-ОІ inhibitor; ASK1 inhibitor (Selonsertib); GLP-1RA (Semaglutide); THRОІ agonist (Resmetirom); VAP-1 inhibitor |
| Clinical Endpoints | Decompensation events (ascites/VB/HE/SBP), transplant listing (MELDвүҘ15), 6-month/1-year survival, 30-day readmission, QoL (SF-36/CLDQ), post-transplant fibrosis recurrence |

### Adult-Onset Still's Disease (AOSD)

> Directory: [`adult-onset-stills-disease/`](adult-onset-stills-disease/)

**Mechanistic Map** (13 subgraph clusters, 154 named nodes, 200+ edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Innate Immune Triggers | PAMP/DAMP, TLR2/4/7/9, RAGE receptor, S100A8/A9/A12 (calprotectin), HMGB1, MyD88/TRIF adapters, NF-ОәB, AP-1, IRF3/7, pro-IL-1ОІ/IL-18 priming |
| NLRP3 Inflammasome | NLRP3 sensor, ASC adaptor, Caspase-1 effector, Signal 1 (NF-ОәB priming) + Signal 2 (ATP/crystals/ROS/KвҒә-efflux activation), NEK7, Gasdermin D/pyroptosis, mature IL-1ОІвҳ… + IL-18вҳ… cleavage |
| Macrophage/Monocyte Biology | Classical/non-classical monocytes, M1/M2 polarization, AOSD-phenotype activated macrophage, ferritin secretion (H-chain dominant), hemophagocyte differentiation, M-CSF/GM-CSF, pDC/mDC |
| Cytokine Network | IL-1ОІвҳ…, IL-6вҳ…, IL-18вҳ…, IFN-Оівҳ…, TNF-Оұ, IL-12, IL-23, IL-17A, IL-15, IL-10 (anti-inflam), IL-18BP (natural inhibitor), CXCL8/MCP-1/CXCL9/CXCL10 chemokines |
| JAK-STAT Signaling | IL-6RОұ/gp130 complex, sIL-6R trans-signaling, JAK1/2/TYK2/JAK3, STAT1/3/4/5, SOCS1/3 negative feedback, PIAS, IL-1R1/IL-1RAcP, IRAK4/TRAF6 вҶ’ NF-ОәB, p38 MAPK, PI3K/AKT/mTOR |
| Adaptive Immunity | NaГҜve Th0 вҶ’ Th1 (IL-12/IL-18вҶ’IFN-Оі) / Th17 (IL-6/TGF-ОІвҶ’IL-17A) / Treg (TGF-ОІ/IL-10) / CD8+CTL; NK cell activation (IL-15/IL-18вҶ’IFN-Оі); B cells; APC/DC, MHC-II, CD28/CTLA-4 co-stimulation |
| Acute Phase Response | Hepatocyte APP induction (IL-6/IL-1ОІ/TNF-Оұ), CRPвҳ…, SAA, fibrinogen, albuminвҶ“, glycosylated ferritin (<20% = AOSD-specific), hepcidin, LDH, ALT/AST |
| Hyperferritinemia | Serum ferritinвҳ… (5,000вҶ’10,000вҶ’>50,000 ng/mL), ferritin H-chain as immunomodulator, macrophage ferritin secretion vs hepatic synthesis, ferritin >10,000 ng/mL MAS threshold |
| Clinical Manifestations | Quotidian fever >39В°Cвҳ… (PGE2-mediated), salmon-coloured evanescent rashвҳ…, polyarthritis (DAS28/Pouchot), lymphadenopathy, hepatosplenomegaly, serositis (pleuritis/pericarditis), leukocytosis/neutrophilia; AOSD activity score (Pouchot 0-12 / Rau scoring) |
| MAS (Macrophage Activation Syndrome) | IFN-Оівҳ… MAS driver, NK/CTL dysfunction (CD107aвҶ“, perforinвҶ“), PRF1/STX11/XLP genetic variants, cytokine storm (IL-1ОІ/IL-6/IL-18/IFN-Оі/TNF-Оұ), hemophagocytosis (bone marrow), bicytopenia, coagulopathy/DIC, multi-organ failure, CXCL9 biomarker, HScore (2016 Ravelli criteria) |
| NSAIDs & Corticosteroids | Naproxen/Ibuprofen вҶ’ COX-1/2 inhibition вҶ’ PGE2вҶ“; Prednisolone/Dexamethasone вҶ’ GR-Оұ вҶ’ GILZ/MKP-1 transactivation вҶ’ NF-ОәB/AP-1 suppression вҶ’ IL-1ОІ/IL-6/TNF-ОұвҶ“; HPA axis feedback |
| Biologics вҖ” Anti-IL-1/IL-6 | Anakinra (IL-1Ra, SC QD: ka=2/d, kel=3/d, EC50=0.5 Ојg/mL, competitive IL-1R1 blockade) + Canakinumab (anti-IL-1ОІ mAb, 4mg/kg q4w: tВҪ=26d, EC50=0.1 Ојg/mL) + Rilonacept (IL-1 trap) + Tocilizumab (anti-IL-6RОұ: 8mg/kg q2w, tВҪ=11d, mIL-6R+sIL-6R dual blockade, EC50=1 Ојg/mL) + Sarilumab + Siltuximab |
| JAK Inhibitors | Tofacitinib (JAK1/3: 5mg BID, Vd=87L, tВҪ=3h; STAT3/STAT5вҶ“); Baricitinib (JAK1/2); Ruxolitinib (MAS rescue: IFN-Оі signalingвҶ“); Upadacitinib (selective JAK1); Cyclosporine A (calcineurin-NFAT вҶ’ IFN-Оі/NKвҶ“); Etoposide (topoisomerase II вҶ’ macrophage/hemophagocyteвҶ“) |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![AOSD QSP Map](adult-onset-stills-disease/aosd_qsp_model.png)](adult-onset-stills-disease/aosd_qsp_model.svg)

**mrgsolve ODE Model (20 compartments, 21 ODEs):**

| Compartment Group | States | Key Dynamics |
|-------------------|--------|--------------|
| Anakinra PK | ANAP (depot SC), ANAC (central) | ka=2/d, CL=21 L/d, Vd=7L; EC50=0.5 Ојg/mL IL-1R competitive inhibition |
| Canakinumab PK | CANAP (periph), CANAC (central) | tВҪ=26d, Vd=3.8 L/kg; EC50=0.1 Ојg/mL; IL-1ОІ neutralization (freeвҶ’bound) |
| Tocilizumab PK | TCZP (periph), TCZC (central) | tВҪ=11d, Vd=3.7 L/kg; EC50=1 Ојg/mL; mIL-6R + sIL-6R dual blockade |
| Corticosteroid PK | CORT | kel=1.5/d; GR transactivation вҶ’ NF-ОәB/AP-1 suppression |
| Tofacitinib PK | TOFP (depot), TOFC (central) | kel=4/d, Vd=87L; JAK1/3 вҶ’ STAT3/STAT5вҶ“ |
| Cytokines | IL1B, IL6, IL18, IFNG, TNFA | ProductionвҖ“degradation ODEs with positive cross-stimulation, drug inhibition (Hill equations, Imax=0.9) |
| Macrophage/NK | MACACT, NK_ACT | MACACT driven by cytokine storm; NK_ACT inversely correlated with MAS |
| Biomarkers | FERT, CRP | FERT: dual hepatic+macrophage synthesis (IL-6/IL-18 driven); CRP: hepatic IL-6 response |
| Composite Scores | AOSD_ACT, MAS_RISK | Pouchot-inspired (0-20); MAS logistic probability (0-1: IL-18, ferritin, NK_ACT) |

**6 Treatment Scenarios:**

| Scenario | Regimen | Key Clinical Trial Reference |
|----------|---------|------------------------------|
| 1 Untreated | Natural history (severity-dependent progression) | вҖ” |
| 2 Corticosteroids | Prednisolone 0.5 mg/kg/day PO | Standard of care; Pouchot 1991 |
| 3 Anakinra | 100 mg SC QD (IL-1Ra) | CONSIDER-AOSD (Feist 2018); Nordstrom 2012 RCT |
| 4 Canakinumab | 4 mg/kg q4w IV (anti-IL-1ОІ) | Ruperto 2012 (PMID 23252526); Quartuccio 2020 |
| 5 Tocilizumab | 8 mg/kg q2w IV (anti-IL-6R) | Matsumoto 2018 case series; Ortiz-Sanjuan 2015 |
| 6 Tofacitinib | 5 mg BID PO (JAK1/3i) | Hu 2019; Kedor 2021 (refractory AOSD) |
